// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        $(document).ready(function() {
            $('[id="Consignee Name Address"]').on('keydown', $('[id="Consignee Name Address"]').find("input[name='code']"), function(e) { 
                var keyCode = e.keyCode || e.which; 

                if (keyCode == 9) { 
                    e.preventDefault(); 
                    // look up the address on tab
                    $('[caption="Consignee Name Address"]').find('button[ng-click="search(nameaddress)"]').click();
                } 
            });
        });
    }

// Source: Alight Solutions (ALISOL)_DirectToMobileCBR_2434.cs
// function IsEventAttached($element, elementEvent, elementEventHandler) // returns boolean indicating whether a matching event handler is attached
function IsEventAttached($element, elementEvent, elementEventHandler)
	{				
		var result = false;
		
		var elementEvents = $._data($element.get(0), "events");
		
		if (elementEvents != undefined)
		{
			elementEventHandler = elementEventHandler.toString();
			result = (elementEvents && elementEvents[elementEvent]?.some(ev => ev.handler.toString() === elementEventHandler))
		}
		
		return result;
	}

        $saveShipmentProfileModal = angular.element('#saveShipmentProfileModal');
        $saveShipmentProfileModal.on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShippingProfile"]').focus();
            });
        $deleteShipmentProfileModal = angular.element('#deleteShipmentProfileModal');
        $processEODModal = angular.element('#processEODModal');
        
        vm.showSaveShippingProfileModal = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            $saveShipmentProfileModal.modal('show');
            }

        vm.showDeleteShippingProfileModal = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            $deleteShipmentProfileModal.modal('show');
            }
        
        vm.saveShippingProfile = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            var selsvc = this.selectedServices[0].Symbol;
            shipmentRequest.Action = 'S';
            shipmentRequest.ShippingProfileName = vm.currentShippingProfile;
            shipmentRequest.SelService = selsvc;
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest) };
            client.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(
                function(ret) {
                var curprofilelist = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));
                vm.shippingProfiles = curprofilelist;
                })
            
            $saveShipmentProfileModal.modal('hide');
            }

        vm.deleteShippingProfile = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            shipmentRequest.Action = 'D';
            shipmentRequest.ShippingProfileName = vm.currentShippingProfile;
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest) };
            client.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(
                function(ret) {
                var curprofilelist = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));
                vm.shippingProfiles = curprofilelist;
                })
            
            $deleteShipmentProfileModal.modal('hide');
            }

        vm.shippingProfileChange = function (shipmentRequest)
            {
            var tmpShippingProfile = vm.shippingProfiles.find(({ ShippingProfileName }) => ShippingProfileName === this.currentShippingProfile);
            var newShippingProfile = structuredClone(tmpShippingProfile);    
            if( newShippingProfile !== null && newShippingProfile !== undefined) {
                var selsvc = newShippingProfile.SelService;
                var myservice = {Symbol: selsvc };
                if( newShippingProfile.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery === true) {
                    newShippingProfile.Packages[0].SelectedProactiveRecoveryInstructions = [4096,2048,32];                    
                }

                var today = new Date();
                var curdate = {Year: today.getFullYear(), Month: today.getMonth() + 1, Day: today.getDate()};
                newShippingProfile.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = curdate;
                this.currentShipment = newShippingProfile;
                this.selectedServices[0] = myservice;
                }
            }

        vm.CreateReturnLabelFromPrevious = function ()
            {
            vm.currentShipment = structuredClone(vm.lastShipmentRequest);
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDelivery = true;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ProactiveRecovery = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DirectDelivery = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Proof = false;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ProofRequireSignature = false; 
            vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.2DA" };
            if (!vm.selectedServices) {
                vm.selectedServices = [];
            }
            vm.selectedServices.push(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service);
            };

        vm.showProcessEODModal = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            $processEODModal.modal('show');
            }

        vm.ProcessEOD = function(shipmentRequest)
            {
            shipmentRequest.Action = 'EOD';
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest) };
            client.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(
                function(ret) {
                var eodresult = ret.Data;
                $processEODModal.modal('hide');                
                })
            }

        }
        
    }

    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {

// this.Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {
        
        //debugger;
        
        this.vm.useCustomGoodsTab = false;
        this.vm.customAddCommodity = customAddCommodity;
        this.vm.importerOfRecordSameAsConsignee = importerOfRecordSameAsConsignee;
        this.vm.addSameAsConsigneeCheckbox = addSameAsConsigneeCheckbox;
        this.vm.addSameAsConsigneeCheckbox();
                
        this.vm.delegateTravelerLabel = delegateTravelerLabel;
        
        this.vm.delegateTabSelected = delegateTabSelected;
        
        this.vm.anotherTabSelected = anotherTabSelected;
        
        var includeIndex = this.vm.profile.CommercialInvoiceMethods.findIndex(function(item) { return item.Name == 'Included'})
        this.vm.profile.CommercialInvoiceMethods.splice(includeIndex, 1);

        if (this.vm.shipping.IsTraveler) {
            client.shipping.notificationGeneralVisibilityBtn.hide();
            client.shipping.returnDeliveryNotificationBtn.hide();
        }

        function delegateTravelerLabel(shipmentRequest) {

            //vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = vm.selectedServices[0];            
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest) };
            
            debugger;
            
            var result = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).responseJSON;
            var travelerlabelresp = JSON.parse(atob(result.Data));
            var travelerlabelpdf64 = travelerlabelresp.DocumentResponses[0].PdfData[0];
            
            // This works but only when the user switches to the new tab and refereshes page
            var dataURI = "data:application/pdf;base64," + travelerlabelpdf64;
            window.open(dataURI, '_blank');

            // This also fails
            //let pdfWindow = window.open("")
            //setTimeout(() => pdfWindow.document.title = 'Delegate Label',50);
            //const iframe = pdfWindow.document.createElement('iframe');
            //iframe.width = '100%';
            //iframe.height = '100%';
            //iframe.title = 'PDF Viewer';  
            //iframe.src = 'data:application/pdf;base64, ' + encodeURI(travelerlabelpdf64);
            //pdfWindow.document.body.appendChild(iframe);
            
            
            // Original code that fails on the document.write call
            //let pdfWindow = window.open("")
            //setTimeout(() => pdfWindow.document.title = 'Delegate Label',50);
            //pdfWindow.document.write(
            //    "<iframe width='100%' height='100%' src='data:application/pdf;base64, " +
            //    encodeURI(travelerlabelpdf64) + "'></iframe>"
            //    )            

            alert("Delegate Label Created");
        }

        function delegateTabSelected() {
            $('#btnSave').hide();
            $('#btnPrintTravelerLabel').show();
        }
        
        function anotherTabSelected() {
            $('#btnSave').show();
            $('#btnPrintTravelerLabel').hide();
        }
        
        $('body').on('click', 'input[ng-click="vm.selectLicensePlate(licensePlate)"]', this.vm, function(e) {
            client.shipping.changeStateProvince('');
            var stateProvince = e.data.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince;
            $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] input[name="stateProvince"]').val(stateProvince);
        });        
        
        $('body').on('click', client.shipping.intl.importerOfRecordClearSelector, function(e) {
            client.shipping.intl.$iorSameAsConsignee.get(0).checked = false;
        });

        $('body').on('change', client.shipping.consignee.countrySelector, this.vm, function(e) {
            client.shipping.changeStateProvince(e.data.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country);
        });

        $('body').on('change', client.shipping.consignee.stateProvinceSelector, this.vm, function(e) {
            e.data.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince = e.target.value;
            
        });

        $('body').on('click', 'button:contains("'+ this.vm.addCommodityContentsButtonTitle +'")', this.vm, function(e) {
            var interval = setInterval(function(vm) {
                var commodityModalTitle = $('.modal-content h4:contains("Add/Edit Commodity")');
                if (commodityModalTitle.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    var commodityModal = commodityModalTitle.closest('div.modal-dialog');
                    commodityModal.removeClass('modal-lg').addClass('modal-md');
                    var tabPanes = commodityModal.find('.tab-content:first > div.tab-pane');
                    hideTabs(commodityModal);
                    hideGeneralElement(tabPanes.eq(0), vm);
                }
            }, 10, e.data)

            function hideTabs(commodityModal) {
                var hideIndex = ['1','2','3','4','5','6','7'];
                Array.from(commodityModal.find('li.uib-tab.nav-item')).forEach(function(item) {
                    if (hideIndex.indexOf(item.getAttribute('index')) > -1) $(item).hide();
                });
            }

            function hideGeneralElement(generalPane, vm) {
                var paneRow = generalPane.find('div.row');
                // var originCountry = paneRow.find('div[caption="Origin Country"]').parent().append('<div class="row col-md-12 col-lg-12 ng-scope" \>')
                // var coo = paneRow.find('div[caption="Origin Country"]').closest('div.row');
                // coo.find('div[caption="' + vm.translations.Common.UnitWeight + '"]').hide();
                
                var originCountry = $(paneRow.find('div[caption="Origin Country"]').closest('div.row')[0].outerHTML);
                originCountry.find('div[caption="' + vm.translations.Common.OriginCountry + '"]').removeClass('col-md-6').addClass('col-md-12')
                originCountry.find('div[caption="' + vm.translations.Common.UnitWeight + '"]').hide();
                Array.from(paneRow.find('div')).forEach(function(item) {
                    if (item.classList.contains('col-md-6')) {
                        $(item).removeClass('col-md-6').addClass('col-md-12');
                    }
                })
                
                // coo = coo[0].outerHTML;

                var hideGeneralElement = [
                    vm.translations.Common.CommodityCondition,
                    vm.translations.Common.ApprovedCommunityMemberNumber,
                    vm.translations.Common.OriginCountry,
                    vm.translations.Common.ManufacturerIDCode,
                    vm.translations.Common.OriginDescription
                ];

                hideGeneralElement.forEach(function(item) {
                    var generalElement = paneRow.find('div[caption="' + item + '"]');
                    generalElement.hide(); //remove() causes id error
                });
                
                // $(coo).insertBefore(paneRow[5])
                // originCountry.insertBefore(paneRow[5])
                originCountry.insertBefore(paneRow[5]);
            }
        });

        function importerOfRecordSameAsConsignee(checked) {
            if (checked) {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].ImporterOfRecord = {
                    Company: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company,
                    Contact: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Contact,
                    Address1: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1,
                    Address2: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address2,
                    Address3: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address3,
                    City: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.City,
                    StateProvince: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.StateProvince,
                    PostalCode: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.PostalCode,
                    Country: this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country
                }
            } else {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].ImporterOfRecord = {}
            }
        }

        function addSameAsConsigneeCheckbox () {
            var interval = setInterval(function(vm) {
                var $target = $(client.shipping.intl.importerOfRecordBtnSelector);
                if ($target.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval)
                    client.shipping.intl.$iorSameAsConsignee = $('<input type="checkbox">');
                    client.shipping.intl.$iorSameAsConsignee.click(function(e) { vm.importerOfRecordSameAsConsignee(e.target.checked) });
                    $target.before(client.shipping.intl.$iorSameAsConsignee, '<label style="padding-left: 6px;">Same As Consignee</label>');
                }
            }, 10, this)
        }       
    }

// this.PostRate(shipmentRequest, rateResults) // returns void
    this.PostRate = function (shipmentRequest, rateResults) {
        debugger;
        modifiedRateResults();
        if (this.vm.shipping.IsMailroom) {
            rateResults[0].customRateResults = customRateResults;
        }

        function modifiedRateResults() {
            for(var i = 0; i< rateResults.length; i++) {
                var rateService = rateResults[i].PackageDefaults.Service;
                rateService.Name = rateService.Name.replace('(CSAdapter)', '').trim();
                rateResults[i].SortIndex = rateService.Symbol == shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol ? 0 : i + 1;
            }
        } 

        function customRateResults(vm) {
            var selectService = selectSortIndex();
            vm.selectService = [ selectService ];
            vm.selectedRow = selectService.Symbol;

            vm.customOnSelectService = customOnSelectService;

            function selectSortIndex () {
                for(var index in rateResults) {
                    if (rateResults[index].SortIndex === 0) {
                        return rateResults[index].PackageDefaults.Service;
                    }
                }
            }

            function customOnSelectService(service, serviceType) {
                if (this.profile.ProfileSetting.ServiceSelectionMode === this.serviceSelectionMode.ShipByService) {
                    this.onSelectService(service, serviceType)
                } else {
                    this.selectService = [ service ];
                    this.selectedRow = service.Symbol;
                    if (!this.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableJustificationMessage) {
                        this.selectedRow = service.Symbol;
                        if (serviceType === "ApplicableService" && selectSortIndex() !== service)
                            this.justify = true;
                        else if (serviceType === "NotApplicableService")
                            this.justify = true;
                        else
                            this.justify = false;
                    } else this.justify = false;
                }
            }
        }
    }

// this.PreSearchHistory(searchCriteria) // returns void
    this.PreSearchHistory = function (searchCriteria) {
        this.vm.shipping ??= client.setMailroomOrTraveler(this.vm.profile.Name);
        if (this.vm.shipping.IsTraveler) searchCriteria.WhereClauses.push({ FieldName: 'MiscReference20', FieldValue: client.userName, Operator: 5 });
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {

        this.vm.shipping ??= client.setMailroomOrTraveler(this.vm.profile.Name);
        if (this.vm.shipping.IsMailroom) client.shipping.loadValue.focus();        
        client.shipping.consignee.updateStateProvince(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults?.Consignee?.Country);
        
        if (this.vm.shipping.IsTraveler) {
            this.vm.disableShipMode = true;
            this.vm.createLicensePlateButtonCaption = 'Get Rate'
            shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = client.userName;
        } 
        this.vm.validateClientMatter = this.validateClientMatter;
        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = client.userName;        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = client.userName;        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = client.userName;  
        // shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference = '040614-548313';
    }

// this.PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        client.shipping.changeStateProvince('');
    }

// this.validateClientMatter() // returns void
    this.validateClientMatter = function() {

        if( theVM.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference === null) {
            alert('Client Matter field is required. Please enter a valid client matter number!');
            setFocus('input[name="ShipperReference_txt"]');            
            return;
        }
        
        var cmFound = false;
        var cm = theVM.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        var cmValidationList = theVM.fieldOptions.ShipperReference.FieldOptionValidations;
        for(var i = 0; i < cmValidationList.length; i++) {
            var cmValidationItem = cmValidationList[i];
            if( cmValidationItem.Value == cm) {
                cmFound = true;
                break;
            }
        }
        if( cmFound )
            theVM.saveLicensePlate();
        else {
            alert("Client Matter field is invalid. Please enter a valid client matter number!");
            setFocus('input[name="ShipperReference_txt"]');                        
        }
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;
        shipmentRequest.itemSkuTextChanged = this.handleItemSkuTextChanged;
        shipmentRequest.viewPackedBoxListModal = this.handleViewPackedBoxListModal;
        shipmentRequest.AlertTitle = "";
        shipmentRequest.AlertMessage = "";
        shipmentRequest.orderItemListPB = "";
        angular.element('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').focus();
    };

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;
        shipmentRequest.itemSkuTextChanged = this.handleItemSkuTextChanged;
        shipmentRequest.viewPackedBoxListModal = this.handleViewPackedBoxListModal;       
        if( shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company == "Order not found") {
            ShowAlert("Order Error", "Order not found");
            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').focus();    	
        } else {
            var json = jQuery.parseJSON(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData1);
    	    orderItemList = json;
    	    shipmentRequest.orderItemListPB = json;
    	    //vm.getWeight();
            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	
        }
    };

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;

	    // Verify all items have been packed
	    var omscheck = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;

    	// If OMS check for items not fully packed and prompt, otherwise disallow partial packs
    	if( omscheck == "OMS") {
    		if( orderItemList !== null)	{
    			var orderItemListCount1 = orderItemList.length;
    			for (var i = 0; i < orderItemListCount1; i++) {
    				if( orderItemList[i].qtyordered != orderItemList[i].qtyshipped ) {
    					var msg = 'SKU: ' + orderItemList[i].itemsku + ' has not been fully packed. Click OK to continue or Cancel to continue packing.';
    					var r = confirm(msg);
    					if( r === false )
    						throw Error("Ship cancelled - please continue packing.");
    				}
    			}
    		}
    	} else {
    		if( orderItemList !== null)	{
    			var orderItemListCount = orderItemList.length;
    			for (var j = 0; j < orderItemListCount; j++) {
    				if( orderItemList[j].qtyordered != orderItemList[j].qtyshipped ) {
    					var msg2 = 'SKU: ' + orderItemList[j].itemsku + ' has not been fully packed.';
    					throw Error(msg2);
    				}
    			}
    		}
    	}
	    var itempackedlist = JSON.stringify(orderItemList);

    	//alert("itempackedlist JSONized: " + itempackedlist);

  	    userParams.PACKEDDATA = itempackedlist;
        };

// function ShowAlert(title, msg) // returns undefined
    function ShowAlert(title, msg){
        vm.currentShipment.AlertTitle = title;
        vm.currentShipment.AlertMessage = msg;
        $alertModal.modal('show');
    }

// function HideAlert() // returns undefined
    function HideAlert(){
        $alertModal.modal('hide');
    }

// this.handleItemSkuTextChanged(event) // returns undefined
    this.handleItemSkuTextChanged = function(event) {

        var newitemsku = this.Packages[0].MiscReference10;
		if( newitemsku.trim().length === 0 )
			return;

        //debugger;
        
		//alert("Item number: " + orderItemList[1].itemcode + "  qtyordered: " + orderItemList[1].qtyordered + " qtyshipped: " + orderItemList[1].qtyshipped);

		// Check for item code SHIPCOMPLETE indicating that this order is complete
		if( newitemsku == "SHIPCOMPLETE") {

            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = "SHIPCOMPLETE";
		    //var pkg = sox_current_shipment.packages[sox_current_package_idx];
			//pkg.misc_reference_5 = "SHIPCOMPLETE";
			//$("#item_sku_txt").val("");			
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
			vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// Check for SHIP indicating that this box is complete but not the whole order
		if( newitemsku == "SHIP") {
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference5 = "";		    
		    //var pkg = sox_current_shipment.packages[sox_current_package_idx];
			//pkg.misc_reference_5 = "";
			//$("#item_sku_txt").val("");			
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";			
			vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// Pad the input sku to 14 digits with leading zeros
		var skulen = newitemsku.length;
		var newitemskupad = "";
		if( skulen == 6)
			newitemskupad = '00000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 7)
			newitemskupad = '0000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 8)
			newitemskupad = '000000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 9)
			newitemskupad = '00000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 10)
			newitemskupad = '0000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 11)
			newitemskupad = '000' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 12)
			newitemskupad = '00' + newitemsku;
		else if( skulen == 13)
			newitemskupad = '0' + newitemsku;
		else
			newitemskupad = newitemsku;
			
		newitemsku = newitemskupad;

		//alert("newitemsku: " + newitemsku);

        //alert("orderItemList length: " + orderItemList.length);
        
        //alert("orderItemList itemsku: " + orderItemList[0].itemsku);
       
       //debugger;
       
		// Verify item sku is on this order
		var itemFound = false;
		var orderItemListCount = orderItemList.length;
		for (var i = 0; i < orderItemListCount; i++) {
		    if( itemFound === true)
		        break;
			var skuarr = orderItemList[i].itemsku.split(",");
			for(var j = 0; j < skuarr.length; j++) {
				if( skuarr[j] == newitemsku ) {
					itemFound = true;
					break;
				}
			}
		}
		
		//alert("itemFound: " + itemFound);
		
		if( itemFound === false) {
			ShowAlert("Pack Error","This SKU (" + newitemsku + ") does not belong in this shipment. Please remove it before proceeding.");
            $("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	    				
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
            return;			
		}

		// Search for itemcode
		itemFound = false;
		var fullyPacked = false;
		var svSkuCode = "";
		var orderItemListCount = orderItemList.length;
		for (var i = 0; i < orderItemListCount; i++) {
			if( itemFound == true)
				break;
			
			var nextitem = false;
			var skuarr = orderItemList[i].itemsku.split(",");
			for(var j = 0; j < skuarr.length; j++) {
				if( skuarr[j] == newitemsku ) {
					if( orderItemList[i].qtyshipped == orderItemList[i].qtyordered ) {
						fullyPacked = true;
						nextitem = true;
						break;
					} else {
						itemFound = true;
						fullyPacked = false;
						var tmpqtyshipped = Number(orderItemList[i].qtyshipped);
						var tmptotqtyshipped = Number(orderItemList[i].totqtyshipped);
						var tmpqtyordered = Number(orderItemList[i].qtyordered);
						if( (tmpqtyshipped + tmptotqtyshipped) < tmpqtyordered) {
							var calcqty1 = tmpqtyshipped + 1 + tmptotqtyshipped;
							var calcqty2 = tmpqtyordered - tmpqtyshipped - tmptotqtyshipped;
							/*alert("Calc quantity 1: " + calcqty1 + " qtyordered: " + tmpqtyordered);*/
							/*alert("Calc quantity 2: " + calcqty2);*/
							if( calcqty1 <= tmpqtyordered) {
								var tmpnewqty = tmpqtyshipped + 1;
								orderItemList[i].qtyshipped = tmpnewqty;
								orderItemList[i].modified = true;
								svSkuCode = newitemsku;
								/*alert("Item added to box ok");*/
							} else {
							    ShowAlert("Pack Error","Scanned quantity for SKU (" + newitemsku + ") would exceed order quantity. Please remove extras from the shipment and try again.");
								$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	    				
                                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
                                angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
								return;							
							}
						} else {
							ShowAlert("Pack Alert","This item has been fully packed");
							$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	    				
                            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
                            angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
							return;							
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if( nextitem == true)
				continue;
		}

		if( fullyPacked == true) {
			ShowAlert("Pack Alert","This item has been fully packed");
			$("#mr10").css("background-color","Red");        	    				
			vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
			angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
			return;					
		}

		$("#mr10").css("background-color","Green");        	    	

		//if( itemFound == false) {
		//	ShowAlert("Pack Error 2","This SKU (" + newitemsku + ") does not belong in this shipment. Please remove it before proceeding.");
		//} else {
        //    $("#mr10").css("background-color","Green");        	    	
		//}

        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10 = "";
        angular.element('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"]').focus();    	                                
		}

// GetEmail() // returns string
   GetEmail(){
      var emailText = "";
      var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a"); 
      Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag){
         if(tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!","").trim(); 
      });
      return emailText;
   }

// AssignCustomEvents() // returns undefined
this.AssignCustomEvents = function(){
        $("#btnCustomBatchProcessing").on( "click", function() {
        debugger;
            var userMethodParams = {"ActionMessage": "CustomBatchProcessing"};
            var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
            var shipExecServiceUrl = client.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
            var authorizationToken = client.getAuthorizationToken();
            $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + 'UserMethod', data : data, async:false, headers: authorizationToken });
        });     
    }

// InitiateDelegates() // returns undefined
InitiateDelegates()
    {
      let that = this

      $('body').delegate('#btnAssignCommodities', 'click', function()
      {
        if ($('#divAssignCommodities:visible').length > 0) return;
        that.ShowAssignGoodsPane();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#btnApplyCommodityAssignments', 'click', function(e)
      {
        that.ApplyCommodityAssignments();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#btnCancelAssignGoods', 'click', function(e)
      {
        that.HideAssignGoodsPane();
      });

      $('body').delegate('.assign-to-new-box', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        $('button[ng-click="vm.addPackage();"]').trigger('click').promise().done((e) =>
        {
          const cp = +$('#spanCurrentPackageIndex').text();
          that.MoveGoodToBox(li, cp);
        });
      });

      $('body').delegate('.assign-to-current-box', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        const cp = +$('#spanCurrentPackageIndex').text();
        that.MoveGoodToBox(li, cp);
      });

      $('body').delegate('.undo-box-assignment', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        that.MoveGoodToBox(li, 1);
      });

    }

            ];
            
            var name = document.querySelector("body > div.main-container > div.container-fluid.body-content.body > div > div.ng-scope > div > div > div:nth-child(2)");
            name.appendChild(document.createElement('div')).innerHTML = desc;
            
            alert('Please click on "Close Manifest" to transfer all your shipping information to UPS.')
        }
		
		 if (location === '/closemanifest') {
        $('.panel-footer').append('<div style="margin-left:10px"><b>For scheduling pick-up, please <a target="_blank" href="'+ pickuplink +'">click here</a> to access the contact details of nearest UPS center.</div>'); 
    
    }
    }

// PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns undefined
    this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
        let confirmReprocess = confirm("Do you want to create more shipments?" + "\n" + " OK = YES and CANCEL = NO");

        if (confirmReprocess) {
            document.location = '#!/shipping';
        } else {
            document.location = '#!/closemanifest';
        }
    }

// Source: Boston Scientific (BOSTON)_Boston Coyol Client Business Rules_2474.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {  
    if (location === '/shipping') {
       // debugger;
       
       // Get the Logon Profiles Custom Data Values Which Determine the Shipping Options Available to them
        if (this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData === "undefined" || this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData === null){
           throw ({ message: 'User Is Missing Required Custom Data Values in Management Studio User Manager Setup Under Address Tab.', errorCode: '' }); 
        }
     
        this.GetCustomDataItems();
            console.log(st_AddressType + ' ' + sf_AddressType + ' ' + uPS_Service + ' ' + return_Type + ' ' + user_description + ' ' + dims + ' ' + user_orderNumber + ' ' + cost_Center + ' ' + user_partNumber + ' ' + insured_Value);
        
        this.ShippingLoaded();
        
        var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
        {
            if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]'))) 
            {
                clearInterval(checkExist);
                $('#sf_Address').focus();
                $("#sf_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
                $("#st_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
                $("#svc_select").prop("selectedIndex", 5);
            
                
            }
        }, 400);
        
        //Get Address Book Data
        var addressBookData = {
            CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
            UserId: client.userContext.UserId
        };
        AddressBooks = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_AddressBook', addressBookData, false).responseJSON;
        AddressBooks.AddressBooks.forEach(item => {
            if(item.Name === "COYOL_ShipToAddress"){
                shipToAddressBookId = item.Id;
            }
            if(item.Name === "COYOL_ShipFromAddress"){
                shipFromAddressBookId = item.Id;
            }
        });
        console.log("shipToAddressBookId: " + shipToAddressBookId);
        console.log("shipFromAddressBookId " + shipFromAddressBookId);    
        
        //Get the Shipper Account Number from Profile
        this.GetShipperAccount(); 
        console.log(thisShipperAccount);

        this.vm.shipToAddressBookEntries = this.GetShipToAddresses();
        //Setup Ship To Address Drop Down Change Event
       $('body').on('change', '#st_Address', function(e) {             // Not seeing a difference between using either of these as far as GUI reacts.
            var userSelectedShipToCompany = $('#st_Address option:selected').text();
            console.log("User Selected ShipTo Company :" + userSelectedShipToCompany);
            for(let i = 0; i < ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
                if(userSelectedShipToCompany ==  ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company){
                    SelectedShipToAddress = ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i];
                    vm.populateShipToAddress();
                }
            } 
            
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
            {
                if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]'))) 
                {
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address2"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address3"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                    
                    
                }
            }, 300);
        });

        
        this.vm.returnAddressBookEntries = this.GetShipFromAddresses();
        //Setup Ship From Address Drop Down Change Event
        $('body').on('change', '#sf_Address', function(e) {
            //debugger;
            SelectedReturnAddress = null;
            var userSelectedReturnCompany = $('#sf_Address option:selected').text();
            console.log("User Selected Return Company :" + userSelectedReturnCompany);
            for(let i = 0; i < ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
                if(userSelectedReturnCompany ==  ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company){
                    SelectedReturnAddress = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i];
                    vm.populateReturnAddress();
                }
            } 
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
            {
                if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]'))) 
                {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address2"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address3"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                  
                }
            }, 300);
         
        });
        
        $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount"]', function(e){
             
            if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount > 2500 ){
                alert('ITN/AES Transaction Number Required');
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
                
            }
        });
        
        
       // $('#billWeight').after('<div id="billable_weight"><strong id="billable_weight_text"></strong></div>');
       // $('#volumetricWeight').after('<div id="custom_volumetric"><span id="volumetric_value_text"></span></div>');
       
        $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]', function(e){
            // debugger;
              totalShipWeight = 0;
              
              vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
                totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
              });
              
              totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
              //console.log(totalShipWeight);
             
              document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
         });
       
          $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height"]', function(e){
           
            totalVolumetricResult = 0;
           
            vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
                totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
            });
            //debugger;
             totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
            console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
         
            $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
         
            document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
            
            if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
            {
                $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
                throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
            }
           
        });
       
    }
};

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {    
  
    // We will require the actual shipment to send weight and dims in kg/cm
    // However, because US Vendors are sending the product the client gui needs to be in Lb/In.
    
    debugger;
    //kg = lbs*0.453592 
    totalShipWeight = 0;
    totalVolumetricResult = 0;
    
    vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
        totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
    });
              
    totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
    console.log(totalShipWeight);
    console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
    if (totalShipWeight > 150)
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Shipment Weight Limit of 150lbs")
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule " + totalShipWeight);
    }
    
    if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
    {
        alert("Total Shipment Weight Exceeds Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Limit of " + Number(maxvolumetric))
        throw new Error("Shipping halted due to Total Shipment Volumetric Weight Rule " + Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2));
    }
    
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Weight.Units === "LB"){
             pkg.Weight.Amount = Number(pkg.Weight.Amount * 0.453592).toFixed(2);
             pkg.Weight.Units = "KG";
         }
         
     });
     
    //cm=in/0.39370
     vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
         if (pkg.Dimensions.Units === 0){
             pkg.Dimensions.Length = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Width = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Height = Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height/0.39370).toFixed(2)
             pkg.Dimensions.Units = 1;
         }
         
     });
     
     
    // debugger;
      if(Number(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount).toFixed(2) > 2500 ){
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = "OS";
          }
          if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber === null){
              vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
              $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
              throw new Error('Missing AES/ITN Number');
          } 
          if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber !== null){
              shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Comments + "\n ITN/AES Filer " + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
             
          }
      }
     
    console.log(shipmentRequest);
  
};

// ShippingLoaded() // returns void
this.ShippingLoaded = function(){
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress;
    this.vm.serviceOption = serviceOption;
    this.vm.serviceOptions = serviceOptions(this.vm.profile);
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
   

    function serviceOption() {
        this.selectedServices = [this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service];
    }
    function serviceOptions(profile) {
        //debugger;
        var filterServices = [];
        var customData3 = uPS_Service.split(',');
        for (var item of customData3) {
            var symbol = getServiceSymbol(item.toLowerCase());
            for (var service of profile.Services) {
                if (service.Symbol === symbol) {
                    service.Name = service.Name.replace('(UPS Adapter)','').trim();
                    if (service.Name.includes("Expedited")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (MAIN SERVICE)";
                    }
                    if (service.Name.includes("Saver")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (Only with Boston's Authorization)";
                    }
                    filterServices.push(service);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return filterServices;
        function getServiceSymbol(code) {
            if (code == '2dn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.2DA'
            else if (code == '3dd') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.3DS'
            else if (code == 'exp') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'ess') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'nda') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDA'
            else if (code == 'dae') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDAEAM'
            else if (code == 'grn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.GND'
            else if (code == 'uwe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'wep') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESSSP'
            else if (code == 'swe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'uws') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER'
            else if (code == 'std') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD'
        }
        
    }
    
    if(dims.includes(',')){
        var dimensions = dims.split(',');
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount = Number(dimensions[0]);
        maxvolumetric = Number(dimensions[4]);
        console.log("Max Volumetric: " + maxvolumetric);
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Dimensions = {
            Length: Number(dimensions[1]),
            Height: Number(dimensions[2]),
            Width: Number(dimensions[3]),
            Units: 0
        };
    }
   
    vm = this.vm;
};

// PopulateReturnAddress() // returns void
this.PopulateReturnAddress = function(){
   // debugger;
   
    if(SelectedReturnAddress !== undefined && SelectedReturnAddress !== null){
         this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee = {
            Code : SelectedReturnAddress.Code,
            Company : SelectedReturnAddress.Company,
            Contact : SelectedReturnAddress.Contact,
            Address1 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address1,
            Address2 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address2,
            Address3 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address3,
            City : SelectedReturnAddress.City,
            StateProvince : SelectedReturnAddress.StateProvince,
            PostalCode : SelectedReturnAddress.PostalCode,
            Country : SelectedReturnAddress.Country,
            Email : SelectedReturnAddress.Email,
            Phone : SelectedReturnAddress.Phone
        };
    }
};

// PopulateShipToAddress() // returns void
this.PopulateShipToAddress = function(){
 // debugger;
    if(SelectedShipToAddress !== undefined && SelectedShipToAddress !== null){
         this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {
            Code : SelectedShipToAddress.Code,
            Company : SelectedShipToAddress.Company,
            Contact : SelectedShipToAddress.Contact,
            Address1 : SelectedShipToAddress.Address1,
            Address2 : SelectedShipToAddress.Address2,
            Address3 : SelectedShipToAddress.Address3,
            City : SelectedShipToAddress.City,
            StateProvince : SelectedShipToAddress.StateProvince,
            PostalCode : SelectedShipToAddress.PostalCode,
            Country : SelectedShipToAddress.Country,
            Email : SelectedShipToAddress.Email,
            Phone : SelectedShipToAddress.Phone
        };
    }
};

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
  // debugger;
  
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress
  
    $('#sf_Address').focus();
    $("#sf_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
    $("#st_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
   // $('#billable_weight_text').html(0.00 + ' Lbs');
   // $('#volumetric_value_text').html(0.00 +' Lbs');
    
   
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
    //debugger;
     this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = {
         Symbol:"UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED"
     };
     
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber = null;
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode = 'OS';
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount = null;
     
    

};

         });
       
          $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height"]', function(e){
           
            totalVolumetricResult = 0;
           
            vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
                totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
            });
             totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
            //console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
         
            $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
         
            document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
            //debugger;
            if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
            {
                $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
                throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
            }
           
        });
    }
};

// ShippingLoaded() // returns void
this.ShippingLoaded = function(){
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress;
    this.vm.serviceOption = serviceOption;
    this.vm.serviceOptions = serviceOptions(this.vm.profile);
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = cost_Center;
    //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = po_number;
    //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = po_Number;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
  
    function serviceOption() {
        this.selectedServices = [this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service];
    }
    function serviceOptions(profile) {
        //debugger;
        var filterServices = [];
        var customData3 = uPS_Service.split(',');
        for (var item of customData3) {
            var symbol = getServiceSymbol(item.toLowerCase());
            for (var service of profile.Services) {
                if (service.Symbol === symbol) {
                    //service.Name = service.Name.replace('(UPS Adapter)','').trim();
                    filterServices.push(service);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return filterServices;
        function getServiceSymbol(code) {
             if (code == '2dn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.2DA'
            else if (code == '3dd') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.3DS'
            else if (code == 'exp') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'ess') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'nda') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDA'
            else if (code == 'dae') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDAEAM'
            else if (code == 'grn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.GND'
            else if (code == 'uwe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'wep') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESSSP'
            else if (code == 'swe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'uws') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER'
            else if (code == 'std') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD'
        }
        
    }
    
    if(dims.includes(',')){
        var dimensions = dims.split(',');
        
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount = Number(dimensions[0]);
        maxvolumetric = Number(dimensions[4]);
        console.log("Max Volumetric: " + maxvolumetric);
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Dimensions = {
            Length: Number(dimensions[1]),
            Height: Number(dimensions[2]),
            Width: Number(dimensions[3]),
            Units: 0
        };
    }
    vm = this.vm;
};

// PopulateReturnAddress() // returns void
this.PopulateReturnAddress = function(){
    // debugger;
    if(SelectedReturnAddress !== undefined && SelectedReturnAddress !== null){
         this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee = {
            Code : SelectedReturnAddress.Code,
            Company : SelectedReturnAddress.Company,
            Contact : SelectedReturnAddress.Contact,
            Address1 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address1,
            Address2 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address2,
            Address3 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address3,
            City : SelectedReturnAddress.City,
            StateProvince : SelectedReturnAddress.StateProvince,
            PostalCode : SelectedReturnAddress.PostalCode,
            Country : SelectedReturnAddress.Country,
            Email : SelectedReturnAddress.Email,
            Phone : SelectedReturnAddress.Phone
        };
    }
};

// PopulateShipToAddress() // returns void
this.PopulateShipToAddress = function(){
    // debugger;
    if(SelectedShipToAddress !== undefined && SelectedShipToAddress !== null){
         this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {
            Code : SelectedShipToAddress.Code,
            Company : SelectedShipToAddress.Company,
            Contact : SelectedShipToAddress.Contact,
            Address1 : SelectedShipToAddress.Address1,
            Address2 : SelectedShipToAddress.Address2,
            Address3 : SelectedShipToAddress.Address3,
            City : SelectedShipToAddress.City,
            StateProvince : SelectedShipToAddress.StateProvince,
            PostalCode : SelectedShipToAddress.PostalCode,
            Country : SelectedShipToAddress.Country,
            Email : SelectedShipToAddress.Email,
            Phone : SelectedShipToAddress.Phone
        };
    }
};

// GetShipperAccount() // returns void
this.GetShipperAccount = function(){
    //debugger;
    var shippers = this.vm.profile.Shippers;
    shippers.forEach(shipper => {
       if(shipper.Name === "Boston Scientific HEREDIA"){
           var shipperCustomData = shipper.CustomData;
            shipperCustomData.forEach(item => {
                 if(item.Key === "Account"){
                     thisShipperAccount = item.Value;
                     
                 }
                 
            });  
        } 
        else{
            throw ({ message: 'No Shipper Found for User Profile', errorCode: '' });
        }
    });
};

// GetCustomDataItems() // returns void
this.GetCustomDataItems = function(){
    //debugger;
    userCustomData = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData;
   
    st_AddressType = client.getValueByKey('Custom1',userCustomData);   
    sf_AddressType = client.getValueByKey('Custom2',userCustomData);  
    uPS_Service = client.getValueByKey('Custom3',userCustomData);        
    return_Type = client.getValueByKey('Custom4',userCustomData);            
    user_description = client.getValueByKey('Custom5',userCustomData);             
    dims = client.getValueByKey('Custom6',userCustomData);                   
    user_orderNumber = client.getValueByKey('Custom7',userCustomData);     
    cost_Center = client.getValueByKey('Custom8',userCustomData);        
    user_partNumber = client.getValueByKey('Custom9',userCustomData);     
    insured_Value = client.getValueByKey('Custom10',userCustomData);     
    
    
    
};

// GetShipToAddresses() // returns Array
this.GetShipToAddresses = function(){
    var payloadShipToAddress = {
        "Skip": 0,
        "Take": 10,
        "WhereClauses": [{
            "FieldName": "Group",
            "FieldValue": "2",
            "Operator": 0
        }]
    };
    
    var data = {
        CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
        addressBookIds: shipToAddressBookId,
        SearchCriteria: payloadShipToAddress
    };
    //console.log(data);
  
    ShipToAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', data, false).responseJSON;

    console.log(ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries);
    
    return ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries;
            
};

// GetShipFromAddresses() // returns Array
this.GetShipFromAddresses = function(){
    var payloadShipFromAddress = {
        "Skip": 0,
        "Take": 0,
        "WhereClauses": [{
           "FieldName": "Code",
                    "FieldValue": sf_AddressType,   //'ze-'
                    "Operator": 6
                }]
    };
 
    var sfdata = {
        CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
        addressBookIds: shipFromAddressBookId,
        SearchCriteria: payloadShipFromAddress
    };
   
    ShipFromAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', sfdata, false).responseJSON;
    
     //debugger;
    
    for(let i = 0; i < ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
    
        ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Code = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Code.replace("&amp;",'&');
        ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company.replace("&amp;",'&');
   }


    console.log(ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries);
    
    return ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries;
};

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
    // debugger;
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress
   
    $('#sf_Address').focus();
    $("#sf_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
    $("#st_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
   // $('#billable_weight_text').html(0.00 + ' Lbs');
  //  $('#volumetric_value_text').html(0.00 +' Lbs');
   
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = cost_Center;
    //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = po_Number;
    //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = po_Number;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
    
    this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = {
         Symbol:"UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER"
    };
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber = null;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode = 'OS';
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount = null;
  
};

// AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
     //debugger;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
    //shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Packaging = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Packaging;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Description;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ExportInformationCode = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode;
    shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].SedMethod = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].SedMethod;

}

// RemovePackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.RemovePackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
      
      var totalShipWeight = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
      });
      totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
      document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
      
      var totalVolumetricResult = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
           totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
      });
      totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
      $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
      document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
      if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
        {
           $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
           throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
        }
  
      
}

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {  
    if (location === '/shipping') {
       // debugger;
       
       // Get the Logon Profiles Custom Data Values Which Determine the Shipping Options Available to them
        if (this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData === "undefined" || this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData === null){
           throw ({ message: 'User Is Missing Required Custom Data Values in Management Studio User Manager Setup Under Address Tab.', errorCode: '' }); 
        }
     
        this.GetCustomDataItems();
            console.log(st_AddressType + ' ' + sf_AddressType + ' ' + uPS_Service + ' ' + return_Type + ' ' + user_description + ' ' + dims + ' ' + user_orderNumber + ' ' + cost_Center + ' ' + user_partNumber + ' ' + insured_Value);
        
        this.ShippingLoaded();
        
        var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
        {
            if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]'))) 
            {
                clearInterval(checkExist);
                $('#sf_Address').focus();
                $("#sf_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
                $("#st_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
                $("#svc_select").prop("selectedIndex", 5);
            
                
            }
        }, 400);
        
        //Get Address Book Data
        var addressBookData = {
            CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
            UserId: client.userContext.UserId
        };
        AddressBooks = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_AddressBook', addressBookData, false).responseJSON;
        AddressBooks.AddressBooks.forEach(item => {
            if(item.Name === "MULTI_ST"){
                shipToAddressBookId = item.Id;
            }
            if(item.Name === "MULTI_SF"){
                shipFromAddressBookId = item.Id;
            }
        });
        console.log("shipToAddressBookId: " + shipToAddressBookId);
        console.log("shipFromAddressBookId " + shipFromAddressBookId);    
        
        //Get the Shipper Account Number from Profile
        //this.GetShipperAccount(); 
        //console.log(thisShipperAccount);

        this.vm.shipToAddressBookEntries = this.GetShipToAddresses();
        //Setup Ship To Address Drop Down Change Event
       $('body').on('change', '#st_Address', function(e) {             // Not seeing a difference between using either of these as far as GUI reacts.
            var userSelectedShipToCompany = $('#st_Address option:selected').text();
            console.log("User Selected ShipTo Company :" + userSelectedShipToCompany);
            for(let i = 0; i < ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
                if(userSelectedShipToCompany ==  ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company){
                    SelectedShipToAddress = ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i];
                    vm.populateShipToAddress();
                }
            } 
            
            //Multi Profile only
            
            if(userSelectedShipToCompany == "BOSTON SCIENTIFIC COYOL"){
                vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "BS_26737";
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = "26737";
                //vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = {
                //    Symbol:"UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED"
                //};
            }
            if(userSelectedShipToCompany == "BOSTON SCIENTIFIC HEREDIA"){
                vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper = "BS_26701";
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = "26701";
               // vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = {
               //     Symbol:"UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER"
               // };
            }
            
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
            {
                if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]'))) 
                {
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address2"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address3"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                  
                }
            }, 300);
        });

        
        this.vm.returnAddressBookEntries = this.GetShipFromAddresses();
        //Setup Ship From Address Drop Down Change Event
        $('body').on('change', '#sf_Address', function(e) {
            //debugger;
            SelectedReturnAddress = null;
            var userSelectedReturnCompany = $('#sf_Address option:selected').text();
            console.log("User Selected Return Company :" + userSelectedReturnCompany);
            for(let i = 0; i < ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
                if(userSelectedReturnCompany ==  ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company){
                    SelectedReturnAddress = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i];
                    vm.populateReturnAddress();
                }
            } 
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () 
            {
                if (($) && ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]'))) 
                {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address2"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="nameaddress.Address3"]').focus();
                    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                  
                }
            }, 300);
         
        });
        
        $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount"]', function(e){
             
            if(vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount > 2500 ){
                alert('ITN/AES Transaction Number Required');
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].AesTransactionNumber"]').focus();
                
            }
        });
        
        
       // $('#billWeight').after('<div id="billable_weight"><strong id="billable_weight_text"></strong></div>');
       // $('#volumetricWeight').after('<div id="custom_volumetric"><span id="volumetric_value_text"></span></div>');
       
        $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]', function(e){
            // debugger;
              totalShipWeight = 0;
              
              vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
                totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
              });
              
              totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
              //console.log(totalShipWeight);
             
              document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
         });
       
          $('body').on('keyup', '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width"],[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height"]', function(e){
           
            totalVolumetricResult = 0;
           
            vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
                totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
            });
             totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
            //console.log(totalVolumetricResult);
         
            $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
         
            document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
            //debugger;
            if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
            {
                $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
                throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
            }
           
        });
       
    }
};

// ShippingLoaded() // returns undefined
this.ShippingLoaded = function(){
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress;
    this.vm.serviceOption = serviceOption;
    this.vm.serviceOptions = serviceOptions(this.vm.profile);
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
   

    function serviceOption() {
        this.selectedServices = [this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service];
    }
    function serviceOptions(profile) {
        //debugger;
        var filterServices = [];
        var customData3 = uPS_Service.split(',');
        for (var item of customData3) {
            var symbol = getServiceSymbol(item.toLowerCase());
            for (var service of profile.Services) {
                if (service.Symbol === symbol) {
                    service.Name = service.Name.replace('(UPS Adapter)','').trim();
                    if (service.Name.includes("Expedited")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (MAIN SERVICE)";
                    }
                    if (service.Name.includes("Saver")){
                        service.Name = service.Name + " (To Heredia or Only with Boston's Authorization)";
                    }
                    filterServices.push(service);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return filterServices;
        function getServiceSymbol(code) {
            if (code == '2dn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.2DA'
            else if (code == '3dd') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.3DS'
            else if (code == 'exp') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'ess') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'nda') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDA'
            else if (code == 'dae') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.NDAEAM'
            else if (code == 'grn') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.GND'
            else if (code == 'uwe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED'
            else if (code == 'wep') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESSSP'
            else if (code == 'swe') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS'
            else if (code == 'uws') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.SAVER'
            else if (code == 'std') return 'UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD'
        }
        
    }
    
    if(dims.includes(',')){
        var dimensions = dims.split(',');
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount = Number(dimensions[0]);
        maxvolumetric = Number(dimensions[4]);
        console.log("Max Volumetric: " + maxvolumetric);
        this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Dimensions = {
            Length: Number(dimensions[1]),
            Height: Number(dimensions[2]),
            Width: Number(dimensions[3]),
            Units: 0
        };
    }
   
    vm = this.vm;
};

   // debugger;

         this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee = {
            Code : SelectedReturnAddress.Code,
            Company : SelectedReturnAddress.Company,
            Contact : SelectedReturnAddress.Contact,
            Address1 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address1,
            Address2 : SelectedReturnAddress.Address2,

            StateProvince : SelectedReturnAddress.StateProvince,

    }

    var payloadShipToAddress = {
        "Skip": 0,
        "Take": 10,
        "WhereClauses": [{
            "FieldName": "Group",
            "FieldValue": "3",
            "Operator": 0
        }]
    };
    
    var data = {
        CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
        addressBookIds: shipToAddressBookId,
        SearchCriteria: payloadShipToAddress
    };
    //console.log(data);
  
    ShipToAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', data, false).responseJSON;

    console.log(ShipToAddressBook.AddressBookEntries);
