// GetShipFromAddresses() // returns array of address book entries
this.GetShipFromAddresses = function(){
    var payloadShipFromAddress = {
        "Skip": 0,
        "Take": 0,
        "WhereClauses": [{
           "FieldName": "Code",
                    "FieldValue": sf_AddressType,   //'ze-'
                    "Operator": 6
                }]
    };
 
    var sfdata = {
        CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId,
        addressBookIds: shipFromAddressBookId,
        SearchCriteria: payloadShipFromAddress
    };
   
    ShipFromAddressBook = client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_AddressBook', sfdata, false).responseJSON;
    
     //debugger;
    
    for(let i = 0; i < ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries.length; i++){
    
        ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Code = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Code.replace("&amp;",'&');
        ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company = ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries[i].Company.replace("&amp;",'&');
   }


    console.log(ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries);
    
    return ShipFromAddressBook.AddressBookEntries;
};

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
  // debugger;
  
    this.vm.populateReturnAddress = this.PopulateReturnAddress;
    this.vm.populateShipToAddress = this.PopulateShipToAddress
  
    $('#sf_Address').focus();
    $("#sf_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
    $("#st_Address").prop("selectedIndex", 0);
   // $('#billable_weight_text').html(0.00 + ' Lbs');
   // $('#volumetric_value_text').html(0.00 +' Lbs');
    
   
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = user_orderNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = cost_Center;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference3 = user_partNumber;
    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Description = user_description;
    //debugger;
    // this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = {
    //     Symbol:"UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED"
    // };
     
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].SedMethod = 2;
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].AesTransactionNumber = null;
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].ExportInformationCode = 'OS';
     this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms.Amount = null;

};

// RemovePackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
this.RemovePackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
      var totalShipWeight = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
        totalShipWeight += Number(pkg.Weight.Amount);
      });
      totalShipWeight = Number(totalShipWeight).toFixed(2);
      document.getElementById('totWgt').innerHTML = totalShipWeight;
      
      var totalVolumetricResult = 0;
      vm.currentShipment.Packages.forEach(pkg => {
           totalVolumetricResult += ((Number(pkg.Dimensions.Length).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Width).toFixed(2)*Number(pkg.Dimensions.Height)).toFixed(2))/166;
      });
      totalVolumetricResult = Number(totalVolumetricResult).toFixed(2);
      $('#volumetric_value_text').html(totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs');
      document.getElementById('totVolumeWgt').innerHTML = totalVolumetricResult;
      if (totalVolumetricResult > Number(maxvolumetric))
        {
           $('#totVolumeWgt').html('<span>'+totalVolumetricResult+' Lbs <br> <small style="color:red;font-weight:normal;">Weight Over Maximum Allowed Please Review</small></span>');
           throw ({ 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule': 'Shipping halted due to Over Maximum Weight Rule' });
        }
  
};

this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
    // debugger;
    $('button[ng-click="vm.newShipment()"]').click();
};

        }

// ChangeTransportationCharges() // returns undefined
    this.ChangeTransportationCharges = function () {
        var shipmentRequest = this.currentShipment;
        var transportationCharges = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.TransportationCharges;

        this.xReceiverAccountsIsHidden = transportationCharges != 'consignee';
        this.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddressCodesIsHidden = transportationCharges != 'thirdParty';

        this.xReceiverAccount = null;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = null;
        this.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress = null;
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress = null;
    }

    }

// TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddressChange() // returns undefined
    this.TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddressChange = function () {
        this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling = true;
        this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress = this.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress;
        this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress = this.xTransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress;
    }

// cvsContinue() // returns undefined
    function cvsContinue() {
        $('body').delegate('div[ng-if="vm.rateResults.length > 0"] tr td a', 'click', serviceUpgrade)
        $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.ReasonForUpgrade"]', 'click', function () {
            if (this.value != '?') {
                $('button:contains("Ship")').prop('disabled', false);
            }
        })

        var validateAddressOnRate = getObjectValue(vm.profile.ProfileSetting.ValidateAddressOnRate);
        if (validateAddressOnRate == 'true') {
            $('body').delegate('[ng-click="vm.returnData(button.role)"]', 'click', defaultRateService)
        } else {
            defaultRateService();
        }
    }

// defaultRateService() // returns undefined
    function defaultRateService() {
        var interval = setInterval(function () {
            var rateModalTable = $('table tbody[ng-repeat="rateResult in vm.rateResults"]');
            var rateModalServices = rateModalTable.find('tr td a');

            if (rateModalServices.length) {
                clearInterval(interval);

                rateModalServices.each(function (index, element) {
                    if ($(this).text() == 'UPS Second Day Air (UPS Adapter)') {
                        $(this).click();
                    }
                });
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// serviceUpgrade() // returns undefined
    function serviceUpgrade() {
        var ignoreReasonService = [
            'UPS Next Day Air Saver (UPS Adapter)',
            'UPS Next Day Air EAM (UPS Adapter)',
            'UPS Next Day Air (UPS Adapter)',
            'UPS Second Day Air AM (UPS Adapter)'
        ]

        var selectedService = $(this).text();
        var ignoreReason = ignoreReasonService.indexOf(selectedService) >= 0;
        if ($('[ng-model="vm.ReasonForUpgrade"]').val() != '?') {
            $('button:contains("Ship")').prop('disabled', false);
        }

        if (!ignoreReason) {
            $('[name="reasonForUpgrade_txt"]').hide();
        } else {
            $('[name="reasonForUpgrade_txt"]').show();
        }
    }

                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').hide();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();
                } else {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').hide();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();
                }
            });

            var tpbSelectedIndex = 0;

            });

            // International Tab

                    if ($consignee.length && consineeSearchAddress.length) {
                        consigneeFound = true;
                    }
                    var loaded = tpbFound && consigneeFound;


                    // console.log(`is consignee loaded: ${loaded}`)

                    if (loaded) {
                        if ($thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').length > 0) {
                            startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Validate Address"]').hide();

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Save Address")').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.IsUpdateAddressBookEntry"]').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').hide();

                            $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').hide();

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Third Party Options")').hide();
                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();

                            //International
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Search Addresses"]').hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('button[title="Validate Address"]').hide();

                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Save Address")').hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.IsUpdateAddressBookEntry"]').hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').hide();

                            $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').hide();

                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('label:contains("Who pays Duties and Taxes")').hide();
                            $dutyAndTaxesthirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();

                        }
                    }
                }
            }, 125);
        }
    };

// Source: Cabinet Works Group (MASCO)_Masco Client Side Business Rules_1752.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {        
        // If we are the Shipping page....Set focus on load field AND define sw.swogShipment on Shipping screen 
        // AND map the vm.f10Keystroke defined in the shipping template to the F10Keystroke function
        if (location === '/shipping') {
            this.vm.swogShipment = this.SWOGShipment;
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                loadText = ('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');
                var loaded = loadText.length;
                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    setFocus(loadText);
                }
            }, 50);           
            this.vm.f10Keystroke = this.F10Keystroke; 
            masterOrderNumber = "";
        }
    }

// F10Keystroke() // returns undefined
this.F10Keystroke = function () {
        // custom function that fires when F10 is pressed that starts the SWOGShipment function
        //alert("F10Keystroke");
        //debugger;
        this.swogShipment();        
    }

// SWOGShipment() // returns undefined
this.SWOGShipment = function () {
        // Custom function that fires when SWOG button is clicked
        // If Shipper is "MCD" "MCT" or "MCC" there is no validation done on SWOGS and then focus on Dimensions when completed
        
        // Get current Shipper from screen       
        var shipper = this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper;        

        debugger;
        // Define initial SWOG array and counter
        var swogArray = ["SWOG_START"];
        var counter = 0;

        // If the masterOrderNumber has an initial SWOG value from PreLoad, push that into the swogArray before collecting new ones.  Set the counter to 1.
        if (masterOrderNumber != '') {
            swogArray.push(masterOrderNumber);
            swogArray = unique(swogArray);
            counter = 1;
        }

        do {
            // Prompt for SWOG data entry until END_SWOG is scanned
            var swog = window.prompt("Enter SWOG order number.  Scan END_SWOG Barcode when complete", "");
            debugger;
            // Make sure swog is not empty
            if (swog != '') {
                if (counter > 0 && swogArray.length > 1) {
                    // This check is only done when the Shipper is NOT MCD, MCT or MCC
                    if (shipper != "MCD" && shipper != "MCT" && shipper != "MCC") {
                        // Make sure the entry is valid (not 'END_SWOG' AND length is greater than 9, not the same as the first entry in the array)
                        if (swog != 'END_SWOG' && swog.length > 9 && swog.substring(0, 9) != swogArray[1].substring(0, 9)) {
                            alert("The order that you scanned = " + swog + " is invalid for this SWOG and will be removed.");
                            swog = '';
                        }
                    }
                }
                // If masterOrderNumber is not empty, this function was called from PreShip.  Otherwise it came from clicking SWOG
                if (masterOrderNumber != '') {
                    // function called from PreShip...validate length of swog
                    if ((swog != '' && swog.length > 9) || swog == 'END_SWOG') {
                        // Add the swog to the swogArray
                        swogArray.push(swog);
                        // Make sure that only unique entries are in the swogArray
                        swogArray = unique(swogArray);
                        counter++;
                    }
                }
                else {
                    // function called from clicking button...do not validate length of swog
                    if (swog != ''  || swog == 'END_SWOG') {
                        // Add the swog to the swogArray
                        swogArray.push(swog);
                        // Make sure that only unique entries are in the swogArray
                        swogArray = unique(swogArray);
                        counter++;
                    }
                }                
            }
        } while (swog != 'END_SWOG');        

        // Put '|' between each SWOG number
        var swogOrderNumbers = "";
        swogArray.forEach(function (item, index, array) { swogOrderNumbers = swogOrderNumbers + "|" + item; });
        swogOrderNumbers = removeFirstChar(swogOrderNumbers);

        // Store final swog data in UserData1
        //this.currentShipment.Packages[0].ShipperReference = 123;
        //this.currentShipment.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = swogOrderNumbers;
        this.currentShipment.Packages[0].UserData1 = swogOrderNumbers;

        // If Shipper IS MCD, MCT or MCC then put focus on length field in dimensions
        if (shipper == "MCD" || shipper == "MCT" || shipper == "MCC") {
            lengthText = ('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]');
            setFocus(lengthText);
        }
        // Clear out masterOrderNumber
        masterOrderNumber = "";
        debugger;
    }

// Keystroke(shipmentRequest, vm, event) // returns undefined
this.Keystroke = function (shipmentRequest, vm, event) {
        debugger;
    }

// PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns undefined
this.PostShip = function (shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
        // if the shipmentRequest comes back with null or an error code, set focus on the Load field
        if (shipmentResponse != null) {
            if (shipmentResponse.PackageDefaults != null) {
                if (shipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode != 0) {
                    loadText = ('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');
                    setFocus(loadText);
                }
            }
        }
        if (shipmentResponse == null) {
            loadText = ('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');
            setFocus(loadText);
        }

    }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
  this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {

    // 🔄 Reset any previous SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = "";

    // 🧾 First prompt: general input
    var firstInput = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###)\n' +
        '— OR type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip dimensions\n' +
        '— OR enter a SWOG Order Number to start the SWOG function:',
        ''
    );

    if (firstInput === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";
        return;  // ❌ Cancelled
    }

    firstInput = firstInput.trim();
    var dimRegex = /^[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+\s*x\s*[0-9]+$/i;

    if (firstInput.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';
        return;  // ✅ Skip dimensions
    }

    if (dimRegex.test(firstInput)) {
        userParams.dimensions = firstInput.toLowerCase();
        return;  // ✅ Valid dimensions directly
    }

    // 🌀 Else: treat as SWOG starter
    masterOrderNumber = firstInput;
    this.vm.swogShipment();

    // 🧾 Second prompt after SWOG
    var dimsAfterSwog = window.prompt(
        'Enter Package Dimensions (###x###x###), type PACKSIZE_CONTINUE to skip, or leave blank:',
        ''
    );

    if (dimsAfterSwog === null) {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Cancelled
        return;
    }

    dimsAfterSwog = dimsAfterSwog.trim();

    if (dimsAfterSwog.toUpperCase() === 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE') {
        userParams.dimensions = 'PACKSIZE_CONTINUE';  // ✅ PACKSIZE_CONTINUE accepted in second prompt too
    } else if (dimRegex.test(dimsAfterSwog)) {
        userParams.dimensions = dimsAfterSwog.toLowerCase();  // ✅ Dimensions entered
    } else {
        userParams.dimensions = "";  // ❌ Nothing valid entered
    }
}

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        let vm = this.vm ?? {};
        vm.thinClient = thinClient.vm;
        // let httpClient = this.httpClient;

        clearInterval(thinClient.notificationIntervalId);

        if (location == '/') document.location = '#!/shipping'
        else if (location == '/shipping') shipping();
        else if (location == '/history') history();

        function shipping () {
            vm.shipping = {
                panelMessage: '',
                loadValue: '[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]',
                notificationInterval: 1800000, //30 minutes
                // notificationInterval: 1200000, //20 minutes
                // notificationInterval: 5000, //5 seconds
                videoModal: {
                    selector: '#VideoModalId',
                    zoom: {
                        in: zoomIn,
                        out: zoomOut,
                    },
                    close: videoModalClose,
                    stream: {
                        selector: '#CameraStreamId',
                        start: videoStreamStart,
                        stop: videoStreamStop,
                        captureImage: captureImage
                    }
                },
                imageFile: {
                    selector: '#CarrierLabelImageId',
                    upload: uploadCarrierLabelFile
                },
                menu: {
                    guide: {
                        inputFile: {
                            selector: '#inputFileDownload',
                        }
                    }
                },
                load: loadShip,
                customerChange: customerChange,
                getNotification: getNotification,
                selectDownloadFile: selectDownloadFile
            }
            vm.shipping.videoModal.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.imageFile.id = vm.shipping.imageFile.selector.substring(1);
            vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.id = vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector.substring(1);

            $(document).on('change', vm.shipping.imageFile.selector, uploadCarrierLabelFile);
            $(document).on('change', vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector, inputFileDownloadChange);

            vm.shipping.slic = vm.UserInformation.SiteId ? vm.profile.Name.substring(0,5) : vm.profile.Name == thinClient.adminProfileName ? "XXXXX" : null;
            vm.shipping.customers = getShipperCustomers(vm.profile.Shippers);
            var enabledCustomers = vm.shipping.customers.filter(function(c) { return c.disabled != true; });
            vm.shipping.customer = enabledCustomers.length == 1 ? vm.shipping.customers[1] : vm.shipping.customers[0];
            vm.shipping.activePanel = vm.shipping.slic == undefined || vm.clientContext.Machine.Name == undefined ? 0 : 1;

            debugger;

            vm.fieldOptions = {
                Consignee: {
                    hideSaveAddress: true,
                    hideAddressSearch: true,
                    hideValidateAddress: true
                },
                ReturnAddress: {
                    hideSaveAddress: true,
                    hideAddressSearch: true,
                    hideValidateAddress: true
                }
            };
            vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference18.IsDisabled = true;
            vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference20.DefaultValue = vm.shipping.slic;
            vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = vm.shipping.slic;

            activate();

            function activate() {
                if (!vm.profile.FieldOptions?.Reference?.IsHidden)
                    'form[name="referenceForm"] .panel > div'.unwrap();

                'name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] div[active="activeSubtabIndex"]'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[ng-hide="poBox.isHidden()"'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[active="activeSubtabIndex"]'.remove();
                'name-address[address-property-name="ReturnAddress"] div[ng-hide="residential.isHidden()"'.remove();


                vm.shipping.getNotification();
                thinClient.notificationIntervalId = setInterval(function() {
                    vm.shipping.getNotification();
                }, vm.shipping.notificationInterval);

                if (vm.shipping.customer.disabled)
                    vm.shipping.customer.selector.focus();
                else
                    vm.shipping.loadValue.focus();
            }

            function getNotification() {
                var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id }
                thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                    if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications)) {
                        if (vm.clientContext.Site.Name == undefined)
                            vm.notification = null;
                        else {
                            var data = { CompanyId: vm.clientContext.Company.Id, SiteId: vm.clientContext.Site.Id };
                            thinClient.httpClient('GetClientNotifications', data).then(function (ret) {
                                if (!vm.shipping.setNotification(ret.Notifications))
                                    vm.notification = null;

                                vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                            })
                        }
                    }
                    vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                })

                this.setNotification = function(notifications) {
                    var notification = notifications.at(-1);
                    if (notification == undefined) return false;

                    this.notification = {
                        Title: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Title),
                        Message: thinClient.htmlText(notification.Message)
                    }
                    return true;
                }
            }

            function selectDownloadFile(event) {
                this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile = event.target.innerText;
                if (this.menu.guide.inputFile.selected) {
                    if (this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile.slice(-3) == this.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.name.slice(-3))
                        updateFile();
                } else {
                    var payload = { Action: 'downloadFile', Data: this.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile };
                    var data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                    thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                        if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                            var data = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));

                            let linkData = `data:${data.fileType};base64,${data.encodedFile}`;
                            let downloadLink = document.createElement("a");
                            downloadLink.style.display = "none";
                            downloadLink.download = data.fileName;
                            downloadLink.href = linkData;
                            document.body.appendChild(downloadLink);
                            downloadLink.click();
                            document.body.removeChild(downloadLink);
                        }
                    });
                }

                function updateFile() {
                    var reader = new FileReader();
                    reader.onload = function () {
                        var request = {
                            Key: vm.shipping.menu.guide.selectedDownloadFile,
                            Value: JSON.stringify({
                                fileType: vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.type,
                                fileName: vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected.name,
                                encodedFile: this.result.split(',')[1]
                            })
                        }
                        var payload = { Action: 'updateFile', Data: request };
                        var data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                        thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                            if (ret.ErrorCode !== 0)
                                vm.notificationService.notifyDanger(ret.ErrorCode + " - " + ret.ErrorMessage);
                        }).catch(function (response) {
                            vm.notificationService.notifyDanger(vm.translations.Common.ErrorConnectingWCFService + ": " + response.status + " " + response.statusText);
                        })
                        vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected = null;
                        $(vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selector).val(null);
                        vm.thinClient.loadData.show();

                    }
                    if (vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected) reader.readAsDataURL(vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected);
                }
            }

            function inputFileDownloadChange(event) {
                if (event.target.files == undefined) return;
                vm.shipping.menu.guide.inputFile.selected = event.target.files[0];
                vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
            }

            function getShipperCustomers(shippers) {
                var shipper = shippers.find(shipper => shipper.Symbol == vm.shipping.slic);
                if (shipper == undefined)
                     return [{ name: '--- No Shipper Configured ---', disabled: true }];

                var customData = shipper.CustomData.filter(c => c.Key.toUpperCase() == "CUSTOMER");
                var customers = customData.map(function(c) {
                    var customer = c.Value.toUpperCase();

                    if (customer == 'AMAZON')
                        return { name: "Amazon", value: customer, hasLoad: true, hasReturn: true, autoShip: true };
                    else if (customer == 'UPS')
                        return { name: "UPS", value: customer, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'DEMO')
                        return { name: "Demo", value: customer, hasLoad: false, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, hasFileImage: false, autoShip: false };
                    else if (customer == 'FANATICS')
                        return { name: "Fanatics", value: customer, hasReturn: true, hasCameraImage: true, autoShip: false };
                    else
                        return { name: `--- ${customer} ---`, disabled: true };
                });

                customers.sort(function(a, b) {
                    if (a.disabled && !b.disabled) return 1;
                    if (!a.disabled && b.disabled) return -1;
                    return a.name.localeCompare(b.name);
                });
                return [{ name: '--- Select Customer Option ---', selector: 'select[ng-model="vm.shipping.customer"]', disabled: true }].concat(customers);
            }

            function customerChange() {
                vm.shipping.loadValue.focus();
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19 = vm.shipping.customer.value;
            }


            function videoModalClose () {
                var $videoModal = $(vm.shipping.videoModal.selector);
                if ($videoModal.is(':visible'))
                    $videoModal.find('.close').click();
            }

            function uploadCarrierLabelFile () {
                var $carrierLabelImage = $(vm.shipping.imageFile.selector);
                var imageFile = $carrierLabelImage.prop('files')[0];
                if (imageFile == undefined) {
                    $carrierLabelImage.click();
                    return;
                }
                var reader = new FileReader();
                reader.readAsDataURL(imageFile);
                reader.onload = function () {
                    var dataURL = this.result;
                    getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                        console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                    });

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Upload';
                    vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    vm.load();
                    $carrierLabelImage.val(null);
                }
            }

            function captureImage () {
                // vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id = vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.selector
                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                var track = cameraStream.srcObject.getVideoTracks()[0];
                var imageCapture = new ImageCapture(track);

                imageCapture.grabFrame().then(function(imageBitmap) {
                    const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
                    const ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');

                    // Set canvas dimensions to match the imageBitmap
                    canvas.width = imageBitmap.width;
                    canvas.height = imageBitmap.height;

                    // Draw the imageBitmap onto the canvas
                    ctx.drawImage(imageBitmap, 0, 0);

                    // Get the image data as a Base64 data URL
                    // You can specify format and quality (e.g., 'image/jpeg', 0.8)
                    const base64DataUrl = canvas.toDataURL('image/png', 1.0);
                    // var newTab = window.open('about:blank','image from canvas');
                    // newTab.document.write("<img src='" + base64DataUrl + "' alt='from canvas'/>");

                    vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                    vm.labelImage = base64DataUrl.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                    // vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();
                    vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.stop();
                    vm.load();
                })


                // imageCapture.takePhoto().then(function(blob) {
                //     var reader = new FileReader();
                //     reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
                //     reader.onloadend = function () {
                //         var dataURL = reader.result;
                //         getMegapixelsFromFileReader(dataURL).then(function(megapixels) {
                //             console.log(`The image is ${megapixels.toFixed(2)} megapixels.`);
                //         });

                //         vm.loadValue = 'Label Capture';
                //         vm.labelImage = dataURL.replace(/^data:.+;base64,/, '');
                //         vm.videoModal.stopVideoStream();

                //         vm.load();
                //     }
                // })
            }

            function getMegapixelsFromFileReader(fileData) {
                return new Promise(function(resolve, reject) {
                    var img = new Image();
                    img.src = fileData;
                    img.onload = function () {
                        var width = this.naturalWidth;
                        var height = this.naturalHeight;
                        console.log(`Image dimensions: ${width}x${height}`);
                        var megapixels = (width * height) / 1000000;
                        resolve(megapixels);
                    }
                })
            }

            function videoStreamStop(isCanceled) {
                vm.labelImage = isCanceled ? null : vm.labelImage;

                var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                if (cameraStream.srcObject) {
                    var tracks = cameraStream.srcObject.getTracks();
                    tracks.forEach(track => track.stop()); // Stop each track in the stream
                    cameraStream.srcObject = null;
                }
            }


            function videoStreamStart () {
                if (navigator.mediaDevices && navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia) {
                    // Request access to the video stream
                    var constraints = {
                        audio: false,
                        video: {
                            zoom: true,
                            facingMode: 'environment',
                            // aspectRatio: { ideal: 9/16 }
                        }
                    };
                    //HD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 1920 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1080 };

                    //QHD
                    constraints.video.width = { ideal: 2560 };
                    constraints.video.height = { ideal: 1440 };

                    //4K UHD
                    // constraints.video.width = { ideal: 3840 };
                    // constraints.video.height = { ideal: 2160 }

                    navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia(constraints).then(function(stream) {
                        // Assign the stream to the video element's source object
                        var cameraStream = document.getElementById(vm.shipping.videoModal.stream.id);
                        cameraStream.srcObject = stream;

                        var [track] = stream.getVideoTracks();
                        var capabilities = track.getCapabilities();

                        vm.videoModal.zoom ??= {
                            min: capabilities.zoom.min,
                            max: capabilities.zoom.max,
                            current: track.getSettings().zoom
                        }
                        var zoomLevel = localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel') ?? getZoomLevel(track.getSettings().zoom);

                        track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                        vm.videoModal.track = track;
                        // if (capabilities.zoom) {
                        //     track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: capabilities.zoom.max }] });
                        // }
                    }).catch(function(error) {
                        console.error("Error accessing the camera: ", error);
                    });
                } else {
                    // Fallback for older browsers
                    console.error("Your browser does not support the getUserMedia API.");
                }

                function getZoomLevel(currentZoom) {
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', currentZoom);
                    return currentZoom;
                }
            }

            function zoomOut() {
                // localStorage.setItem("settings", JSON.stringify(userSettings));
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel > vm.videoModal.zoom.min) {
                    zoomLevel -= 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

            function zoomIn() {
                var zoomLevel = Number(localStorage.getItem('zoomLevel'));
                if (zoomLevel < vm.videoModal.zoom.max) {
                    zoomLevel += 100;
                    localStorage.setItem('zoomLevel', zoomLevel);
                    vm.videoModal.track.applyConstraints({ advanced: [{ zoom: zoomLevel }] });
                }
            }

            function loadShip(shipmentRequest) {
                debugger;
                vm.load();
                if (vm.shipping.customer.autoShip) {
                    vm.intervalId = setInterval(function(shipmentRequest) {
                        console.log(shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment)
                        if (shipmentRequest != vm.currentShipment) {
                            clearInterval(vm.intervalId);
                            // if(!(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage ?? '').includes('Invalid Service Option'))
                                vm.ship();
                        }
                    }, 20, shipmentRequest)
                }
            }
        }

        function history() {
            vm.history = {
                searchButton: 'button:contains("Search")',
                reportSelector: '#reports'
            };

            $(document).on('click', vm.history.searchButton, selectReportChange);
            $(document).on('change', vm.history.reportSelector, selectReportChange);

            activate();

            function activate() {
                if (vm.profile.Name != vm.thinClient.adminProfileName) {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = true;

                    let reports = [ 'Default', 'Detailed Report', 'Void Report', 'Summary Report' ];
                    vm.reports = vm.reports.filter(function(report) {
                        report.TemplateHtml = report.TemplateHtml.replace(/<span.*glyphicon-search.*<\/span>/g, '');
                        return reports.includes(report.Name);
                    });
                }
            }

            function selectReportChange(event) {
                if (vm.report?.Name == 'Summary Report') {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = true;
                    vm.history.carrierAcceptTableContainer = {
                        'height': $('.panel-body').height() + 'px',
                        'overflow-y': 'auto'
                    };

                    let payload = {
                        Action: 'summaryReport',
                        Data: {
                            startDate: vm.dtstart.toLocaleDateString('en-CA'),
                            endDate: vm.dtend.toLocaleDateString('en-CA'),
                            sites: getSites()
                        }
                    };
                    let data = { UserContext: undefined, Data: JSON.stringify(payload) };
                    thinClient.httpClient('UserMethod', data).then(function (ret) {
                        debugger;
                        vm.history.carrierAcceptReport = JSON.parse(atob(ret.Data));
                        vm.thinClient.loadData.show();
                    });
                } else {
                    vm.hideButtonExport = false;
                }

                function getSites() {
                    let sites = vm.UserInformation.SiteId ? vm.sites.filter(function(site) { return site.Id == vm.UserInformation.SiteId;}) : vm.sites;
                    return sites.map(function(site) { return { name: site.Name }; });
                }
            }
        }
    }

    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
        
          $(function ()
  {

    {
       
      var chkBox = $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]');

      {
        $(chkBox).click();
        //$('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find($('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Account"]').attr('ng-required', 'account.isRequired()').css('border', '1px solid #ccc'));

// Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function () {
        $('body').on('change', client.shipping.fileInputPaperless, this.vm, paperlessChange);
  
         function paperlessChange(e) {
             var file = e.target.files[0]
             if (file === undefined) {
                e.data.paperless = null;
             }
             else {
                 var reader = new FileReader();
                 reader.readAsDataURL(file);
                 reader.onloadend = function () {
                     e.data.paperless = { fileName: file.name, fileData: this.result.split(',')[1] }
                 }
             }                
         }       
     }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location){
        if(location =="/shipping"){
            // $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] input[name="PostalCode"]', 'keydown', function() {
            //    alert('hello');
            //});
            $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] input[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'keydown', function(event) {
                if(event.which == 13 || event.which == 9)$('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] button[title="Search Addresses"]').click();
            });
            
            $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] input[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'keydown', function(event) {
                if(event.which == 13 || event.which == 9){

        function clickUploadFile() {

                if ($('#fileInputField').val() != '') {
                    showSpinner();

                }

        }

// AddEmailToNotification(event) // returns undefined
    this.AddEmailToNotification = function(event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = GetShipmentEmailAddresses(this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults);
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];

        if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
		//debugger;
		vmTemp = this.vm;
		
		console.log(vmTemp);

		shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].CommodityClass = "CLASS_65";
		//document.getElementById("autoship_checkbox").checked = false;
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = false;   // autoship checkbox

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol = "x";
		}

		// clear Markup Percentage
		$("#custom_markup_id").val("");

		// set dialog values/events
		$('#newOrderNumber').val('');
		$('#newWeight').val('');
		$('#newWeight').keypress(function(e) {
			// enforce weight mask
			if (!String.fromCharCode(e.which).match(/[0-9.]+/g)) {
				return false;
			}
		})
		$('#newBoxType').change(function() {
			if ($(this).find('option:selected').val() !== '') {
				// show dimensions string if box was selected
				let length = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length;
				let width = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width;
				let height = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height;
				let units = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units === 0 ? "IN" : "CM";
				$('#newDimensions').val(length + "x" + width + "x" + height + " " + units);
				
				if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					$('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"').prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
			else {
				$('#newDimensions').val('');
			}
		});
		$('#newDimensions').val('');
		$('#newDimensions').keyup(function(e) {
			let loadButton = $('#newShipmentDialog button[ng-click="vm.load()"');
			if (this.value.trim() === '' && vmTemp.loadValue) {
				loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
			}
			else {
				// enforce dimensions mask if entered LxWxH (IN/CM optional)
				let regEx = /(\d+)x(\d+)x(\d+)( IN| CM)?/
				if (!regEx.test(this.value)) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', true);
				}
				else if (vmTemp.loadValue) {
					loadButton.prop('disabled', false);
				}
			}
		});

		// show Load Shipment dialog and set focus
		if (!$('#newShipmentDialog').is(':visible')) {
			$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('show');
			$('#newShipmentDialog').on('shown.bs.modal', function() {
				$(this).find('[autofocus]').focus();
			});
		}
	};

// this.AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
		//debugger;

		// if ($("#ctl00_cphContent_ship_mode_list").val() == "0")
		// {
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].UserData1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].UserData1;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].ShipperReference;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].ConsigneeReference;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference1;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference1;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference3;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference4;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference5 = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].MiscReference5;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].Description;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommercialInvoiceMethod = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].CommercialInvoiceMethod;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].SaturdayDelivery = shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex - 1].SaturdayDelivery;
		//}

		getWeight(this.vm);
	};

// this.PreLoad(value, shipmentRequest, params) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest, params) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === undefined || shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].BoxType === null) {
			// if box is empty, add custom dimensions from dialog
			let dims = $('#newDimensions').val().trim().split(/x| /);
			if (dims !== null && dims.length >= 3) {
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="length"]').val(dims[0]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="width"]').val(dims[1]).change();
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('input[name="height"]').val(dims[2]).change();
				
				let index = 1;
				if (dims.length === 4) {
					dims[3] = dims[3].toUpperCase();
					index = (dims[3] === 'IN' ? 1 : 2);
				}
				$('form[name="generalForm"]').find('select[name="units"] option:eq(' + index + ')').prop('selected', true);
			}
		}

		let oChk = this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20;		// autoship
		if (oChk === true) {
			params.autoship = oChk;
		}

		$('#newShipmentDialog').modal('hide');
		showLoading(true);
	};

// this.PostLoad(value, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(value, shipmentRequest) {
		debugger;
		let errorMessage = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage;
		
		if (errorMessage === undefined) errorMessage = "";
		if (errorMessage === null) errorMessage = "";

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service !== undefined && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol === "x") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert("No service selected!");
		}
		
		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage === 'validate') {
			//$("#ctl00_cphContent_left_tabs_consignee_tab_consignee_na_ab_ctrl_na_ctrl_validate_addr_btn").click();
			showLoading(false);
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage.substring(0, 4) === "pop:") {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage.substring(4));
			return;
		}

		if (errorMessage !== undefined && errorMessage !== '') {
			showLoading(false);
			alert(errorMessage);
			let errors = ["not found", "already shipped", "too many"];
			if (errors.some(errorText => errorMessage.includes(errorText))) {
				// open Load Shipment dialog
				this.vm.newShipment();
			}
			return;
		}

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country === 'US') {
			this.vm.shipMode = 1;
		} else {
			this.vm.shipMode = 0;
		}

		$("#custom_markup_id").val(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);

		//getWeight();

		if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 !== null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 === 'autoship') {
			this.vm.checkShip();
			return;
		}

		// select all services before rate
		setTimeout(function() {
			// check Select All after delay to allow UI update
			vmTemp.isAllServicesSelected = true;
			vmTemp.selectAllServices();
			vmTemp.rate();
		}, 100);
		
	};

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
		console.log("🚀 [PreShip] Starting PreShip function...");
	    shipmentRequest = vmTemp.currentShipment;
		// Validate shipmentRequest and Packages array
		if (!shipmentRequest || !shipmentRequest.Packages || !Array.isArray(shipmentRequest.Packages)) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			//alert("[PreShip Error] Shipment request is invalid or missing required properties.");
			return;
		}
	
		let validDimensions = [];
	
		console.log(`📦 [PreShip] Processing ${shipmentRequest.Packages.length} package(s)...`);
	
		// Retrieve current package dimensions from vmTemp
		try {
			let currentPackage = vmTemp.currentShipment.Packages[vmTemp.packageIndex];
			if (!currentPackage || !currentPackage.Dimensions) {
				console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] vmTemp.currentShipment package or dimensions not found.");
			} else {
				let dims = currentPackage.Dimensions;
				console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Current Package Dimensions from vmTemp: ${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`);
			}
		} catch (error) {
			console.error("❌ [PreShip Error] Unable to retrieve package dimensions from vmTemp.");
		}
	
		// Loop through all packages to validate their dimensions
		for (let i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
			console.log(`🔍 [PreShip] Checking package at index ${i}...`);
	
			let packageData = shipmentRequest.Packages[i];
	
			if (!packageData) {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} is undefined.`);
				return;
			}
	
			if (!packageData.Dimensions) {
				console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} does not contain 'Dimensions'.`);
				return;
			}
	
			let dims = packageData.Dimensions;
	
			// Ensure all dimension values exist and are valid numbers
			if (dims.Length > 0 && dims.Width > 0 && dims.Height > 0) {
				let dimensionString = `${dims.Length}x${dims.Width}x${dims.Height} 0`; // Always append "0"
	
				// Validate format (three numeric values + "0" at the end)
				let dimParts = dimensionString.split(new RegExp("[x ]"), 4); // Split on 'x' and space
	
				if (dimParts.length === 4 && !isNaN(dimParts[0]) && !isNaN(dimParts[1]) && !isNaN(dimParts[2]) && dimParts[3] === "0") {
					validDimensions.push(dimensionString);
					console.log(`✅ [PreShip] Package ${i} Dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
				} else {
					console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions: ${dimensionString}`);
					//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has incorrectly formatted dimensions.`);
					return;
				}
			} else {
				console.error(`❌ [PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				//alert(`[PreShip Error] Package at index ${i} has invalid dimensions.`);
				return;
			}
		}
	
		// Store only valid dimensions in MiscReference5
		if (validDimensions.length > 0) {
			shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5 = validDimensions.join(", ");
			console.log(`✅ [PreShip] All dimensions successfully stored in MiscReference5: ${shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference5}`);
		} else {
			console.warn("⚠️ [PreShip Warning] No packages had valid dimensions.");
		}
	
		// Retrieve weight and markup values
		userParams.weight = $('div[caption="Weight"]').find('input[name="unitValue_txt"]').val();
		userParams.markup = $("#custom_markup_id").val();
		console.log(`📏 [PreShip] Retrieved weight: ${userParams.weight}, Markup: ${userParams.markup}`);
	
		// Custom code to hide/filter on postship errors - must be started here
		$("<style> .alert-danger { display: none; } </style>").appendTo("head");
		console.log("🚫 [PreShip] Hidden alert-danger elements to prevent UI issues.");
	
		alertInterval = setInterval(function () {
			var errAlert = $('div.alert-danger');
		
			// Filter and show alert
			if (errAlert.length > 0) {
				clearInterval(alertInterval);
				let msg = errAlert.text();
				if (msg.indexOf('-1') === -1 && msg.indexOf('CONNECTSHIP') === -1) {
					errAlert.show();
					console.warn(`⚠️ [PreShip Warning] PostShip Alert Detected: ${msg}`);
				}
			}
		}, 200);
	
		console.log("✅ [PreShip] Function completed successfully.");
	};

// this.PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
		//debugger;
		if (shipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== undefined && shipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.ErrorCode !== 0) {
			showLoading(false);
			alert("Shipping error: " + shipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage);
		}
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20 = false;		// autoship
		$("#custom_markup_id").val("");
/**
		labelInterval = setInterval(function () {
			var labelDialog = $('[uib-modal-window="modal-window"]');
		
			// close label popup if displayed after shipping
			if (labelDialog.length > 0) {
				clearInterval(labelInterval);
				$('[uib-modal-window="modal-window"]').find('.modal-header .row button').click();
			}
		}, 20);
*/
		// clear waiting on alert and dialog intervals
		setTimeout(function() {
			clearInterval(alertInterval);
			clearInterval(labelInterval);
		}, 5000);
	};

// this.AddEmailToNotification(event) // returns undefined
    this.AddEmailToNotification = function (event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = getShipmentEmailAddresses(this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults);
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];

        if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    }

// function dismissAlertDialog() // returns undefined
    function dismissAlertDialog() {
        $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) {
            $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
        });
    }

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns void
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
        
        var customData1 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom1");
        var customData2 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom2");
        var customData3 = PullCustomData(nameaddress.CustomData, "Custom3");
        
        var stName = objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Company;
        
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = customData2 + "~" + stName;
        
        if(customData3=="FC"){
            objVM.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
            nameaddress.Account = customData1;
        }
        
        
        function PullCustomData(consignee, field){
            //alert(JSON.stringify(consignee));
            
            for(var item in consignee){
                if(consignee[item].Key==field)return consignee[item].Value;
            }
        }
    }

// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        appendCSS();
        //getUserContext();
        //getClientProfile()
        dismissAlertDialog();
        //userCustomData = getCustomData(clientProfile.UserInformation.Address)

        if (location === '/') {
            //document.location = '#!/shipping';

            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var h2SystemNotification = $('h2:contains("System Notification")');

                if (h2SystemNotification.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    h2SystemNotification.parent().hide();
                }
            }, 50);


        } else if (location === '/shipping') {
            $('body').delegate('input:checkbox', 'change', singleCheckbox)
            $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', function () {
                $('#consigneeCountryChange').click();
            });

            client.shipping.consignee.searchAddresses.addButtonLabel(' ' + this.vm.translations.Common.SearchAddresses);
            client.shipping.consignee.validateAddress.addButtonLabel(' ' + this.vm.translations.Common.ValidateAddress);
            client.shipping.origin.searchAddresses.addButtonLabel(' ' + this.vm.translations.Common.SearchAddresses);
            client.shipping.origin.validateAddress.addButtonLabel(' ' + this.vm.translations.Common.ValidateAddress);
        }
    }

// this.ConsigneeCountryChange() // returns undefined
    this.ConsigneeCountryChange = function () {
        setInternationalPackaging(this.currentShipment, this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee);
    }

// function singleCheckbox() // returns undefined
    function singleCheckbox() {
        var $checkbox = $(this);
        if ($checkbox.is(':checked') && $checkbox.is('[name]')) {
            // the name of the box is retrieved using the .attr() method
            // as it is assumed and expected to be immutable
            var group = 'input:checkbox[name="' + $checkbox.attr("name") + '"]';

            // the checked state of the group/box on the other hand will change
            // and the current value is retrieved using .prop() method
            $(group).prop('checked', false);
            $checkbox.prop('checked', true);
        }

    }

// function dismissAlertDialog() // returns undefined
    function dismissAlertDialog() {
        $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function(e) {
            $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
        })
    }

// dismiss: $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function () { $('div[role="alert"]:visible').hide(); }) // returns a jQuery object
        dismiss: $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function () { $('div[role="alert"]:visible').hide(); }),

// closealert.on('click', function () { uibalert.hide(); }) // returns a jQuery object
            closealert.on('click', function () { uibalert.hide(); })

// singleCheckbox() // returns undefined
    function singleCheckbox() {
        var $checkbox = $(this);
        if ($checkbox.is(':checked') && $checkbox.is('[name]')) {
            // the name of the box is retrieved using the .attr() method
            // as it is assumed and expected to be immutable
            var group = 'input:checkbox[name="' + $checkbox.attr("name") + '"]';

            // the checked state of the group/box on the other hand will change
            // and the current value is retrieved using .prop() method
            $(group).prop('checked', false);
            $checkbox.prop('checked', true);
        }

    }

// dismissAlertDialog() // returns undefined

            $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
        })
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
  this.PageLoaded = function(location)

      {

        $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"]').delegate('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'blur', function(e)
        {
          $('div[ng-hide="vm.profile.FieldOptions.Consignee.IsHidden"] button[ng-click="search(nameaddress)"]').trigger('click');
        });
      });
    }

    if (location == '/batchmanager')
    {
      $(document).ready(function()
      {
        $.globalEval('var userContext;');

        $('#batchUpdateTabs').delegate('li', 'click', function(e)
        {
          e.preventDefault();
          e.stopImmediatePropagation();
          e.stopPropagation();

          var i = $(this).attr('index');
          UIMethods.SwitchToTab(i);
        });

        $('body').delegate('input[required]', 'keydown', function(e)
        {
          $(this).removeClass('has-error');
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkEditBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.EditThisBatch(this);
        });

        $('body').delegate('#checkboxthirdparty', 'click', function(e)
        {

        $('body').delegate('#buttonBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.UpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonCancelBulkUpdateBatch', 'click', function(e)
        {
          BatchClass.CancelUpdateCurrentBatch();
        });

      });
    }
  }

// ClientBusinessRules() // returns void
function ClientBusinessRules ()
{
  this.PageLoaded = function (location)
  {
    //console.log(this.vm.UserInformation);
    SessionData.SetCurrentUserContext(this.vm.UserInformation);

    if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping")
    {
      var checkExist = setInterval(function ()
      {

        if (($) && ($('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').find('option')))
        {
          /* Stop the timer. */
          clearInterval(checkExist);

        //   SessionData.SetServerDebugMode(true);
        //   Logger.Log({Source: 'PageLoad()', Message: 'Test of CBR page load'});

        }

      }, 100);
    }
  }

  this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse)
  {
    /* Implicitly set the MiscReference7 here as sometimes the view model won't update in time. */
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val();
    PackVerify.ClosePackVerifyDialog();
  }

  this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
      
      console.log(shipmentRequest);

    /* If there is nothing on the scale, this won't return a value. */
    $('[ng-click="vm.getWeight()"]').trigger('click').promise().done(function ()
    {

      var checkExist = setInterval(function ()
      {

        /* Wait until the load comes back and populates the Country field. */
        if ($('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]').prop('selectedIndex') > 1)
        {

          /* Stop the timer. */
          clearInterval(checkExist);

          /* Don Beal (dbeal@ups.com) - 2021-12-09 */
          /* Commented as the attribute list is not needed with PackVerify. */

          // /* Deal with consolidated orders if we have them.  The function that creates this attr on the load input is in the Shipping template. */
          // /* I use the attribute as a lot of the form values reset once the load is completed. */
          // /* Set the Misc Ref 7 to the orderList that was passed from the calling function. */
          // if ($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').attr('orderList') && $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').attr('orderList').length > 0)
          // {
          //   $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').attr('orderList'));
          //   $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').attr('orderList'));

          //   /* Get rid of the attributes now. */
          //   $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').attr('orderList', '');
          // }

          if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper == 'FSCO7F4175')
          {
            /* Set the default box type to 'BAG 1'.  The multiple props and attr are for older browsers. */
            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"] > option[label="SAMPLE BAG 1"]').prop({ 'selected': 'true', 'selected': true }).attr('selected', 'selected').trigger('change');
          }

          /* Don Beal (dbeal@ups.com) - 2021-12-09 */
          /* Commented as this was not enabled in production. */

          // /* Validate the address, this is only needed for 7F4175 and 8942X4 */
          // var CountryCodeString = $('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]').val();
          // if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper == 'FSCO7F4175' || shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper == 'FSCO8942X4' && CountryCodeString == "string:US")
          // {
          //   //$('[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]').find('[ng-click="validate(nameaddress)"]').trigger('click');
          // }

          /* Change the service to UPS Ground if the package is over 1lb and using USPS FC */
          CheckWeightAndService($('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val());

          /* After loading an order show the Pack Verify dialog and fill out the columns. */
          HideLoader();
          PackVerify.ShowPackVerifyDialog(JSON.parse(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData5), shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference);

        }

      }, 150);
    });

  }

  this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest)
  {
      console.log(this.vm);
    SessionData.SetCurrentViewModel(this.vm);
    $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').focus();
  }

  // /* This will throw an exception, make sure to remove from PROD code. */
  // /* Use this to test the logging of client data to the server by assigning it to a button click or some other event. */
  // function TestServerLogging ()
  // {
  //   var i = 1;
  //   try
  //   {
  //     i.replace("-", "");
  //   }
  //   catch (error)
  //   {
  //     Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: error });
  //   }
