  function CheckWeightAndService (weightVal)
  {
    // /* Once the button is clicked, start a timer and wait for the weight to populate. */
    // /* If the weight is over 1 pound, switch the service from USPS FC to UPS Ground. */
    if ((weightVal > 1) && ($('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').find('option:selected').val() == "CONNECTSHIP_ENDICIA.USPS.FIRST"))
    {

      /* Deselect any currently selected options. */
      $('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').val([]).scrollTop(10);

      /* Select the ground option. */
      $('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"] > option[value="CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.GND"]')
        .prop({ 'selected': 'true', 'selected': true })
        .attr('selected', 'selected')
        .trigger('change').promise().done(function ()
        {

        });
    }
  }

  /* This function is used to get the name of a function during error handling when option strict is true. */
  function GetCallingFunctionName ()
  {
    try
    {
      throw new Error();
    }
    catch (e)
    {
      try
      {
        return e.stack.split('at ')[3].split(' ')[0] + '()';
      }
      catch (e)
      {
        return '';
      }
    }
  }

  function ShowLoader ()
  {
    $('div.loading').removeClass('ng-hide').addClass('ng-show');
  }

  function HideLoader ()
  {
    $('div.loading').removeClass('ng-show').addClass('ng-hide');
  }

  function ShowOverlay ()
  {
    $('div.overlay').show();
  }

  function HideOverlay ()
  {
    $('div.overlay').hide();
  }

  /* Don Beal (dbeal@ups.com) 2021-11-03 */
  /* This needs to be at the bottom of the CSBR so it runs after everything else. */
  /* All event delegates should be set within the $(document).ready section */
  $(document).ready(function ()
  {
    try
    {
      /* All global CBR declarations should go here using $.globalEval(). */

      /* I moved all global vars into the classes using the 'let' construct so they are only exposed in that class and not leaked during user sessions. */
      /* If the SessionData vars are needed during debugging, add the following to the this.PageLoaded function. */
      /* this.vm.SessionData = SessionData; */
      /* sessionData = this.vm.SessionData; */
      /* AND */
      /* Add the following line to $(document).ready */
      /* $.globalEval('var sessionData;'); */

      /* Global ajax event handlers. */
      $.ajaxSetup({ global: true });

      $(document).ajaxStart(function (event, jqXHR, ajaxSettings)
      {
        ShowLoader();
      });

      $(document).ajaxStop(function ()
      {
        HideLoader();
      });

      $(document).ajaxComplete(function ()
      {
        HideLoader();
      });
      /* End global ajax event handlers. */

      /* Hide any error alerts when another element has focus. */
      $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) { $('div.alert').hide(); });

      $(document).delegate('body', 'keydown', function (e)
      {
        /* If the user presses F12, close the dialog and ship the package. */
        var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
        if (keycode == 123 && $('#divModalPackVerify').is(':visible'))
        {
          PackVerify.ClosePackVerifyDialog();
        }
      });

      $('body').delegate('#inputScanCutTicket', 'keydown', function (e)
      {
        var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
        if (keycode == 13)
        {
          PackVerify.ParseCutTicket($(this).val());
          /* Clear out the value of the text box. */
          $(this).val([]);
        }
      });

      $('body').delegate('#textOrderNumber', 'keyup', function (e)
      {
        var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
        if (keycode == 13 | keycode == 9)
        {
          PackVerify.AddOrderNumbersToList();
        }
      });

      /* The two following delegates do the same thing, one reacts to the event when the 'Enter' key is pressed while the load value is populated, the other intercepts the 'Load' button click. */
      /* The loader will not show as part of the global ajax handlers as this event called from within the Angular controller. */
      $('body').delegate('#inputLoadValue', 'keydown', function (e)
      {
        var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
        if (keycode == 13)
        {
          ShowLoader();
        }
      });

      $('body').delegate('input[type=button][ng-click="vm.load()"]', 'click', function (e)
      {
        ShowLoader();
      });

      /* If the user clicks on an alert, hide the loader and the alert. */
      $('body').delegate('div.alert', 'click mousedown', function ()
      {
        HideLoader();
        $(this).hide();
      });

      /* Remove .hasCustomError classes from any controls. */
      $('body').delegate('.form-control', 'keydown mousedown', function (e)
      {
        $(this).removeClass('hasCustomError');
      });

      $('body').delegate('#buttonVerifyPacking', 'click', function (e)
      {
        PackVerify.ClosePackVerifyDialog();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#buttonAddOrderNumbers', 'click', function (e)
      {
        PackVerify.AddOrderNumbersToList();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#divCurrentContainer span.glyphicon-minus', 'click', function (e)
      {
        PackVerify.RemoveCurrentBoxFromShipment();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#divCurrentContainer span.glyphicon-plus', 'click', function (e)
      {
        PackVerify.AddNewBoxToCurrentShipment();
      });

      $('body').delegate('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom span.glyphicon-minus', 'click', function (e)
      {
        PackVerify.RemoveThisTableRow(this);
      });

      $('body').delegate('span.glyphicon.get-weight', 'click', function (e)
      {
        PackVerify.GetCurrentWeightFromScale();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#divConsolidatedOrderList span.glyphicon-duplicate', 'click', function (e)
      {
        PackVerify.ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#buttonSaveConsolidatedOrders', 'click', function (e)
      {
        PackVerify.SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#buttonShipAfterVerify', 'click', function (e)
      {
        //$('#divModalPackVerify').hide();
        PackVerify.ClosePackVerifyDialog();
        $('input[type=button][ng-click="vm.checkShip()"]').first().click();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#buttonPackVerifyNextContainer', 'click', function (e)
      {
        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        PackVerify.ShowContainerTable('next');

        /* Check button status. */
        $(this).attr('disabled', $('button[type=button][ng-click="vm.nextPackage();"]').attr('disabled'));
        $('#buttonPackVerifyPreviousContainer').attr('disabled', $('button[type=button][ng-click="vm.previousPackage();"]').attr('disabled'));
      });

      $('body').delegate('#buttonPackVerifyPreviousContainer', 'click', function (e)
      {
        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
        e.preventDefault();
        e.stopPropagation();
        PackVerify.ShowContainerTable('prev');

        /* Check button status. */
        $(this).attr('disabled', $('button[type=button][ng-click="vm.nextPackage();"]').attr('disabled'));
        $('#buttonPackVerifyNextContainer').attr('disabled', $('button[type=button][ng-click="vm.nextPackage();"]').attr('disabled'));
      });

      $('body').delegate('span.add-box-item', 'click', function (e)
      {
        try
        {
          var descString = $(this).closest('tr').find('td:eq(0)').text();
          var qtyInt = $(this).closest('tr').find('td:eq(3)').text();
          var singleArray = descString.split(" ", 1);

          var parseString = singleArray[0] + ' ' + qtyInt;

          PackVerify.ParseCutTicket(parseString);
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: error });
        }
      });

      $('body').delegate('#selectClonedBoxTypes', 'change', function (e)
      {
        /* Reset the border color, in case it was red from a previous error. */
        $(this).css('border-color', '#ccc');

        if ($(this).prop('selectedIndex') === 0)
        {
          $('span.dim-length').text('0');
          $('span.dim-height').text('0');
          $('span.dim-width').text('0');
          $('span.dim-weight').text('0');
          return false;
        }

        var currentSel = $(this).prop('selectedIndex');
        $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"]').prop('selectedIndex', currentSel).trigger('click').trigger('change');

        /* A new box has been selected, get the weight from the scale. */
        PackVerify.GetCurrentWeightFromScale();

        /* Create the data object of the visible container to hold the select value. */
        var containerBoxData = {};
        containerBoxData.SelectedIndex = $(this).find('option:selected').index();
        containerBoxData.SelectedText = $(this).find('option:selected').text();

        var currentContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:visible');
        $(currentContainer).data(containerBoxData);

        /* The vals could be the same, maybe clear out the val first, wait until it automatically changes, then run our function. */
        var checkExist = setInterval(function ()
        {
          if ($('input[type="text"][name="length"]').first().val().length > 0)
          {
            /* Stop the timer. */
            clearInterval(checkExist);
            var l = $('input[type="text"][name="length"]').first().val();
            var h = $('input[type="text"][name="height"]').first().val();
            var w = $('input[type="text"][name="width"]').first().val();

            if ($('#divModalPackVerify').is(':visible'))
            {
              $('span.dim-length').text(l);
              $('span.dim-height').text(h);
              $('span.dim-width').text(w);
            }
          }

        }, 100);

        PackVerify.CheckForCompletedPacking();

        $('#inputScanCutTicket').focus();
      });

      /*
        The service select box will present in non-alphabetical order so sort it accordingly.
        Need to wait until the services are populated to do this so add an interval.
        Make sure this stays at the BOTTOM of the $(document).ready function.

        Once the sort is completed the callback will focus the cursor on the 'Load' input and the default shipper will be selected.
      */
      var checkExist = setInterval(function ()
      {
        if ($('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').find('option').length > 0)
        {
          /* Stop the timer. */
          clearInterval(checkExist);

          var selServiceOptions = $('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').find('option');

          selServiceOptions.detach().sort(function (a, b)
          {
            return ($(a).text() > $(b).text()) ? 1 : (($(a).text() < $(b).text()) ? -1 : 0);
          });

          selServiceOptions.appendTo('select[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').promise().done(function (e)
          {
            /* The sorting is done, now select the default shipper and set the focus to the Load input box. */
            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').find('option:eq(1)').prop(
              {
                'selected': 'selected',
                'selected': true
              }).change();

            /* Now set the focus to the 'Load' input box and select the first shipper in the list. */
            $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.loadValue"]').focus();
            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').find('option:eq(1)').prop({ 'selected': 'selected', 'selected': true }).change();
          });
        }

      }, 100);

    }
    catch (error)
    {
      Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: error });
    }
  }); /* end $(document).ready(function () */

  var PackVerify = (function ()
  {
    /* Private methods and variables, accessible only to the PackVerify class. */
    /* Using 'let var = value;' here will be available to all functions in the class, as will 'var v = value;'. */
    /* NOTE:  If the functions have return values, they MUST be called with the class identifier, ie PackVerify.FunctionName */

    function UpdateItemCounts ()
    {
      var itemCount = ($('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:visible').find('tr:visible').not('.empty-table').length - 1);
      $('span.box-pkg-count').text(itemCount);

      var unpackedCount = ($('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails').find('tr.not-packed, tr.not-complete').length);
      $('span.unpacked-item-count').text(unpackedCount);

      $('#inputScanCutTicket').focus();
    }

    function UpdateContainerCounts ()
    {
      var totalContainers = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom').length;
      $('span.total-container-count').text(totalContainers);

      /* Get the index of the visible table.table-custom. */
      var currentContainer = ($('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:visible').index() + 1);
      $('span.current-container-index').text(currentContainer);

      UpdateItemCounts();
    }

    function UpdateCommodities (PackageIndex)
    {
      /* Click the active tab, just to refresh the commodities.  This will only work on the first commodity added. */
      $('div.ui-tab-container > div.ng-isolate-scope > ul > li.active > a').click();

      if ($('#goods').find('div.ng-table-counts.btn-group:eq(' + PackageIndex + ')').length > 0)
      {
        /* Clicking the button below refreshes the commodities list in the UI. */
        /* Find the first button that does not have the .active class. */
        $('#goods').find('div.ng-table-counts.btn-group').find('button:not(.active):first').click();
      }
    }

    function ResetDivElements (CloseDialog)
    {
      /* Remove the items from the incoming orders table. */
      $('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails').find('tr:gt(0)').remove();

      $('#tablePackVerifyCutTicketScanResults').find('tr:gt(1)').remove();
      $('#tablePackVerifyCutTicketScanResults').find('tr.empty-table').show();

      $('span.order-number-list').text('');
      $('span.pack-verify-instructions-detail').text('');

      $('#inputScanCutTicket').val([]);

      $('#divPackVerifyButtonGroup').find('input[type=button]').prop('disabled', 'disabled');

      UpdateContainerCounts();

      if (CloseDialog) { $('#divModalPackVerify').hide(); }
    }

    function GetRandomNumber (DigitCount)
    {
      return Math.floor(Math.pow(10, (DigitCount - 1)) + Math.random() * 9 * Math.pow(10, (DigitCount - 1)));
    }

    function GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement (sVal)
    {
      switch (sVal.toUpperCase())
      {
        case "EACH":
          return "EA";
        case "YARDS":
        case "YARD":
          return "YD";
        case "METER":
          return "M";
        case "SF":
          return "SFT";
        case "PAIR":
          return "PR";
        case "SR":
          return "ROL";
        default:
          return sVal;
      }
    }

    function CheckForBasicErrors ()
    {
      var i = 0;
      /* Sometimes the weight OR service won't come across from the api, check for valid values and paint the invalid inputs red. */
      var weightInput = $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]');
      if (weightInput.val() == "") { $(weightInput).addClass('hasCustomError'); i += 1; }

      return i;
    }

    /* Public methods (accessible to entire CBR, prefixed with PackVerify.function). */
    /* The opening brace MUST be on the same line as the return statement. */
    /* With the exception of the last function in the return section, all functions need to have a comma ',' after the closing brace. */
    /* NOTE:  If the functions have returns, they MUST be called with the class identifier, ie PackVerify.FunctionName */
    return {

      ShowErrorAlert: function (ErrorMessage)
      {
        $('#divCustomAlert div.alert-message').text(ErrorMessage).closest('div.alert').show();
      },

      AddCommoditiesToPackage: function (packageIndex, commodityContent)
      {
        /* The commodityContent object has a number of items that can't be pushed to the shipmentRequest array. */
        /* Create a new object just with the items needed in the shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityContents array. */
        try
        {
          var shipmentRequest = SessionData.GetCurrentViewModel().currentShipment;

          if (!shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityContents)
          {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityContents = [];
          }
          shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityContents.push(commodityContent);

          UpdateCommodities(packageIndex);

          /* If there are no commodities yet, the buttons will not exist to click. */
          /* As a workaround, trigger the .change event for the selectClonedBoxTypes select box.  This will trigger an update of the view model, and the commodities list. */
          /* Need to find a way to trigger the same view model update on the nth package in the shipment. */



          // if ($('#goods').find('div.ng-table-counts.btn-group:eq(' + packageIndex + ')').length === 0)
          // {
          //   console.log(packageIndex);
          //   console.log('No button group found.  No commodites loaded.');
          //   $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').trigger('change');
          // }
          // else
          // {
          //   /* Clicking the button below refreshes the commodities list in the UI. */
          //   /* Find the first button that does not have the .active class. */
          //   console.log('Button group found.  Commodities loaded');
          //   $('#goods').find('div.ng-table-counts.btn-group').find('button:not(.active):first').click();
          // }
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'AddCommoditiesToPackage()', Error: error});
        }
      }, /* end AddCommoditiesToPackage */

      RemoveCommoditiesFromPackage: function (packageIndex, commodityContent)
      {
        try
        {
          var shipmentRequest = SessionData.GetCurrentViewModel().currentShipment;

          if (!shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityContents)
          {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityContents = [];
          }
          shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CommodityContents.pop(commodityContent);

          /* Update the commodities by clicking on the active tab. */
          //$('div.ui-tab-container > div.ng-isolate-scope > ul > li.active > a').click();
          UpdateCommodities(packageIndex);
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'RemoveCommoditiesFromPackage()', Error: error });
        }
      },

      ShowPackVerifyDialog: function (CommodityContents, ShipperReference)
      {
        /* Delete and re-create the individual container tables.
          <table class="table-custom" id="tablePackVerifyCutTicketScanResults">
            <tbody>
              <tr>
                <th>Order #</th>
                <th>Item #</th>
                <th>Qty</th>
                <th>Total</th>
                <th style="width: 32px;"></th>
              </tr>
              <tr class="empty-table">
                <td colspan="6" style="text-align: center;">No items placed in container.</td>
              </tr>
            </tbody>
          </table>
        */
        try
        {
          /* Get rid of any previous container tables, then create a new empty one. */
          /* This is more efficient than looking for possible existing table(s) and dealing with them. */
          $('div.table-box-contents').find('table').remove().promise().done(function (e)
          {
            var tableResults = $('<table />').addClass('table-custom').attr('id', 'tablePackVerifyCutTicketScanResults');

            $(tableResults).append($('<tr />')
              .append($('<th />').text('Order #'))
              .append($('<th />').text('Item #'))
              .append($('<th />').text('Qty'))
              .append($('<th />').text('Total'))
              .append($('<th />').css('width', '32px')));

            $(tableResults).append($('<tr />').addClass('empty-table')
              .append($('<td />')
                .attr('colspan', '6')
                .css('text-align', 'center')
                .text('No items placed in container.')));

            $('div.table-box-contents').append($(tableResults));

          });

          $('span.total-container-count').text('1');
          $('span.current-container-index').text('1');
          $('span.box-pkg-count').text('0');

          $('#divModalPackVerify').fadeIn(200).promise().done(function ()
          {
            // $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"]', 'change', function (e)
            // {
            //   $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').first().prop('selectedIndex', $(this).prop('selectedIndex'));
            //   $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').first().trigger('change').trigger('click');
            // });

            var i = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"]').prop('selectedIndex');

            $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').prop('selectedIndex', i).trigger('change');
            $('span.order-number-list').text(ShipperReference);

            ShowOverlay();

            PackVerify.AddCommoditiesToTable(CommodityContents);

            $('#inputScanCutTicket').focus();

          });
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: error, Data: CommodityContents });
          HideOverlay();
        }
      },

      /* This is called when the user clicks the 'Done' button on the Pack Verify dialog. */
      ClosePackVerifyDialog: function ()
      {
        /* Need to reset all the elements on the page. */
        ResetDivElements(true);
        HideOverlay();
      },

      AddAllItemsToCurrentBox: function ()
      {
        var tableRows = $('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails').find('tr.not-packed');

        $(tableRows).each(function (e)
        {
          AddRowItemToCurrentBox($(this));
        });
      },

      AddNewBoxToCurrentShipment: function ()
      {
        try
        {
          /* No box type selected, return out. */
          if ($('#selectClonedBoxTypes').prop('selectedIndex') === 0)
          {
            $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').css('border-color', 'crimson');
            return false;
          }

          /* Trigger the button on the shipping screen. */
          $('#buttonAddPackageToShipment').first().click();

          //need to clone the tablePackVerifyCutTicketScanResults object, fill it with details, append it to table-box-contents
          var newTable = $('<table />').addClass('table-custom').css('display', 'none');

          $(newTable).append($('<tr />')
            .append($('<th />').text('Order #'))
            .append($('<th />').text('Item #'))
            .append($('<th />').text('Qty'))
            .append($('<th />').text('Total'))
            .append($('<th />').css('width', '32px')));

          $(newTable).append($('<tr />').addClass('empty-table')
            .append($('<td />')
              .attr('colspan', '6')
              .css('text-align', 'center')
              .text('No items placed in container.')));

          /* Hide any visible tables, then show the new one. */
          $('div.table-box-contents').find('table.table-custom').hide();
          $('div.table-box-contents').append($(newTable).fadeIn().show());

          /* Reset the box type select element. */
          $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').prop('selectedIndex', 0).trigger('change');

          UpdateContainerCounts();
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: error });
        }
      },

      ParseCutTicket: function (inVal)
      {
        var splitArray = inVal.split(" ", 2);
        var itemNumber = splitArray[0];
        var itemQuantity = splitArray[1];
        var remainingQuantity, shippedQuantity;
        var matchingArray;

        try
        {
          /* Now find the table row that corresponds to the item number passed into the function. */
          var rowsArray = $('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails').find('tr.not-packed, tr.not-complete');

          matchingArray = $.grep(rowsArray, function (pVal, pIndex)
          {
            remainingQuantity = parseFloat($(pVal).find('td:eq(3)').text());
            shippedQuantity = parseFloat($(pVal).find('td:eq(2)').text());
            return (($(pVal).text().split(" ")[0] == itemNumber) && (itemQuantity == remainingQuantity));
          })[0];

          /* The matchingArray will contain rows that match the item needed with the quantity needed. */
          /* If the array is empty, find rows that have enough material to use. */
          if ($.isEmptyObject(matchingArray))
          {
            matchingArray = $.grep(rowsArray, function (pVal, pIndex)
            {
              remainingQuantity = parseFloat($(pVal).find('td:eq(3)').text());
              shippedQuantity = parseFloat($(pVal).find('td:eq(2)').text());
              return (($(pVal).text().split(" ")[0] == itemNumber) && (itemQuantity < remainingQuantity));
            })[0];
          }

          /* If the matchingArray is still empty, then the user tried to scan something into the box that wasn't part of the order.  Raise an error. */
          if ($.isEmptyObject(matchingArray))
          {
            this.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR: Item ' + itemNumber + ' not found within currently loaded order(s).');
            return false;
          }

          $(matchingArray).data().ScanQuantity = itemQuantity;
          $(matchingArray).data().ItemNumber = itemNumber;

          this.AddRowItemToCurrentBox(matchingArray);
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'ParseCutTicket()', Error: error });
        }
      },

      GetOrderInformationFromCustomer: function (OrderList, CallBack)
      {
        var dataObject = {
          ServerMethod: 'GetOrderInformation',
          OrderList: OrderList
        };

        var ajaxObject = {
          UserContext: SessionData.GetCurrentUserContext(),
          Data: JSON.stringify(dataObject)
        };

        var ajaxRequest = $.ajax(
        {
          url: 'api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
          method: 'POST',
          contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
          dataType: 'json',
          data: ajaxObject
        });

        ajaxRequest.done(function (data)
        {
          var jsonData = JSON.parse(data.Data);

          for (var x = 0; x < jsonData.length; x++)
          {
            if (PackVerify.CheckForMatchingConsignee(jsonData[x]) === true)
            {
              PackVerify.AddCommoditiesToTable(jsonData[x].Details);
              PackVerify.UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(jsonData[x].Header.Order_Number);
            }
            else
            {
              /* Add a note to the footer of the dialog. */
              $('#spanPackVerifyFooter').text('Could not add commodities for order ' + jsonData[x].Header.Order_Number);
            }
          }
        });

        ajaxRequest.fail(function (jqXHR, textStatus)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: { name: 'AjaxError', message: jqXHR.ResponseText } });
        });

        ajaxRequest.always(function (jqXHR, textStatus, jqXHRError)
        {
          if (CallBack && typeof (CallBack) == "function")
          {
            CallBack();
          }
        });
      },

      AddCommoditiesToTable: function (CommodityContents)
      {
        /* Incoming CommodityContents Structure - ARRAY. */
        /*
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY": 2.0,
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY_UNIT_MEASURE": "EACH",
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_UNIT_VALUE": 0.01,
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_PRODUCT_CODE": "MS66184",
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_ORIGIN_COUNTRY": "US",
          "Order_Number": "50980336.4",
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_DESCRIPTION": "DONT FRET",
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_COMMENTS": null,
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_TARRIFFCODE1": null,
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_TARRIFCODE2": "",
          "COMMODITY_CONTENTS_AVERAGEWEIGHT": 0.0
        */
        try
        {
          for (var x = 0; x < CommodityContents.length; x++)
          {
            /* Map the CommodityContent object here that will be used on the server.  By matching the structure here, hoping to push it straight to the viewmodel without any translation. */
            var CommodityObject = {
              UnitWeight: { Amount: "1" },
              Quantity: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY,
              ProductCode: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_PRODUCT_CODE,
              UnitValue: { Amount: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_UNIT_VALUE, Currency: 'USD' },
              QuantityUnitMeasure: GetTranslatedUnitOfMeasurement(CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY_UNIT_MEASURE),
              Description: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_DESCRIPTION,
              OriginCountry: (CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_ORIGIN_COUNTRY.length > 0 ? CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_ORIGIN_COUNTRY : 'US'),
              ConsigneePostalCode: (CommodityContents[x].CONSIGNEE_POSTALCODE ? CommodityContents[x].CONSIGNEE_POSTALCODE.substring(0, 5) : null),
              EntryId: GetRandomNumber(8),
              OrderNumber: CommodityContents[x].Order_Number,
              HarmonizedCode: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_TARRIFFCODE1,
              HarmonizedCode2: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_TARRIFCODE2,
              AverageWeight: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_AVERAGEWEIGHT,
              UserData1: CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_COMMENTS
            };

            $('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails')
              .append($('<tr />').addClass('not-packed').attr('title', 'Order Number: ' + CommodityObject.OrderNumber)
                .append($('<td />').text(CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_PRODUCT_CODE + ' ' + CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_DESCRIPTION))
                .append($('<td />').text(CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY))
                .append($('<td />').text(0))
                .append($('<td />').text(CommodityContents[x].COMMODITY_CONTENTS_QUANTITY))
                .append($('<td />').append('<span class="glyphicon glyphicon-plus trigger-icon add-box-item" title="Add this item to the current box." style="color: green;"></span>'))
                .data(CommodityObject))
              .promise().done(function ()
              {
                UpdateItemCounts();
                HideLoader();
              })
          }
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'AddCommoditiesToTable()', Error: error, Data: CommodityContents });
        }
      },

      CheckForMatchingConsignee: function (CustomerOrderObject)
      {
        try
        {
          var con = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]');
          var a = {
            conCompany: $(con).find('input[name="company"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conAddress1: $(con).find('input[name="address1"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: $(con).find('input[name="city"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: $(con).find('input[name="stateProvince"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: $(con).find('input[name="postalCode"]').val().trim().substring(0, 5).toUpperCase()
          };

          var hdr = CustomerOrderObject.Header;
          var b = {
            conCompany: hdr.CONSIGNEE_COMPANY.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conAddress1: hdr.CONSIGNEE_ADDRESS_LINE_1.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: hdr.CONSIGNEE_CITY.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: hdr.CONSIGNEE_STATEPROVINCE.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: hdr.CONSIGNEE_POSTALCODE.trim().substring(0, 5).toUpperCase()
          };

          if (JSON.stringify(a) != JSON.stringify(b))
          {
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + hdr.SHIPPER_REFERENCE + '. Primary order data to follow.', Data: a });
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + hdr.SHIPPER_REFERENCE + '. Subsequent order data to follow.', Data: b });
          }

          /* Quick comparison to see if the strings match. */
          return (JSON.stringify(a) == JSON.stringify(b));
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Error: error });
        }
      },

      CheckForCompletedPacking: function ()
      {
        /* Enable the 'Done' button if the order is completely packed. */
        if ($('#selectClonedBoxTypes').prop('selectedIndex') === 0)
        {
          $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').css('border-color', 'crimson');
        }

        if (($('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails').find('tr.not-packed, tr.not-complete').length == 0) && ($('#selectClonedBoxTypes').prop('selectedIndex') > 0))
        {
          $('#divPackVerifyButtonGroup').find('input[type=button]').prop('disabled', false);
        }
      },

      GetCurrentWeightFromScale: function ()
      {
        var w;

        if ($('input[type=button][ng-click="vm.getWeight()"]').attr('disabled') === 'disabled')
        {
          w = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val();
          $('span.dim-val.dim-weight').text(w);
        }
        else
        {
          $('input[type=button][ng-click="vm.getWeight()"]').click(function ()
          {
            w = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val();
            $('span.dim-val.dim-weight').text(w);
          });
        }
      },

      /* Triggered when the user clicks on the '+' icon within the order list.  Add all items in the row to the current box. */
      AddRowItemToCurrentBox: function (triggerElement)
      {
        try
        {
          var tableRow = $(triggerElement).closest('tr');
          var commodityContent = $(tableRow).data();

          /* No box type selected, paint the border red. */
          // if ($('#selectClonedBoxTypes').prop('selectedIndex') === 0)
          // {
          //   $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').css('border-color', 'crimson');
          // }

          /* This adds the commodities to the 'Goods' tab. */
          var packageIndex = $('span.current-container-index').text();
          packageIndex -= 1;
          this.AddCommoditiesToPackage(packageIndex, commodityContent);

          var newRow = $('<tr />').css('display', 'none');
          var itemDescText = $(tableRow).find('td:eq(0)').text();
          var itemNumber = itemDescText.split(' ')[0];
          var tableCurrent = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:visible');

          var trData = {};
          trData.OrderNumber = commodityContent.OrderNumber;
          trData.ItemNumber = itemNumber;
          trData.ItemDescription = itemDescText;
          trData.StartVal = parseFloat($(tableRow).find('td:eq(1)').text());
          trData.ShippedVal = parseFloat(commodityContent.ScanQuantity);
          trData.RemainingVal = parseFloat(trData.StartVal - trData.ShippedVal);
          trData.TotalVal = trData.ShippedVal;

          /* For the total value, find each entry with the same item# and total the values and add the shipped value. */
          $(tableCurrent).find('tr:gt(0)').find('td:eq(1)').each(function (e)
          {
            if ($(this).text() == trData.ItemNumber)
            {
              trData.TotalVal += parseFloat($(this).closest('tr').find('td:eq(2)').text());
            }
          });

          /* Both html tables will have data objects on the tr's. */
          /* Make the .EntryId element inside each tr data() object equal so it serves as a key between the two tables. */
          trData.EntryId = $(tableRow).data().EntryId;

          $(newRow).append($('<td />').text(commodityContent.OrderNumber))
            .append($('<td />').text(itemNumber))
            .append($('<td />').text(trData.ShippedVal))
            .append($('<td />').text(trData.TotalVal))
            .append($('<td />').append('<span class="glyphicon glyphicon-minus trigger-icon" title="Remove this item from the current box." style="color: crimson;"></span>'))
            .data(trData);

          /* If the destination table (container) is empty, get rid of the single '.empty-table' row. */
          // if ($('tr.empty-table').is(':visible'))
          // {
            $('tr.empty-table').fadeOut().promise().done(function ()
            {
              $(tableCurrent).append($(newRow).fadeIn().show()).promise().done(function (e) { UpdateItemCounts(); });
            });
          // }
          // else
          // {
          //   $(tableCurrent).append($(newRow).fadeIn().show());
          // }

          /* Now update the classes and amounts from the incoming order data (table on left side of screen). */
          /* We can link the source and destination order by using the .EntryKey data() element. */

          /* Update the shipped quantity. */
          var previouslyShipped = parseFloat($(tableRow).find('td:eq(2)').text());

          var a, b;
          a = parseFloat(commodityContent.ScanQuantity) + parseFloat(previouslyShipped);
          b = parseFloat(trData.StartVal) - a;

          $(tableRow).find('td:eq(2)').text(a);
          $(tableRow).find('td:eq(3)').text(b);

          var trCount = ($('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails').find('tr').length - 1);

          /* Update the shipped amount, change the color to green. */
          /* Set Shipped value to the value of the 2nd td. */
          if ($(tableRow).find('td:eq(3)').text() > 0)
          {
            $(tableRow).removeClass('not-packed').addClass('not-complete');

            // /* If there is only a single row then change the class and return. */
            // if (trCount > 1)
            // {
            //   var insertTargetRow = $(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr.packed').first();
            //   if (insertTargetRow.length === 0)
            //   {
            //     insertTargetRow = $(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr.not-packed').last();
            //     //$(tableRow).detach().insertAfter(insertTargetRow);
            //   }
            //   else
            //   {
            //     //$(tableRow).detach().insertBefore(insertTargetRow);
            //   }
            // }
          }
          else
          {
            $(tableRow).removeClass('not-complete not-packed').addClass('packed').promise().done(function () { UpdateItemCounts(); });
            /* Change the icon, don't allow a click. */
            $(tableRow).find('td:eq(4) > span').removeClass('glyphicon-plus add-box-item').addClass('glyphicon-ban-circle').css('color', 'crimson').attr({ 'title': '' });

            // if (trCount > 1)
            // {
            //   /* Now move the row we just added to the box to the end of the list. */
            //   var lastRow = $(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr').last();
            //   //$(tableRow).detach().insertAfter(lastRow);
            // }
          }

          this.CheckForCompletedPacking();

          /* If the user clicked on the last row of the table, don't need to detach and append it.  Exit here. */
          //if ($(tableRow).index() == ($(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr').length - 1)) { return; }

          // if ($(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr').length > 2)
          // {
          //   /* Now move the row we just added to the box to the end of the list. */
          //   var lastRow = $(tableRow).closest('table.table-custom').find('tr').last();
          //   $(tableRow).detach().insertAfter(lastRow);
          // }
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: error});
        }
      },

      RemoveCurrentBoxFromShipment: function ()
      {
        /* If there is only a single box in this shipment, return out. */
        var tableCount = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom').length;
        if (tableCount <= 1) { UpdateItemCounts(); return false; }

        /* Click the button on the main page to remove the box. */
        $('#buttonRemovePackageFromShipment').first().trigger('click');

        /* Send the items from the current box back to the list. */
        var tableItemObjects = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:visible tr:gt(1)');

        $(tableItemObjects).each(function (e)
        {
          PackVerify.RemoveThisTableRow(this);
        }).promise().done(function (e)
        {
          var prevContainerIndex = ($('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:visible').index() - 1);

          $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:visible').fadeOut().remove().promise().done(function ()
          {
            //$('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:eq(' + prevContainerIndex + ')').fadeIn().show();
            PackVerify.ShowContainerTable(prevContainerIndex);
            UpdateContainerCounts();
          });
        });
      },

      /* This takes the order number from the input box and adds it to the select box. */
      AddOrderNumbersToList: function ()
      {
        var inVal = $('#textOrderNumber').val();
        var bExists;

        /* Do not add duplicate entries to the select box. */
        $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').find('option').each(function ()
        {
          if (this.text == inVal)
          {
            bExists = true;
            /* Break out of the .each loop. */
            return false;
          }
        });

        if (bExists == true)
        {
          $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
          return false;
        }

        if (inVal.length > 0)
        {
          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').append($('<option />')
            .val(inVal)
            .text(inVal)
            .trigger('change'))
            .promise().done(function ()
            {
              $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
            });
        }
      },

      ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog: function ()
      {
        /* Add the first order at the top of the list. */
        /* The first order is already set by the user, then the 'Consolidate Orders' button on the Pack Verify dialog triggers this function. */
        $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').fadeIn(400)
          .promise().done(function ()
          {
            /* Clear the input box, then focus on it. */
            $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
          });
      },

      SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers: function ()
      {
        try
        {
          /* Append the shipper reference with each item in the select list in csv format. */
          /* Once this is done, change the SSBR on post load to loop through each option in the csv list. */
          var inputShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]');
          var shipperReferenceVal = $(inputShipperReference).val();

          /* If the user closes the dialog box, then opens it back up, we don't want to check the same orders more than once so only process what was entered into the dialog box this time. */
          var ordersToQuery = '';

          /* Loop through all the orders in the select box and determine if they are already in the list. */
          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').find('option').each(function (i, v)
          {
            /* Remove the spaces before the commas for comparison. */
            var arrayOrders = shipperReferenceVal.split(",").map(function (item)
            {
              return item.trim();
            });

            /* If the current option value is NOT in the list within the Shipper Reference field, add it. */
            if ($.inArray(v.value.trim(), arrayOrders) == -1)
            {
              ordersToQuery += v.value.trim() + ',';
              //shipperReferenceVal += ',' + v.value;
            }

            /* Remove the option once it is added to the input box. */
            $(this).remove();

          }).promise().done(function ()
          {
            /* Done creating the list of orders to get from the server which is now held in the ordersToQuery variable. */

            /* Hide the div. */
            $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').hide();

            /* Make sure there are orders in the list. */
            if (ordersToQuery.length > 0)
            {
              PackVerify.GetOrderInformationFromCustomer(ordersToQuery);
            }
            else
            {
              PackVerify.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR: No unique orders to pull from the server.  All consolidated orders have already been added to this shipment.');
            }
          });
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers()', Error: error });
        }
      },

      UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers: function (OrderNumber)
      {
        var inputShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]');
        var inputMiscReference07 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]');
        var shipperReferenceVal = $(inputShipperReference).val() + ',' + OrderNumber;
        //shipperReferenceVal += ',' + OrderNumber;

        /* Set these input values.  ShipperReference is used by the customer, MiscReference7 is used by the SBR to update each record post-ship. */
        /* ShipperReference ONLY keeps the first order number, before the comma, MiscReference7 keeps the entire string. */
        /* On the server-side, if MiscReference7 contains a comma, each item in the csv list gets posted back.  If MiscReference7 is empty, the ShipperReference is used instead for a single post-back. */
        $(inputShipperReference).val(shipperReferenceVal);
        $(inputMiscReference07).val(shipperReferenceVal);
        $('span.order-number-list').text(shipperReferenceVal);
      },

      /* Remove table rows from the container/box list. */
      /* Take the row from the container, then append it to the item list, adding the not-packed class. */
      RemoveThisTableRow: function (objElement)
      {
        var thisRow = $(objElement).closest('tr');
        var tableObj = $(objElement).closest('table');
        var tableRows = $(tableObj).find('tr').length;
        var trData = $(thisRow).data();

        var removedQuantity = parseFloat($(thisRow).find('td:eq(2)').text());

        try
        {
          $(thisRow).fadeOut().promise().done(function ()
          {
            /* Now remove it from this table and add it to the item list table. */
            $(this).remove();

            var firstRow = $('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails').find('tr').first();

            $('#tablePackVerifyOrderDetails tr').filter(function (index)
            {
              return $(this).data().EntryId == trData.EntryId;

            }).fadeOut('fast').promise().done(function ()
            {
              /* Need to remove commodities from current view model. */
              var currentContainerIndex = (parseInt($('span.current-container-index').text()) - 1);
              PackVerify.RemoveCommoditiesFromPackage(currentContainerIndex, $(this).data());

              trData.ShippedVal -= removedQuantity;

              $(this).find('td:eq(1)').text(trData.StartVal);
              $(this).find('td:eq(2)').text(trData.ShippedVal);
              $(this).find('td:eq(3)').text(trData.StartVal);

              $(this).find('td:eq(4) > span').removeClass('glyphicon-ban-circle').addClass('glyphicon-plus add-box-item').attr({ 'title': 'Add this item to the current box.' });

              $(this).removeClass('packed not-complete')
                .addClass('not-packed')
                .detach()
                .insertAfter(firstRow)
                .fadeIn('fast').promise().done(function (e) { UpdateItemCounts(); });
            });

            /* Show the 'Empty Table' text. */
            if (tableRows <= 3)
            {
              $('#tablePackVerifyCutTicketScanResults').find($('tr.empty-table').fadeIn());
            }

          });
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: error });
        }
      },

      /* tableIndex could be either 'prev', 'next', or an integer. */
      ShowContainerTable: function (tableIndex)
      {
        try
        {
          var currentContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:visible');
          var targetContainer;

          /* fallbackContainer is used when the last table in the container is reached.  Go back to the beginning on 'next', to the end on 'prev'. */
          //var fallbackContainer;
          var uiNavButton;

          //console.log($('span.current-container-index.container-val').text());
          var currentContainerIndex = parseInt($('span.current-container-index.container-val').text());

          switch (tableIndex)
          {
            case 'prev':
              // targetContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:eq(' + ($(currentContainer).index() - 1) + ')');
              targetContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:eq(' + (currentContainerIndex - 2) + ')');


              //fallbackContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom').last();
              uiNavButton = $('button[type=button][ng-click="vm.previousPackage();"]').first();
              break;

            case 'next':
              targetContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:eq(' + ($(currentContainer).index() + 1) + ')');
              //fallbackContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom').first();
              uiNavButton = $('button[type=button][ng-click="vm.nextPackage();"]').first();
              break;

            default:
              targetContainer = $('div.table-box-contents table.table-custom:eq(' + tableIndex + ')');
              break;
          }

          // if (targetContainer.length === 0) {
          //   targetContainer = fallbackContainer;
          // }

          $(uiNavButton).click();

          $(currentContainer).fadeOut(200).hide().promise().done(function ()
          {
            var rows = $(targetContainer).find('tr').length;
            if (rows > 2)
            {
              $(targetContainer).find('tr.empty-table').hide();
            }
            $(targetContainer).fadeIn(200).show().promise().done(function () { UpdateItemCounts(); });
          });

          /* Update the text to show 'Container X of Y'.  .index() + 1 as the index is 0 based. */
          $('span.current-container-index').text($(targetContainer).index() + 1);

          /* Now get the box associated with the table and change the select option. */
          var selIndex = $(targetContainer).data().SelectedIndex;

          $('#selectClonedBoxTypes').prop('selectedIndex', selIndex);

        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: error });
        }
      },

      ShowErrorAlert: function (ErrorMessage)
      {
        $('#divCustomAlert div.alert-message').text(ErrorMessage).closest('div.alert').show();
      }

    }; /* End return { */

  }()); /* end var PackVerify = (function () */

  var SessionData = (function ()
  {
    /* Private variables and functions. */
    let currentViewModel;
    let currentShipmentRequest;
    let currentUserContext = {};
    let serverLogging;

    return {

      SetCurrentUserContext: function (UserInformation)
      {
        /* If we only need the CompanyId, we can get that from the vmProfile. */
        /* If we need the UserId, we'll need to use a $.get call. */

        /* Updated 11/29/2021 */
        /* No need for the GET now as the data is stored in the vm.UserInformation node. */
        var localContext = {
          CompanyId: UserInformation.CompanyId,
          UserId: UserInformation.UserId,
          Machine: UserInformation.Machine
        };

        // if (!currentUserContext.UserId && bIncludeUser === true)
        // {
        //   $.ajax(
        //   {
        //     url: 'api/usercontext/GET',
        //     method: 'GET',
        //     async: false
        //   })
        //   .done(function (data)
        //   {
        //     localContext = data;
        //   })
        //   .fail(function (jqXHR, textStatus)
        //   {
        //     Logger.Log({ Source: GetCallingFunctionName(), Error: { name: 'AjaxError', message: jqXHR.ResponseText } });
        //   });
        // }
        // else if (!currentUserContext.CompanyId)
        // {
        //   /* Just need the CompanyId, get it from the profile, but don't null out the UserId if it is present. */
        //   localContext.CompanyId = vmProfile.CompanyId;
        //   localContext.UserId = currentUserContext.UserId;
        // }

        currentUserContext = localContext;

      }, /* end GetUserContext: function (vmProfile, bIncludeUser) */

      GetCurrentUserContext: function ()
      {
        return currentUserContext;
      },

      SetCurrentShipmentRequest: function (shipmentRequest)
      {
        currentShipmentRequest = shipmentRequest;
      },

      GetCurrentShipmentRequest: function ()
      {
        return currentShipmentRequest;
      },

      SetCurrentViewModel: function (viewModel)
      {
        currentViewModel = viewModel;
      },

      GetCurrentViewModel: function ()
      {
        return currentViewModel;
      },

      /* The debug mode will always write to the console.  Set the var to true to write to the server as well. */
      /* In future versions, add a hidden div to the page which will show errors as part of the UI. */
      SetServerDebugMode: function (writeToServer)
      {
        serverLogging = writeToServer;
      },

      GetServerDebugMode: function ()
      {
        return serverLogging;
      }

    }; /* end return { */

  }()); /* end var SessionData = (function () */

  /* If the below is placed within the Logger class it will need to be accessed using Logger.LogLevel.Trace */
  /* By placing it here, it is accessed using LogLevel.Trace.  This keeps the same nomenclature as the SBR logging class. */
  var LogLevel = {
    Trace: 0,
    Debug: 1,
    Info: 2,
    Warning: 3,
    Error: 4,
    Fatal: 5
  };

  var Logger = (function ()
  {
    let LogObject = {
      Source: null,
      LogLevel: null,
      Message: null,
      Data: null,
      Error: null
    }

    return {

      Log: function (LogObject)
      {
        try
        {
          /*
          Usage:
            Errors:
              try {
                ...
              } catch (error) {
                Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Error: error });
                OR
                Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Error: { name: 'Error name', message: 'Error message' } });
                OR
                Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Error: { name: 'Error name', message: 'Error message' }, Data: 'Simple or complex data object.' });
              }

            Info (default, no 'Type' needed):
              Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Message: 'Test of server info logging', Data: 'Simple or complex data object.' });

            All others:
              Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Type: 'Trace', Message: 'Test of server info logging with a complex data object.', Data: SessionData.GetCurrentUserContext() });
              Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Type: 'Fatal', Message: 'Test of server info logging with a simple data string.', Data: 'Simple data string literal.' });
              Logger.Log({ Source: 'FunctionName()', Type: 'Debug', Message: 'Test of server debug logging with no data object.' });
          */

          /* If the LogObject has an 'error' object, set the LogLevel here.  This makes the LogLevel variable optional for errors. */
          if (LogObject.Error)
          {
            LogObject.LogLevel = LogLevel.Error;

            /* Can't pass the error container to the server without preparing it inside a new object first. */
            var e = {};
            e.name = LogObject.Error.name;
            e.message = LogObject.Error.message;
            LogObject.Error = e;
          }
          else if (!LogObject.LogLevel)
          {
            /* If the LogObject does NOT have an 'error' object AND there is no LogLevel set, use .Info.  This makes the LogLevel variable optional for info logging. */
            LogObject.LogLevel = LogLevel.Info;
          }

          /* All logging will go to the console, output here. */
          switch (LogObject.LogLevel)
          {
            case LogLevel.Error:

              console.error('Exception encountered in', LogObject.Source);
              console.error(LogObject.Error.name);
              console.error(LogObject.Error.message);

              /* Use .trace if needed but within the Angular sandbox the .trace object can be huge and convoluted. */
              /* Be careful if passing .trace data on to the server as it will contain various data types and directives. */
              //console.error(LogObject.Error.trace);

              /* Don't use console.error for the data object, it causes readability issues. */
              if (LogObject.Data) { console.log(LogObject.Data); }
              break;

            /* Using the same nomenclature used by SBR logging. */
            case LogLevel.Info:
            case LogLevel.Debug:
            case LogLevel.Trace:
            case LogLevel.Fatal:
            default:

              console.log('Output from', LogObject.Source);
              console.log(LogObject.Message);
              if (LogObject.Data) { console.log(LogObject.Data); }
              break;
          }

          if (SessionData.GetServerDebugMode() == true)
          {
            var dataObject = {
              ServerMethod: 'AddClientEntry',
              MessageObject: LogObject
            };

            var ajaxObject = {
              UserContext: SessionData.GetCurrentUserContext(),
              Data: JSON.stringify(dataObject)
            };

            /* async doesn't necessarily need to be set to false here but I think it helps with data collisions and getting the error messages to appear in chronological order on the server. */
            var ajaxRequest = $.ajax({
              url: 'api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
              method: 'POST',
              contentType: 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded; charset=UTF-8',
              dataType: 'json',
              data: ajaxObject,
              async: false
            });

            ajaxRequest.done(function (json)
            {
              /* There is no return for this call, if the POST does come back with data, it's a server message/error like 'UserContext cannot be null' or more likely '{"Data":"","ErrorCode":0}' */
              //console.log(JSON.parse(json.Data));
            });

            ajaxRequest.fail(function (jqXHR, textStatus)
            {
              console.log('Unable to log message to server.');
              console.log(jqXHR);
              console.log(textStatus);
            });

            ajaxRequest.always(function (jqXHR, textStatus, jqXHRError)
            {

            });
          }

          /* Need to hide the loader outside the decision trees. */
          HideLoader();

        }
        catch (error)
        {
          console.log(error.message);
        }
      }

    }; /* end return { */

  }()); /* end var Logger = (function () */

} /* end function ClientBusinessRules() */

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
  this.PageLoaded = function(location)
  {
    if (window.location.hash == '#!/shipping')
    {
      window.localStorage.removeItem('cbrValues');
    }
  };

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
  this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {
    Tools.ShowLoader();
  };

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
  this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    ConsolidatedOrders.InitElements();
    Tools.HideLoader();

    GetWeightFromScale();
  };

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns Promise<void>
  this.NewShipment = async function(shipmentRequest)
  {
    Tools.SetCurrentViewModel(this.vm, Tools.FocusOnLoadInput());
    if (Tools.GetCurrentShipper() != '7F4175') { $('#divDoNotRateShop').hide(); }

    //below is for testing the new user method requests
    await Tools.MakeUserMethodRequest('GetJsonObject').then((data) => console.log(data));
  };

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
  this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val();
  };

// GetWeightFromScale(callback) // returns void
  function GetWeightFromScale(callback)
  {
    $('[ng-click="vm.getWeight()" ]'.replace(' ', '')).trigger('click').promise().done(function()
    {
      /* Set the default box type to 'BAG 1'.  The multiple props and attr are for older browsers. */
      if ($.isFunction(callback)) callback;
    });
  }

// InitElements() // returns void
      InitElements: function()
      {
        /* Create the Consolidate Orders button dynamically. */
        /* This is done on the post load for my customer as they want to have a primary order loaded first. */
        /* With each consolidated order being added, I am comparing the consignee to the primary order to confirm this order is going to the correct consignee. */
        $('div.top-tool-bar > div.pull-left').append($('<button />')
          .addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary')
          .attr('id', 'buttonConsolidateOrders')
          .text('Consolidate Orders').fadeIn());

        /* Set up all delegates from within this block. */
        $('body').delegate('#buttonConsolidateOrders', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonAddOrderNumbers', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.AddOrderNumbersToList();
        });

        /* Customer uses a scanner that appends the <enter> key after the scan.  This delegate fires when that happens. */
        $('body').delegate('#textOrderNumber', 'keyup', function(e)
        {
          var keycode = e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which;
          if ((keycode == 13) | (keycode == 9))
          {
            ConsolidatedOrders.AddOrderNumbersToList();
          }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonSaveConsolidatedOrders', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonCloseConsolidatedOrdersWithoutSaving', 'click', function(e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();
        });

      }

// Source: F Schumacher (FSCHUMAC)_Samples Area (7F4175) PROD CBR_2449.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
  this.PageLoaded = function (location)

    {
    }
  }

  this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {
    Tools.ShowLoader();
  }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
  this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    ConsolidatedOrders.InitElements(false);
    Tools.HideLoader();
    
    $('#chkDoNotRateShop').prop('checked', shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData3);

    $('[ng-click="vm.getWeight()"]')
      .trigger('click')
      .promise().done(function () 
    {
      /* Set the default box type to 'BAG 1'.  The multiple props and attr are for older browsers. */
      $('select[property="BoxType"] > option[label="SAMPLE BAG 1"]').prop({ 'selected': 'true', 'selected': true }).attr('selected', 'selected').trigger('change');

    });    
  }

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
  this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val();
    // Tools.GetPackageDefaultsObject().UserData3 = $('#chkDoNotRateShop').prop('checked');
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData3 = $('#chkDoNotRateShop').prop('checked');
  }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
  this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest)
  {
    Tools.SetCurrentViewModel(this.vm, true, true, Tools.FocusOnLoadInput);
  }

// InitElements(LogToServer) // returns void
      InitElements: function (LogToServer)
      {
        /* Create the Consolidate Orders button dynamically. */
        /* This is done on the post load for my customer as they want to have a primary order loaded first. */
        /* With each consolidated order being added, I am comparing the consignee to the primary order to confirm this order is going to the correct consignee. */
        $('div.top-tool-bar > div.pull-left')
          .append($('<button />')
            .addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary')
            .attr('id', 'buttonConsolidateOrders')
            .text('Consolidate Orders')
            .fadeIn());

        /* Set up all delegates from within this block. */
        $('body').delegate('#buttonConsolidateOrders', 'click', function (e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonAddOrderNumbers', 'click', function (e) 
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.AddOrderNumbersToList();
        });

        /* Customer uses a scanner that appends the <enter> key after the scan.  This delegate fires when that happens. */
        $('body').delegate('#textOrderNumber', 'keyup', function (e)
        {
          var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
          if (keycode == 13 | keycode == 9) 
          {
            ConsolidatedOrders.AddOrderNumbersToList();
          }
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonSaveConsolidatedOrders', 'click', function (e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers();
        });

        $('body').delegate('#buttonCloseConsolidatedOrdersWithoutSaving', 'click', function (e)
        {
          ConsolidatedOrders.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();
        });        


        /* Logging to the server only works with SBR, set to false if not using SBR's with a custom logging method. */
        Tools.SetServerDebugMode(LogToServer);
      }

// ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog() // returns void
      ShowConsolidatedOrderDialog: function ()
      {
        Tools.ShowOverlay();

        /* Get rid of any existing options. */
        $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').empty();

        /* Add whatever orders are already in the Shipper Reference to the select box. */
        var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
        var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);

        $(arrayOrders).each(function (a, b)
        {
          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').append($('<option />')
            .val(b)
            .text(b)
            .removeClass('not-processed')
            .addClass('processed')
            .css('color', '#265ca1'));
        });

        $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').fadeIn('fast').promise().done(function () 
        {
          /* Clear the input box, then focus on it. */
          $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
        });
      }

// AddOrderNumbersToList() // returns boolean | void
      AddOrderNumbersToList: function ()
      {
        var inVal = $('#textOrderNumber').val();
        var bExists;

        /* Do not add duplicate entries to the select box. */
        $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').find('option').each(function ()
        {
          if (this.text == inVal) 
          {
            bExists = true;
            /* Break out of the .each loop. */
            return false;
          }
        });

        if (bExists == true)
        {
          $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
          return false;
        }

        /* The order number is unique, add it to the select box. */
        if (inVal.length > 0)
        {
          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders').append($('<option />')
            .val(inVal)
            .text(inVal)
            .addClass('not-processed')
            .trigger('change'))
            .promise().done(function ()
            {
              $('#textOrderNumber').val([]).focus();
            });
        }
      }

// SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers() // returns void
      SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers: function ()
      {
        try
        {
          var ordersToQuery = '';

          $('#selectConsolidatedOrders > option.not-processed').each(function ()
          {
            ordersToQuery += $(this).text() + ',';
          });

          /* Done creating the list of orders to get from the server which is now held in the ordersToQuery variable. */

          /* Hide the div. */
          $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').hide();

          /* Make sure there are orders in the list. */
          if (ordersToQuery.length > 0)
          {
            //ConsolidatedOrders.GetOrderInformationFromCustomer(ordersToQuery);
            Tools.MakeUserMethodRequest('GetOrderInformation', ordersToQuery, true, this.ProcessDataFromCustomer);
          }
          else
          {
            Tools.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR: No unique orders to pull from the server.  All consolidated orders have already been added to this shipment.');
          }

        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'SaveConsolidatedOrderNumbers()', Error: error });
        }
      }

// ProcessDataFromCustomer(jsonData) // returns void
      ProcessDataFromCustomer: function (jsonData)
      {
        try
        {
          $(jsonData).each(function (a, b)
          {
            /* For testing, this is set to '!== true' so it will return order data.  This needs to be set to '=== true' for any other case. */
            if (ConsolidatedOrders.CheckForMatchingConsignee(b) == true)
            {
              var currentPackage = Tools.GetCurrentPackage();
              if (!currentPackage)
              {
                Tools.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR:  Could not add commodities to package for order ' + b.orderId + '.  See error console for details.');
                return false;
              }
              ConsolidatedOrders.UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(b.orderId, b.orderNumber);
            }
            else
            {
              Tools.ShowErrorAlert('ERROR 500:  Could not add commodities for order ' + b.orderId + '.  Address mismatch.');
            }
          });
        }
        catch (error)
        { 
          console.log(error);
        }
      }

// CheckForMatchingConsignee(CustomerOrderObject) // returns boolean | undefined
      CheckForMatchingConsignee: function (CustomerOrderObject)
      {
        try
        {
          var con = $('name-address[nameaddress="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee"]');

          let a = {
            //conCompany: $(con).find('input[name="company"]').val().trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ',''),
            conAddress1: $(con).find('input[name="address1"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: $(con).find('input[name="city"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: $(con).find('input[name="stateProvince"]').val().trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: $(con).find('input[name="postalCode"]').val().trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          let b = {
            //conCompany: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.CONSIGNEE_COMPANY.trim().toUpperCase().replaceAll(' ', ''),
            conAddress1: CustomerOrderObject.shipAddress1.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conCity: CustomerOrderObject.shipCity.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conState: CustomerOrderObject.shipState.trim().toUpperCase(),
            conPostalCode: CustomerOrderObject.shipZipCode.trim().substring(0, 5)
          };

          /* Remove all the spaces in the strings so we get a good comparison, not one that's thrown off by an extra space. */
          let aa = JSON.stringify(a).replaceAll(' ', '');
          let bb = JSON.stringify(b).replaceAll(' ', '');

          /* Quick comparison to see if the strings match. */
          if (aa != bb)
          {
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Primary order data to follow.', Data: a });
            Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Message: 'Could not add order ' + CustomerOrderObject.orderNumber + ' (' + CustomerOrderObject.orderId + '). Subsequent order data to follow.', Data: b });
          }

          return (aa == bb);
        }
        catch (error)
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'CheckForMatchingConsignee()', Error: error });
        }
      }

// UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers(OrderId, OrderNumber) // returns void
      UpdateReferencesWithOrderNumbers: function (OrderId, OrderNumber)
      {
        var inputShipperReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]');
        var inputMiscReference07 = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]');
        var inputConsigneeReference = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ConsigneeReference"]');
        var shipperReferenceVal = $(inputShipperReference).val() + ',' + OrderId;
        var consigneeReferenceVal = $(inputConsigneeReference).val() + ',' + OrderNumber;
        
        var newUniqueString = Tools.GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
        var newConsigneeReferenceString = Tools.GetUniqueCSVStringFromString(consigneeReferenceVal);

        /* Set these input values.  ShipperReference is used by the customer, MiscReference7 is used by the SBR to update each record post-ship. */
        /* ShipperReference ONLY keeps the first order number when it goes to PostShip, before the comma, MiscReference7 keeps the entire string. */
        /* On the server-side, if MiscReference7 contains a comma, each item in the csv list gets posted back.  If MiscReference7 is empty, the ShipperReference is used instead for a single post-back. */
        $(inputShipperReference).val(newUniqueString);
        $(inputMiscReference07).val(newUniqueString);
        $(inputConsigneeReference).val(newConsigneeReferenceString);
      }

        $('#divModalConsolidateShipments').hide();

        Tools.HideLoader();
      }

// ShowOverlay() // returns void
      ShowOverlay: function ()
      {
        if ($('div.overlay').length === 0)
        {
          //console.log('div.overlay not found, creating');
          $('div.body-content').first().append($('<div />')
            .addClass('overlay')
            .css({
              'content': '',
              'position': 'fixed',
              'top': 0, 'left': 0,
              'width': '100vw',
              'height': '100vh',
              'background-color': 'rgba(0, 0, 0, .25)',
              'z-index': 1049
            })).show();

          /*
            .overlay {
              content: '';
              display: none;
              position: fixed;
              top: 0;
              left: 0;
              width: 100%;
              height: 100%;
              background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, .25);
              z-index: 1049;
            }
          */
        }
        else
        {
          $('div.overlay').show();
        }
      }

// HideOverlay() // returns void
