      {
        $('div.overlay').hide();
      }

// ShowErrorAlert(ErrorMessage) // returns void
      ShowErrorAlert: function (ErrorMessage)
      {
        var divAlert = $('<div />').attr('id', this.GetRandomAlphaNumericString());

        $(divAlert).addClass('alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom alert-danger ng-scope')
          .css({ 'z-index': 1550, 'cursor': 'pointer' })
          .attr('role', 'alert')
          .append($('<button />')
            .attr('type', 'button')
            .addClass('close')
            .append($('<span />')
              .attr('aria-hidden', 'false')
              .text('x'))
            .append($('<span />')
              .addClass('sr-only')
              .text('Close')))
          .append($('<div />')
            .append($('<div />')
              // .append($('<span />').addClass('glyphicon glyphicon-alert'))
              // .css({ 'position': 'relative', 'top': '2px' })
              .addClass('ng-scope alert-message')
              .text(ErrorMessage)
              .prepend($('<span />')
                .css('padding-right', '10px')
                .addClass('glyphicon glyphicon-alert custom-error-icon'))));

        $('body').append($(divAlert).show());
        /*
          <button type="button" class="close" onclick="$(this).closest('div').hide();">
            <span aria-hidden="false">×</span>
            <span class="sr-only">Close</span>
          </button>
          <div>
            <div class="ng-scope alert-message"></div>
          </div>
        */
      }

// WaitForElement(element, waitThenFocus, defaultValue, timeoutInSeconds, callback) // returns Promise<void>
      WaitForElement: async function (element, waitThenFocus, defaultValue, timeoutInSeconds, callback)
      {
        let a = await PollDomForElement(element, timeoutInSeconds).then(function (promiseResult)
        {
          if (defaultValue) { $(element).val(defaultValue); }

          if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback(); }

          if (waitThenFocus == true) { $(element).focus(); }

        }).catch(error =>
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'WaitForElement()', Error: error });

        }).finally(() =>
        {
          /* If anything is needed to run whether the promise is resolved or rejected, put it here. */
        });
      }

// WaitForSelectOptions(selectElement, optionLength, indexOptionToSelect, stringOptionToSelect, bClearFirst, timeoutInSeconds, callback) // returns Promise<void>
      WaitForSelectOptions: async function (selectElement, optionLength = 1, indexOptionToSelect, stringOptionToSelect, bClearFirst, timeoutInSeconds, callback)
      {

        if (indexOptionToSelect && stringOptionToSelect)
        {
          throw new error('Cannot use both indexOptionToSelect and stringOptionToSelect.  Please use only one option and try again.');
        }

        if (bClearFirst) { $(selectElement).val([]); }

        var element = selectElement + ' option:gt(' + optionLength + ')';

        let a = await PollDomForElement(element, timeoutInSeconds).then(function (promiseResult)
        {
          if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback(); }

          if (indexOptionToSelect) { $(selectElement + ' option').eq(indexOptionToSelect).prop({ 'selected': 'selected' }); }

          if (stringOptionToSelect) { $(selectElement).val(stringOptionToSelect); }

        }).catch(error =>
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'WaitForSelectOptions()', Error: error });

        }).finally(() =>
        {
          /* If anything is needed to run whether the promise is resolved or rejected, put it here. */
        });
      }

// WaitForTableRows(table, tableRowsNeeded, timeoutInSeconds, callback) // returns Promise<void>
      WaitForTableRows: async function (table, tableRowsNeeded = 1, timeoutInSeconds, callback)
      {
        var element = table + ' tr:gt(' + tableRowsNeeded + ':visible)';

        let a = await PollDomForElement(element, timeoutInSeconds).then(function (promiseResult)
        {
          if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback(); }

        }).catch(error =>
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'WaitForTableRows()', Error: error });

        }).finally(() =>
        {
          /* If anything is needed to run whether the promise is resolved or rejected, put it here. */
        });
      }

// WaitForInputValues(inputSelector, minEntries, timeoutInSeconds, callback) // returns Promise<void>
      WaitForInputValues: async function (inputSelector, minEntries, timeoutInSeconds, callback)
      {
        let a = await PollInputsForValues(inputSelector, minEntries, timeoutInSeconds).then(function (promiseResult)
        {
          if ($.isFunction(callback)) { callback(); }

        }).catch(error =>
        {
          Logger.Log({ Source: 'WaitForInputValues()', Error: error });

        }).finally(() =>
        {
          /* If anything is needed to run whether the promise is resolved or rejected, put it here. */
        });
      }

// Source: FalconNDX (FNDX)_Falcon_CBR_1794.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) { 
        debugger;
        
        //Days List
        const days = ["Sunday","Monday","Tuesday","Wednesday","Thursday","Friday","Saturday"];
         
        // Current Date
        var dt = new Date();  
       //dt.setDate(dt.getDate()  +1);
        //alert(dt);
        
        //Finding Last Date of the Month
        var lastDate=new Date(dt.getFullYear(),dt.getMonth()+1 ,0);
        var onlyDate_lastDate= lastDate.getDate();
       
        
          
        //Months List  
        var month= dt.getMonth()+1;
        var nextmonth =dt.getMonth()+1;  //Get the current month
        
        
        //Year
        var currentYear = dt.getFullYear();
  
        
        
                
        var nextdate=dt.getDate()+1;    
        var newdate=dt.getDate()+2;
        
        
        
        /* Comparing current date(saturday/sunday) with lastdate of the month
        1. Current date and last date is saturday 
        2. Next to Current date and last date is saturday */
        
        /* Scenarios
        1. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Sunday 
            Next to current date should match with last date.
        2. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Sunday
            Current date should match with last date.
        3. Current date - Saturday , Last date - Saturday
        4. Current date - Sunday , Last date - Saturday
        
        
        
        */
        
       if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=2;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
       
     
      else if(dt.getDate()== onlyDate_lastDate && days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
       {
           
           if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
              
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
            
           
           
       }
        else if(nextdate == onlyDate_lastDate )  
       {
            
             if(month==12)
            {
                nextmonth=1; // Setting next month if current date is last date of the month eg: 31/07/2022 => 07 to 08
                newdate=1;
                currentYear=currentYear + 1;
            }else
            {
                 nextmonth=month +1; 
                  newdate=1;
                  currentYear=currentYear;
            }
            
             
           
       }
       
     //Saturday to Monday 
       var monthIndex = nextmonth;
                if(monthIndex<10)
                monthIndex=('0'+monthIndex);
                
       var mondateIndex=newdate;
                if(mondateIndex<10)
                mondateIndex=('0'+mondateIndex);
                
       var lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
        
     if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Saturday")
        {
            lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+mondateIndex);
            $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
        }
         
         
         
      //Sunday to Monday   
         var sundateIndex=dt.getDate();
       
         if(dt.getDate()==onlyDate_lastDate)
            {
              
                 sundateIndex=newdate;   
                   
            }
            else
            {
               
                sundateIndex=dt.getDate()+1;
            }

        
          if(sundateIndex<10)
            sundateIndex=('0'+sundateIndex);
                     
           if(days[dt.getDay()] == "Sunday")
            {
                 lastdate=(currentYear+"-"+ monthIndex+"-"+sundateIndex);
                 $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(lastdate).change();
            }
           
    }

this.PageLoaded = function(location) {

                    });

// Source: FortessaTS (FTS)_FortessaCBR_1897.cs
// function Shiping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {
        this.vm.getWeight = customGetWeight;
        //shipperReferenceKeyUp();
        miscReference7KeyUp();
        replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(this.vm.profile.BoxTypes);

        $('body').delegate(client.shipping.addPackageButton, 'keyup', function (e) {

            if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                //client.shipping.shipperReference.focus();
                client.shipping.miscRef7.focus();
            }
        })


        function shipperReferenceKeyUp() {
            $('body').delegate(client.shipping.shipperReference, 'keydown', function (e) {
                if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
                }
            })
        }

        function miscReference7KeyUp() {
            $('body').delegate(client.shipping.miscRef7, 'keydown', function (e) {
                if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
                }
            })
        }


        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        function replaceSelectBoxTypeWithInputText(boxTypes) {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                client.shipping.$selectBoxType = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].BoxType"]');
                if (client.shipping.$selectBoxType.length > 0) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType = $('<input type="text" />').attr({ class: client.shipping.$selectBoxType.attr('class') });
                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.hide();
                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.insertAfter(client.shipping.$selectBoxType);

                    client.shipping.$inputBoxType.keyup(boxTypes, function (e) {
                        if (e.key === 'Tab' || e.key === "Enter") {
                            for (var boxType of e.data) {
                                if (boxType.Name == this.value) {
                                    this.value = '';
                                    client.shipping.$selectBoxType.val(boxType.Id).change();
                                    client.shipping.addPackageButton.focus();
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    });

                }
            }, 10);
        }




    }

// function PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        this.vm.getWeight();
		
        //scroll selected service into view
        scrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
		
		//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 29, Year: 2024 }
        //this.vm.startshipdate.value = new Date(shipDate.Year, shipDate.Month, shipDate.Day);
        //shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
		
        //this.vm.overrideOptimization = pastDueDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference6)
        pastDueDate(shipmentRequest.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].MiscReference6);
		
		//checkAndSetShipDate(this.vm);
		checkAndSetShipDateTest(this.vm);
		
        this.vm.arriveByDate = client.shipping.arriveByDate;
        client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();

        function pastDueDate(miscReference6) {
            //if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0 && miscReference6 != '*1900-01-01T00:00:00*') {

            if (miscReference6 && miscReference6.trim().length != 0) {

                miscReference6 = miscReference6.replaceAll('*', '');
                client.shipping.arriveByDate = miscReference6.split("T")[0];

                var dateRequired = Date.parse(miscReference6);
                if (dateRequired <= Date.now() && miscReference6 != "1900-01-01T00:00:00") {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-success').addClass('text-danger');
                    return true;
                }
                else {
                    $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').addClass('text-success');
                }
            };
            return false;
        }

        //scroll into view stuff
        function isIE() {
            return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
        }

        function scrollIntoView(element, value) {
            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (element.val() == value) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                        var selectTop = element.offset().top;
                        element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                    }
                }, 50);

            }

        }

		function checkAndSetShipDate(viewModel) {
            var hardCutoffTime = 6;
            var currentDateTime = new Date();//can simulate it being other dates and times by changing this value
            console.log("Current datetime returned: " + currentDateTime);
            var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();

            console.log("Hours: " + hours);
            console.log("Day: " + dayOfWeek);

            

            var dateInterval = setInterval(function () {
                var $shipDt = $('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]');

                if ($shipDt.length) {
                    clearInterval(dateInterval);
                    
                    if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
                        //day is saturday, add 2 days and return new date
                        var newDate = addDays(2);
						//var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                        console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
						//var shipDate = { Month: 8, Day: 29, Year: 2024 }
						viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
						shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
						//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                        //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
						//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                        //return;
                    }

                    if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
                        //cutoff time reached, change date as follows
                        if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
                            //add 3 days making Monday the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(3);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }

                        else {
                            //add 1 day to the date making tomorrow the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(1);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							viewModel.startshipdate.value = new Date(newDate.Year, newDate.Month, newDate.Day);
							shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
							//$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }
                    }
                }

		function checkAndSetShipDateTest(viewModel)
		{
			debugger;

				shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = shipDate;
			}
			
			if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
				if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
					var finalDate = addDays(3);

// function NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {

        this.vm.overrideOptimization = false;
        this.vm.arriveByDate = '';
        $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').removeClass('text-success');
		
        client.shipping.loadValue.focus();
        client.shipping.maintabfocus('General');
        client.shipping.subtabfocus('Consignee', 'Account/Tax');

		

        //check and set the CPD checkbox here
        checkAndSetCPD(this.vm);


        //check for CPD flag here, set checked if true
        function checkAndSetCPD(viewModel) {
            //create interval here to watch for CPD checkbox
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $cpdCB = $('[ng-model="vm.cpdProcessFlow"]');

                if ($cpdCB.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    var cpdFlag = sessionStorage.getItem("cpdflag");
                    //status can be True, False or Null

                    if (cpdFlag == "true") {
                        viewModel.cpdProcessFlow = true;
                    }
                    else {
                        viewModel.cpdProcessFlow = false;
                    }


                }
            }, 10)

        }

		
    }

// function AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
    this.AddPackage = function (shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
        this.vm.getWeight();

        if (this.vm.cpdProcessFlow) {
            //$(client.shipping.shipperReference).focus().select();
            $(client.shipping.miscRef7).focus().select();
        }
        else {
            client.shipping.$inputBoxType.focus();
        }
    }

// function PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        for (var i = 0; i < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; i++) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[i].MiscReference20 = this.vm.overrideOptimization ? '1' : '0';
			
        }
		//this.vm.startshipdate.value = new Date('2024-08-30');
		//checkAndSetShipDate(this.vm);
		
		
		function checkAndSetShipDate(viewModel) {
            var hardCutoffTime = 10;
            var currentDateTime = new Date();//can simulate it being other dates and times by changing this value
            console.log("Current datetime returned: " + currentDateTime);
            var hours = currentDateTime.getHours();
            var dayOfWeek = currentDateTime.getDay();

            console.log("Hours: " + hours);
            console.log("Day: " + dayOfWeek);

            

            var dateInterval = setInterval(function () {
                var $shipDt = $('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]');

                if ($shipDt.length) {
                    clearInterval(dateInterval);
                    
                    if (dayOfWeek == 6) {
                        //day is saturday, add 2 days and return new date
                        var newDate = addDays(2);
						var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+(newDate.getMonth()+1)+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                        console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
						$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                        //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
						//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                        //return;
                    }

                    if (hours >= hardCutoffTime) {
                        //cutoff time reached, change date as follows
                        if (dayOfWeek == 5) {
                            //add 3 days making Monday the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(3);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+newDate.getMonth()+1+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }

                        else {
                            //add 1 day to the date making tomorrow the ship date
                            var newDate = addDays(1);
							var dateFinal = newDate.getFullYear()+'/'+newDate.getMonth()+1+'/'+newDate.getDate();
                            console.log("New Date: " + dateFinal);
							$('[ng-model="vm.startshipdate.value"]').val(dateFinal).change();
                            //viewModel.startshipdate.value = newDate;
							//shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate = dateFinal;
                            //return;
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
            

            

        }

        function addDays(days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setDate(date.getDate() + days);
            return date;
        }
		
		
    }

// function PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
    this.PostShip = function (shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {

        //Set the CPD flag to whatever state the this.vm.CPDWorkflow state is
        sessionStorage.setItem("cpdflag", this.vm.cpdProcessFlow);
    }

        function  translateDates() {
            const monthMapping = {
                "January": "Janvier",
                "February": "Février",
                "March": "Mars",
                "April": "Avril",
                "May": "Mai",
                "June": "Juin",
                "July": "Juillet",
                "August": "Août",
                "September": "Septembre",
                "October": "Octobre",
                "November": "Novembre",
                "December": "Décembre"
                };
                
                const dayMapping = {
                  'Mon': 'Lun',
                  'Tue': 'Mar',
                  'Wed': 'Mer',
                  'Thu': 'Jeu',
                  'Fri': 'Ven',
                  'Sat': 'Sam',
                  'Sun': 'Dim'
                };


                const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
                $("small[aria-label]").each(function() {
                  var day = $(this).text().trim();
                  var translatedDay = dayMapping[day];
                  if (translatedDay) {
                    $(this).text(translatedDay);
                  }
                });
                
                $("strong").each(function() {
                  var dateText = $(this).text().trim();
                  var month = dateText.split(' ')[0];
                  var translatedMonth = monthMapping[month];
                  if (translatedMonth) {
                      var updatedText = dateText.replace(month, translatedMonth);
                      $(this).text(updatedText);
                  }
                });

                var buttonLeft = document.querySelector('.uib-left');
                var buttonRight = document.querySelector('.uib-right');
        
                if (buttonLeft) {
                    $(buttonLeft).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('previous');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }
                
                if (buttonRight) {
                    $(buttonRight).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('next');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }


            }

            function getCurrentMonthYear(action) {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let monthYear = null;
               
                $('strong.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text();
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                        if (text.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                            if(action=='next') {
                                $(this).text(getNextMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            } else {
                                $(this).text(getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            }
                            return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                        }
                    }
                });
                
                return monthYear;
            }


            function getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is December.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 11) {
                    // Increment the year and reset the month to January.
                    year++;
                    month = monthNamesFr[0];
                } else {
                    // Get the next month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex + 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }


            function getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is January.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 0) {
                    // Decrement the year and set the month to December.
                    year--;
                    month = monthNamesFr[11];
                } else {
                    // Get the previous month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex - 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

            translateElements2: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).val();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },
            translateElements: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },

            replaceText: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerHTML = this.innerHTML.replace(oldText, newText);
            },
            replaceText2: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerText = this.innerText.replace(oldText, newText);
            },

            replaceValue: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).val(newText);
            },

            replaceLabel: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).attr('label', newText);
            },
             replaceLabel2(selector, oldText, newText) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('label') === oldText) {
                        $(this).attr('label', newText);
                    }
                });
            },

            handleSpecificCases: function() {
                $('h5:contains("No commodities added")').text('Aucune marchandise ajoutée');
                $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;1") {
                        $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;1');
                    }
                });
            },
        };

// translateDates() // returns void
        function  translateDates() {
            const monthMapping = {
                "January": "Janvier",
                "February": "Février",
                "March": "Mars",
                "April": "Avril",
                "May": "Mai",
                "June": "Juin",
                "July": "Juillet",
                "August": "Août",
                "September": "Septembre",
                "October": "Octobre",
                "November": "Novembre",
                "December": "Décembre"
                };
                
                const dayMapping = {
                  'Mon': 'Lun',
                  'Tue': 'Mar',
                  'Wed': 'Mer',
                  'Thu': 'Jeu',
                  'Fri': 'Ven',
                  'Sat': 'Sam',
                  'Sun': 'Dim'
                };


                const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
                $("small[aria-label]").each(function() {
                  var day = $(this).text().trim();
                  var translatedDay = dayMapping[day];
                  if (translatedDay) {
                    $(this).text(translatedDay);
                  }
                });
                
                $("strong").each(function() {
                  var dateText = $(this).text().trim();
                  var month = dateText.split(' ')[0];
                  var translatedMonth = monthMapping[month];
                  if (translatedMonth) {
                      var updatedText = dateText.replace(month, translatedMonth);
                      $(this).text(updatedText);
                  }
                });

                var buttonLeft = document.querySelector('.uib-left');
                var buttonRight = document.querySelector('.uib-right');
        
                if (buttonLeft) {
                    $(buttonLeft).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('previous');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }
                
                if (buttonRight) {
                    $(buttonRight).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('next');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }


            }

// getCurrentMonthYear(action) // returns monthYear
            function getCurrentMonthYear(action) {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let monthYear = null;
               
                $('strong.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text();
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                        if (text.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                            if(action=='next') {
                                $(this).text(getNextMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            } else {
                                $(this).text(getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            }
                            return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                        }
                    }
                });
                
                return monthYear;
            }

// getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) // returns month + ' ' + year
            function getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is December.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 11) {
                    // Increment the year and reset the month to January.
                    year++;
                    month = monthNamesFr[0];
                } else {
                    // Get the next month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex + 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

// getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) // returns month + ' ' + year
            function getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is January.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 0) {
                    // Decrement the year and set the month to December.
                    year--;
                    month = monthNamesFr[11];
                } else {
                    // Get the previous month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex - 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

// deliverDatePicker() // returns void
         function deliverDatePicker() {

            translateToFrench = {
                "Months": {
                  "January": "Janvier",
                  "February": "Février",
                  "March": "Mars",
                  "April": "Avril",
                  "May": "Mai",
                  "June": "Juin",
                  "July": "Juillet",
                  "August": "Août",
                  "September": "Septembre",
                  "October": "Octobre",
                  "November": "Novembre",
                  "December": "Décembre"
                },
                "Days": {
                  "Sunday": "Dimanche",
                  "Monday": "Lundi",
                  "Tuesday": "Mardi",
                  "Wednesday": "Mercredi",
                  "Thursday": "Jeudi",
                  "Friday": "Vendredi",
                  "Saturday": "Samedi"
                }
              };

            var datePicker = $('div.uib-daypicker');
            var currentMonth = datePicker.find('th button strong');
            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(translateToFrench['Months'])) {
                if (currentMonth.text().indexOf(key) != -1) {
                    currentMonth.text(currentMonth.text().replace(key, value));
                }
            }



            datePicker.find('th small').each(function () {
                $(this).text(translateToFrench.Days[this.innerHTML]);
            })
        }

// AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
    this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
       
        $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
            // Check if the label has the correct style and text
            if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;"+ (packageIndex)) {
                // Change the label's text
                $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;' + (packageIndex+1));
            }
        });
    }

// RemovePackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
    this.RemovePackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
       
        $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
            // Check if the label has the correct style and text
            if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;"+ (packageIndex+2)) {
                // Change the label's text
                $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;' + (packageIndex+1));
            }
        });
    }

// Source: GAP INC (GAPMailrooms)_DirectToMobileCBR_1918.cs
// OnCboReturnAddressChange() // returns void
const OnCboReturnAddressChange = () => 
	{		
		//debugger;
		
		var selectedReturnAddress = $("#cboPredefinedReturnAddress select").val().replace('string:', '');
		
		returnAddressList = GetReturnAddresses();
		
		 if ($.isEmptyObject(returnAddressList) === false)
		 {					
			if (returnAddressList!=undefined)
			{
				var returnAddress = returnAddressList.find(x => x.ReturnLocationDescription === selectedReturnAddress);
				
				if (returnAddress !== undefined)
				{
					//debugger;
					
					vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = returnAddress.LocationAddress;

					CopyReturnAddressToOriginAddress();
					
				}
			} 
		 }								

// IsEventAttached($element, elementEvent, elementEventHandler) // returns boolean
	function IsEventAttached($element, elementEvent, elementEventHandler)
	{			
			debugger;
			
			var result = false;
					
			if (($("#cboPredefinedReturnAddress select").get(0) != undefined) && ($._data($element.get(0), "events") != undefined))
			{
				var elementEvents = $._data($element.get(0), "events");
				elementEventHandler = elementEventHandler.toString();
				result = (elementEvents && elementEvents[elementEvent]?.some(ev => ev.handler.toString() === elementEventHandler))
			}
			
			return result;
		}

// CopyReturnAddressToOriginAddress() // returns void
	function CopyReturnAddressToOriginAddress(){
	
        $('[name="company"]:eq(1)').val($('[name="company"]:eq(2)').val());
        $('[name="company"]:eq(1)').trigger("change");
        
        $('[name="contact"]:eq(1)').val($('[name="contact"]:eq(2)').val());
        $('[name="contact"]:eq(1)').trigger("change");
        
        $('[name="address1"]:eq(1)').val($('[name="address1"]:eq(2)').val());
        $('[name="address1"]:eq(1)').trigger("change");
        
        $('[name="address2"]:eq(1)').val($('[name="address2"]:eq(2)').val());
        $('[name="address2"]:eq(1)').trigger("change");
        
        $('[name="address3"]:eq(1)').val($('[name="address3"]:eq(2)').val());
        $('[name="address3"]:eq(1)').trigger("change");
        
        $('[name="city"]:eq(1)').val($('[name="city"]:eq(2)').val());
        $('[name="city"]:eq(1)').trigger("change");
        
        $('[name="stateProvince"]:eq(1)').val($('[name="stateProvince"]:eq(2)').val());
        $('[name="stateProvince"]:eq(1)').trigger("change");
        
        $('[name="postalCode"]:eq(1)').val($('[name="postalCode"]:eq(2)').val());
        $('[name="postalCode"]:eq(1)').trigger("change");
        
        $('[name="Country"]:eq(1)').val($('[name="Country"]:eq(2)').val());
        $('[name="Country"]:eq(1)').trigger("change");
	}

// GetReturnAddresses() // returns array|undefined
	function GetReturnAddresses()
	{
		var userMethodParams = { "action": "GetD2MAddressBook"};
		
		var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
		
		var returnAddressList = undefined;
		
		thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (response) {
			
			if (response.ErrorCode != 0) 
			{
				alert(response.ErrorMessage);
			} 
			else 
			{
				
				var json = DecodeReturnString(response.Data);
				returnAddressList = json.ReturnAddressList;		
				returnAddressList.forEach(function (returnAddress) {
					var x = returnAddress;
					console.log(x);
				});
			}
		});
		return returnAddressList;
	}

// setD2MCheckboxAsChecked() // returns void
	function setD2MCheckboxAsChecked()
	{
		var checkIsLoadedInterval = setInterval(function(){
								
		var checkIsLoaded =  $('#DirectToMobileShipmentID');
	
		if (checkIsLoaded)
		{
			$('#DirectToMobileShipmentID').prop( "checked", true );
			clearInterval(checkIsLoadedInterval);								
		}
	    },50);
	}

// thinClientAPIRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns jqXHR
	function thinClientAPIRequest (method, data, isAsync) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = client.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = client.getAuthorizationToken();
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken });
    };

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {   
        if (location == '/') document.location = '#!/shipping';
        
        $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function () { $('div[role="alert"]:visible').hide(); })
        $('body').on('click', 'input[ng-click="vm.opendeliverDate()"], button[ng-click="vm.opendeliverDate()"]', translateDates);
        $('a[href="/Manage"][title="Manage"]').remove();

        
        setInterval(function() {
            translateDates();
            $('button').each(function() {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let text = $(this).text().trim();
                let month = text.split(' ')[0];

                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-info.uib-datepicker-current.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Today') {
                        $(this).text('Aujourd\'hui');  // Translate "Today" to French
                    }
                });
                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-danger.uib-clear.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Clear') {
                        $(this).text('Effacer');  // Translate "Clear" to French
                    }
                });

                $('button.btn.btn-sm.btn-success.pull-right.uib-close.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (text === 'Close') {
                        $(this).text('Fermer');  // Translate "Close" to French
                    }
                });
                
        
                for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                    if (month.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                        $(this).prop('disabled', true);  // Disable the button if it contains a month name
                        return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                    }
                }
            });
        }, 1500);

            translateElements2: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).val();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },
            translateElements: function(selector, translation, replacer) {
                $(selector).each(function() {
                    var text = $(this).text().trim();
                    if (translation[text] !== undefined) {
                        replacer.call(this, text, translation[text]);
                    }
                });
            },

            replaceText: function(oldText, newText) {
                this.innerHTML = this.innerHTML.replace(oldText, newText);
            },

            replaceValue: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).val(newText);
            },

            replaceLabel: function(oldText, newText) {
                $(this).attr('label', newText);
            },

            handleSpecificCases: function() {
                $('h5:contains("No commodities added")').text('Aucune marchandise ajoutée');
                $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;of&nbsp;&nbsp;1") {
                        $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;1');
                    }
                });
            },
        };

            client.init();

        }, 1000);

            case '/shipping':

                break;
            case '/history':
                $("h4:first").text("Historique");
                
                break;
            // Add more cases as needed
        }

// translateDates() // returns undefined
        function  translateDates() {
            const monthMapping = {
                "January": "Janvier",
                "February": "Février",
                "March": "Mars",
                "April": "Avril",
                "May": "Mai",
                "June": "Juin",
                "July": "Juillet",
                "August": "Août",
                "September": "Septembre",
                "October": "Octobre",
                "November": "Novembre",
                "December": "Décembre"
                };
                
                const dayMapping = {
                  'Mon': 'Lun',
                  'Tue': 'Mar',
                  'Wed': 'Mer',
                  'Thu': 'Jeu',
                  'Fri': 'Ven',
                  'Sat': 'Sam',
                  'Sun': 'Dim'
                };


                const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
                $("small[aria-label]").each(function() {
                  var day = $(this).text().trim();
                  var translatedDay = dayMapping[day];
                  if (translatedDay) {
                    $(this).text(translatedDay);
                  }
                });
                
                $("strong").each(function() {
                  var dateText = $(this).text().trim();
                  var month = dateText.split(' ')[0];
                  var translatedMonth = monthMapping[month];
                  if (translatedMonth) {
                      var updatedText = dateText.replace(month, translatedMonth);
                      $(this).text(updatedText);
                  }
                });

                var buttonLeft = document.querySelector('.uib-left');
                var buttonRight = document.querySelector('.uib-right');
        
                if (buttonLeft) {
                    $(buttonLeft).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('previous');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }
        
                if (buttonRight) {
                    $(buttonRight).off('click.custom').on('click.custom', function() {
                       return getCurrentMonthYear('next');
                        // Your logic here
                    });
                }


            }

// getCurrentMonthYear(action) // returns monthYear
            function getCurrentMonthYear(action) {
                const frenchMonths = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                let monthYear = null;
               
                $('strong.ng-binding').each(function() {
                    let text = $(this).text();
                    
                    for (let i = 0; i < frenchMonths.length; i++) {
                        if (text.includes(frenchMonths[i])) {
                            if(action=='next') {
                                $(this).text(getNextMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            } else {
                                $(this).text(getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(text));
                            }
                            return false;  // Break out of the .each() loop
                        }
                    }
                });
                
                return monthYear;
            }

// getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) // returns month + ' ' + year
            function getNextMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is December.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 11) {
                    // Increment the year and reset the month to January.
                    year++;
                    month = monthNamesFr[0];
                } else {
                    // Get the next month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex + 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

// getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) // returns month + ' ' + year
            function getPreviousMonthYearInFrench(dateStr) {
                var monthNamesFr = ['Janvier', 'Février', 'Mars', 'Avril', 'Mai', 'Juin', 'Juillet', 'Août', 'Septembre', 'Octobre', 'Novembre', 'Décembre'];
                var splitDate = dateStr.split(' ');
                var month = splitDate[0];
                var year = splitDate[1];
            
                var currentMonthIndex = monthNamesFr.indexOf(month);
                
                // Check if the current month is January.
                if (currentMonthIndex === 0) {
                    // Decrement the year and set the month to December.
                    year--;
                    month = monthNamesFr[11];
                } else {
                    // Get the previous month.
                    month = monthNamesFr[currentMonthIndex - 1];
                }
                
                return month + ' ' + year;
            }

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(translateToFrench['Months'])) {

// AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
    this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
       
        $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
            // Check if the label has the correct style and text
            if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;"+ (packageIndex)) {
                // Change the label's text
                $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;' + (packageIndex+1));
            }
        });
    }

// RemovePackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
    this.RemovePackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
       
        $('label.control-label.no-left-padding.ng-binding').each(function() {
            // Check if the label has the correct style and text
            if ($(this).attr('style') === "text-align: center" && $(this).html() === "&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;"+ (packageIndex+2)) {
                // Change the label's text
                $(this).html('&nbsp;de&nbsp;&nbsp;' + (packageIndex+1));
            }
        });
    }

// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns void
  this.PageLoaded = function (location)
  {
    vm = this.vm;
    GetUserContext();
    console.log(vm)

    if (location === '/batchdetail')
    {
      $('body').delegate('#voidBReference', 'click', function ()
      {
        voidBatchJS(this);
      });
    }
    if (location === '/batchmanager')
    {
      console.log(userContext)
      $('body').delegate('#voidBReference', 'click', function ()
      {
        voidBatchJS(this);
      });

      $('body').delegate('#printPSlip', 'change', function ()
      {
        console.log("I have been changed..." + $('#printPSlip').is(":checked"))
      })
    }
    if (location === '/history')
    {
      $('body').delegate('.void-all-btn', 'click', function (e)
      {
        VoidAll(e.currentTarget);
      });

      $('body').delegate('.RePrint-AMP-btn', 'click', function (e)
      {
        RePrintAMP(e.currentTarget);
      });

      // $('body').delegate('#VoidAll', 'click', function ()
      // {
      //   VoidAll(this);
      // });
      $('body').delegate('#CancelCloseModal', 'click', function ()
      {
        CloseModalClose();
      });
      $('body').delegate('#VoidReal', 'click', function ()
      {
        VoidReal();
      });
    }
    if (location === '/shipping')
    {
      var interval = setInterval(function ()
      {
        var $service = $('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]');
        var loaded = $service.length;
        if (loaded)
        {
          $('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]').removeClass("service");
          $('body').delegate('#AddMultiplePackages', 'click', function ()
          {
            AddMultiplePackagesModel();
          });

          $('body').delegate('#MultiCloseModal', 'click', function ()
          {
            MultiCloseModal();
          });

          $('body').delegate('#AddMultiPackagesReal', 'click', function ()
          {
            AddMultiPackagesReal();
          });

          $('body').delegate('#Split', 'click', function ()
          {
            Split();
          });

          $('body').delegate('#AddAll', 'click', function ()
          {
            AddAll();
          });
          clearInterval(interval);
        }
      }, 50);
    }



  }

// editableTable() // returns void
  function editableTable()
  {
    const celdas = document.querySelectorAll("#miTabla td");
    celdas.forEach(celda =>
    {
      celda.addEventListener("dblclick", function ()
      {
        if (this.cellIndex === this.parentElement.cells.length - 1)
        {
          return;
        }
        if (this.cellIndex === 2)
        {
          // QTY
          return;
        }

        const texto = this.textContent;
        this.innerHTML = "";

        const input = document.createElement("input");
        input.type = "text";
        input.value = texto;
        this.appendChild(input);
        input.select();

        input.addEventListener("blur", function ()
        {
          this.parentElement.textContent = this.value;
          this.remove();
        });
      });
    });
  }

// this.PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
  this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {
    var url = new URL(window.location.href);
    console.log(url);
    if (url.hash.includes("batchReference"))
    {
      vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = "Batch-Manual";
      var misc = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference20"]');
      console.log(misc);
    }
    console.log(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
    if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol.indexOf("SHIPCONSOLE") !== -1){
        console.log("Fedex");
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != "US"){
            console.log("International")
            let commodities = [];
            let test = [];
            let description = new Map();
            let currIndex = 0;
            shipmentRequest.Packages.forEach((item, index) => {
                if(item.CommodityContents !== null && item.CommodityContents !== undefined && item.CommodityContents !== []){
                    item.CommodityContents.forEach((commodity, commindex) => {
                        if(description.get(commodity.Description) !== undefined){
                            test[description.get(commodity.Description)].Quantity = String(parseInt(test[description.get(commodity.Description)].Quantity) + parseInt(commodity.Quantity));
                            console.log("Adding: " + commodity.Description)
                            console.log(commodity.Quantity)
                        } else {
                            
                            description.set(commodity.Description, currIndex);
                            let tempCommodity = {
                                UnitValue: commodity.UnitValue,
                                UnitWeight: commodity.UnitWeight,
                                QuantityUnitMeasure: commodity.QuantityUnitMeasure,
                                ExportQuantityUnitMeasure1: commodity.ExportQuantityUnitMeasure1,
                                ExportQuantityUnitMeasure2: commodity.ExportQuantityUnitMeasure2,
                                LicenseUnitValue: commodity.LicenseUnitValue,
                                DdtcUnitMeasure: commodity.DdtcUnitMeasure,
                                Origin: commodity.Origin,
                                OriginCountry: commodity.OriginCountry,
                                ProductCode: commodity.ProductCode,
                                HarmonizedCode: commodity.HarmonizedCode,
                                Quantity: commodity.Quantity,
                                Description: commodity.Description,
                                LicenseExpirationDate: commodity.LicenseExpirationDate,
                                NaftaRvcAvgStartDate: commodity.NaftaRvcAvgStartDate,
                                nAFTARVCAvgEndDate: commodity.nAFTARVCAvgEndDate
                            }
                            let anotherRandom = Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 12);
                            let NewCommodity =
                            {
                              "UnitValue": commodity.UnitValue,
                              "UnitWeight": commodity.UnitWeight,
                              "QuantityUnitMeasure": "PC",
                              "ExportQuantityUnitMeasure1": "PC",
                              "ExportQuantityUnitMeasure2": "PC",
                              "LicenseUnitValue": {
                                "Currency": "USD"
                              },
                              "DdtcUnitMeasure": "PC",
                              "packageIndex": commindex,
                              "Origin": {
                                "AddressBookIdToProcess": null
                              },
                              "OriginCountry": commodity.OriginCountry,
                              "ProductCode": commodity.ProductCode,
                              "HarmonizedCode": commodity.HarmonizedCode,
                              "Quantity": commodity.Quantity,
                              "Description": commodity.Description,
                              "LicenseExpirationDate": null,
                              "NaftaRvcAvgStartDate": null,
                              "nAFTARVCAvgEndDate": null,
                              "$$hashKey": "object:" + commindex + "1" + anotherRandom
                            };
        
                            test[currIndex] = NewCommodity;
                            console.log("Adding new comm");
                            console.log(JSON.stringify(test, null, 2))
                            currIndex+=1;
                        }
                    })
                }
                
                //commodities.push(item.CommodityContents)
                shipmentRequest.Packages[index].CommodityContents = []
            })
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityContents = test;
            console.log(JSON.stringify(test, null, 2))
        } else {
            console.log("Domestic")
        }
        
    }

// this.PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
  this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest)
  {
    try
    {
      //alert = function(){}
      this.vm.getWeight();

    }
    catch (error)
    {
      console.log("Error getting weight")
    }
    if (!shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1)
    {
      client.alert.Danger("Loaded Value " + loadValue + " not found")
    } else
    {
      const Lines = JSON.parse(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1);
      Lines.forEach(line =>
      {
        const fila = document.createElement("tr");
        fila.innerHTML = `
            <td>${line.LineNo}</td>
            <td>${line.ItemNo}</td>
            <td>${line.TotalOrderQuantity}</td>
            <td>${line.SaleUnitOfMeasure}</td>
            <td>${line.SaleUnitPrice}</td>
            <td>${line.ItemDescription}</td>
            <td></td>
            <td>${line.UnitWeight}</td>
            <td></td>
            <td>0</td>
            <td>0</td>
            <td><button class='btn btn-xs btn-success glyphicon glyphicon-plus'></button></td>
            <td hidden>${line.IsKitOrBundle}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.KitDetails ? JSON.stringify(line.KitDetails) : "[]"}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.CountryOfOrigin : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportCurrencyCode : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportTariffCode : ""}</td>
            <td hidden>${line.InternationalDetails ? line.InternationalDetails.ExportUnitPrice : ""}</td>
            `;
        if (line.IsKitOrBundle && line.KitDetails == null)
        {
          client.alert.Danger("WARNING: Kit Details are empty when Commodity Set to Kit");
        }
        document.querySelector("#miTabla").appendChild(fila);
      });
      editableTable();

      const buttons = document.querySelectorAll("#miTabla button");
      buttons.forEach(button =>
      {
        button.addEventListener("click", function ()
        {
          const fila = this.parentElement.parentElement;
          AddCommodity(fila, 1, 0);
        });
      });
      const tabla = document.querySelector("#miTabla");
      tabla.classList.remove("hidden");
    }
    console.log(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate)
    var today = new Date();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Day = today.getDate();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Year = today.getFullYear();
    shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipdate.Month = today.getMonth() + 1;
    if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != null && shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country != 'US')
    {
      for (var ii = 0; ii < shipmentRequest.Packages.length; ii++)
      {
        shipmentRequest.Packages[ii].CommercialInvoiceMethod = 1;
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country == 'GB')
        {
            console.log(shipmentRequest.Packages[ii]);
            shipmentRequest.Packages[ii].AdditionalHardcopyDocumentation = false;
        }
      }
      
    }

  }

// PreRate(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreRate = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        
        let tpb = $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').first();

        if ($(tpb).prop('checked') === true)
      
        {
      
          //uncheck the box before rating
      
          //use .click instead of .prop('checked') as .click will update the VM
      
          $(tpb).click();
      
       
      
          //set a global variable to access later
      
          tpbChecked = true;
      
        }

    }

// PostRate(shipmentRequest, rateResults) // returns undefined
this.PostRate = function (shipmentRequest, rateResults) {
         //if the global variable tpbChecked has a value, check the box after rating.

        if (tpbChecked)
        {
            $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').first().click();
            //clean up
            tpbChecked = null;
        }
    }

// PostSearchHistory(packages) // returns undefined
this.PostSearchHistory = function(packages) {
    var checkExist = setInterval(function ()
        {
          if ($('table[ng-table="vm.tableParamsForDetailed"] tr').length > 1)
          {
            clearInterval(checkExist);
            $('table[ng-table="vm.tableParamsForDetailed"] tr:gt(1)').find('td:eq(2) > div:not(.ng-hide)').html(function() 
            {
                var trackingN = $(this).text().trim();
                
                
              if(trackingN.startsWith('1Z')) {
              return "<a href=https://wwwapps.ups.com/WebTracking/track?track=yes&trackNums=" + $(this).text().trim() + "&requester=ST/trackdetails target='_new'>" + $(this).text().trim() + "</a>";
              }   else {
              return "<a href=https://online.chrobinson.com/tracking/#/?trackingNumber=" + $(this).text().trim() + "&requester=ST/trackdetails target='_new'>" + $(this).text().trim() + "</a>";
              }
            });
          }
        }, 100);
    }

// this.AddEmailToNotification(event) // returns void
    this.AddEmailToNotification = function(event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = GetShipmentEmailAddresses(this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults);
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];

        if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {

        if (location == '/') {
            var w = window.location.href + "batchmanager";
            window.location.replace(w);
        }

        if (location == '/batchmanager') {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                $.globalEval('var userContext;');

                var dataObject = {};
                dataObject.Action = "GetDealerId";
                dataObject.Content = "";
                debugger;
                var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(dataObject), UserContext: client.userContext };
                clientService.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).done(function (jsonData) {
                    debugger;
                    //console.log(jsonData.Data);
                    $('body').find('a[ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]').first().trigger('click').promise().done(function (e) {
                        ProcessDealerId(jsonData.Data);
                    });
                });
            }); //end document.ready
        }

        if (location == '/batchdetail') {
            $(document).ready(function () {
                try {
                    $('body').delegate('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]', 'click', function (e) {
                        var waitForTable = setInterval(function () {
                            /* The spanTotalBatchItems element text defaults to a value of 0, need to wait until it changes before we continue. */
                            if (($('#spanTotalBatchItems').length > 0) && ($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text() != "0")) {
                                var currentDate = new Date();
                                var totalBatchItems = parseInt($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text());

                                /* Once this condition is met, we can remove the rows we don't want. */
                                if ($('#tableBatchDetails tr').length >= totalBatchItems) {
                                    clearInterval(waitForTable);
                                    //console.log('table rows condition met.');
                                    /* Loop the table rows. */
                                    $('#tableBatchDetails tr:gt(0)').each(function (x, y) {
                                        var tdDate = new Date($(this).find('td:eq(1)').text());
                                        if (tdDate < currentDate) {
                                            $(this).remove();
                                        }
                                    }).promise().done(function (e) {
                                        $('#tableBatchDetails').show();
                                        var i = $('#tableBatchDetails tr').length;
                                        $('#spanTotalBatchItems').text(i);
                                    });
                                } //end if ($('#tableBatchDetails tr').length >= totalBatchItems) 

                            } //end if (($('#spanTotalBatchItems').length > 0) && ($('#spanTotalBatchItems').text() != "0")) 

                        }, 250);
                    });

                    /* Event handler for the 'View Labels' button. */
                    $('body').delegate('#buttonViewCheckedLabels', 'click', function (e) {
                        //prevent the subsequent listeners from firing
                        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
                        // console.log("Click");
                        ViewCheckedLabels();
                        //   $('#tableBatchDetails').find('input[type=checkbox]:checked').each(function () 
                        //   { 
                        //     ViewCheckedLabels();
                        //   });
                    }); //end button delegate

                    /* Trigger the click of the 'All' button.  Maybe in the future add an id to the element to make the code a bit more readable. */
                    $('a[ng-model="vm.itemsPerPage"][ng-click="vm.itemPerPageChanged(0)"]').trigger('click');


                }
                catch (err) {
                    console.error(err.message);
                }
            }); //end document.ready
        }

    } //end PageLoaded

// ViewCheckedLabels() // returns void
    function ViewCheckedLabels() {
        $('#tableBatchDetails').find('input[type=checkbox]:checked').each(function () {
            // console.log("Print");
            var btnPrint = $(this).closest('tr').find('input[type="button"][value="Print"]').first().trigger('click');
        });
    }

// ProcessDealerId(DealerId) // returns void
    function ProcessDealerId(DealerId) {
        var WaitForDealerId;

        var tdDealerId = $('td:contains(' + DealerId + ')').first();

        if (tdDealerId.length == 0) {
            /* Wait 150 milliseconds before trying to find the dealer id in the batch list.  A better way would be to get the number of batch items, then wait for that number of rows to show.  Work on that next. */
            WaitForDealerId = setTimeout(function () {
                ProcessDealerId(DealerId);
            }, 150)
        }
        else {
            //console.log('DealerID Found.');
            clearTimeout(WaitForDealerId);
            $(tdDealerId).find('a').first().trigger('click');
        }

    }

// ViewCheckedLabels() // returns void
    function ViewCheckedLabels() {
        const batchItemArr = [];
        $('#tableBatchDetails').find('input[type=checkbox]:checked').each(function () {
            //debugger;
            console.log("Print");
            var btnPrint = $(this).closest('tr').find('input[type="button"][value="Print"]').first().trigger('click');
            batchItemArr.push($(this).attr('data'))
        });
        var dataObject = {};
        dataObject.Action = "RemoveBatchItem";
        let bLen = batchItemArr.length;
        for (let i = 0; i < bLen; i++) {
            if (i == 0) {
                dataObject.Content = batchItemArr[i];
            } else {
                dataObject.Content += "," + batchItemArr[i];
            }
        }
        var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(dataObject), UserContext: client.userContext };
        //debugger;
        clientService.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false)
    }

// Source: Hyve Solutions (HYVE)_Hyve_Solutions_CBR_1593.cs
// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns undefined
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
		//alert("Country " + nameaddress.Country);
		
		var clientContext;
		var resp;

        $.ajax({
            type: "GET",
            url: "api/usercontext/GET",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            success: function (result) {
                debugger;
                clientContext = result;
            },
            error: function (jqXhr, exception) {
                debugger;
            }
        });
     
        $.ajax({
            type: "POST",
            url: "api/ShippingService/UserMethod",
            async: false,
            cache: false,
            dataType: "json",           
            data: { UserContext: clientContext , "Data": nameaddress.Country},    
            success: function (response) {
                debugger;
				resp = JSON.stringify(response);
				resp = JSON.parse(resp);
				if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
				{
					var IOR = JSON.parse(resp.Data);
					shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ImporterOfRecord = IOR;
				}
				else
				{
					alert('No available Importer of Records');
				}
            },
            error: function (xhr) {
                debugger;
                alert(xhr.responseText);
            }
        });
		
	}
