// PassWorldeaseTrackingNumber(docboxtrackingNumber) // returns void
    function PassWorldeaseTrackingNumber(docboxtrackingNumber) {
        debugger;

        var jsonData;

        var dataObject = {
            ConsolidationTrackingNumber: docboxtrackingNumber,
            UserContext: clientService1.userContext
        };

        var payload = JSON.stringify(dataObject);

        debugger;

        var data = {
            Data: payload,
            UserContext: clientService1.userContext
        };

        // Show the spinner
        $("#loadingSpinner").show();

        var ajaxRequest = clientService1.thinclientService1APIRequest('UserMethod', data, true);

        ajaxRequest.done(function (data) {
            jsonData = data.Data;
            $("#loadingSpinner").hide();
            console.log(jsonData);
            setTimeout(function () {
                debugger;
                var dataObj = JSON.parse(jsonData.replaceAll('&quot;', '"'));
                var htmlString = '<div>Total Invoice Amount: '
                    + dataObj.Total
                    + ' '
                    + dataObj.TotalUOM
                    + '<br /><hr />';
                var i = 0, len = dataObj.TrackingNumbers.length;
                for (; i < len; i++) {
                    var currentTracking = dataObj.TrackingNumbers[i];
                    var itemString = currentTracking.TrackingNumber
                    htmlString += itemString + "<br />";
                }
                htmlString += '</div>';
                $('#infoModalLabel').html(htmlString);
                $('#infoModal').modal('show');

            }, 50);
        }).fail(function (xhr, status, error) {
            console.error("Error:", error);
            $("#loadingSpinner").hide();
            alert("Failed to get data.");

        }).always(function () {
            // Hide the spinner regardless of success or failure
            $("#loadingSpinner").hide();
        });
    }

// Source: MarkenLLP2 (MLLP2)_Inbound Returns CBR_CA_TO_US_1915.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        
        StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
        $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
        
        if (location == '/') document.location = '#!/shipping';
        else if (location == '/shipping') {
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
            this.Shipping();
        }
    }

// Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function() {
        $(document).ready(function() {
            client.setDivReference3();

        })

        $('body').delegate('select[name="ConsigneeReference_txt"]', 'change', this.vm, consigneeReferenceOnChange);

        function consigneeReferenceOnChange(e) {
            
            client.vm = e.data;
            if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(3, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Refrigerated')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(5, true);
            else if(e.target.value == 'string:Ambient/Refrigerated Combo Box') 
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Frozen')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(6, false, true);

        }

        function changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(weightAmount, isHidden, isRequired) {
            $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val(weightAmount).change();
            if (isHidden) client.$divReference3.hide();
            else client.$divReference3.show();
            client.$divReference3.find('input').css('border-color', isRequired ? '#a94442' : client.defaultMiscReference3BorderColor);
            client.vm.fieldOptions.MiscReference3.IsRequired = isRequired;
        }

    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
         if (location == '/shipping') {
            StudyReferenceCodeModal.InitElements(false);
            $('#LoadStudyReferenceCodeData').click();
            Tools.HideLoader();
         }
 
        client?.$divReference3?.hide();

        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value; //Study Reference code

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value;  //Protocol Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2 = this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value;  //Site Number

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4 = true;
        
        
            $(document).ready(function() {
               
             $("#OK").on("click", function() {
            
                 var selectedValue = $('#selectShipper').val();
                var shipperReferenceVal = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                var arrayOrders = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(shipperReferenceVal);
                if(arrayOrders.includes(selectedValue)){
                     var selectedIndex = arrayOrders.indexOf(selectedValue); 
                     var selectedStudy= arrayOrders[selectedIndex];
                     //Populating the entered Study Reference code in the Shipper reference field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val(selectedStudy);
                     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]').val();
                     
                     var miscReference1Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                     var arrayOrders1 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference1Val);
                     var selectedProtocol = arrayOrders1[selectedIndex]; 
                     //Populating the corresponding Protocol number in the Misc reference 1 field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val(selectedProtocol);
                      shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference1"]').val();
                      
                     var miscReference2Val = $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                     var arrayOrders2 = Tools.GetUniqueArrayFromString(miscReference2Val);
                     var selectedSite= arrayOrders2[selectedIndex]; 
                     //Populating the corresponding Site number in the Misc reference 2 field.
                     $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val(selectedSite);
                     shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2= $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference2"]').val();
                }
                else
                 {
                     alert("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                     throw new Error("Please contact Marken directly to schedule your pickup.");
                 }
        
                //Calling the SBR Usermethod to get the Shipper Friendly name.    
                 GetUserShipper(selectedStudy,shipmentRequest);
                
                StudyReferenceCodeModal.CloseDialogWithoutSaving();
                
            });
        
        });
     
    }

// GetUserShipper(selectedStudy, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
function GetUserShipper(selectedStudy,shipmentRequest) {
       var jsonData;
       var dataObject = {
                    StudyReferenceCode:selectedStudy, 
                    UserContext: client.userContext
                };
 
                var payload = JSON.stringify(dataObject);
                debugger;
                var data = { Data: payload, UserContext: client.userContext };
 
                var ajaxRequest = client.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, true);
            
                ajaxRequest.done(function (data) {
 
             jsonData = data.Data;
                console.log(jsonData);
               $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"]').val(jsonData);
               shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper=$('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Shipper"] option:selected').val().split(":")[1];

                });
            
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function() {
        $(document).ready(function() {
            client.setDivReference3();

        })

        $('body').delegate('select[name="ConsigneeReference_txt"]', 'change', this.vm, consigneeReferenceOnChange);

        function consigneeReferenceOnChange(e) {
            
            client.vm = e.data;
            if (e.target.value == 'string:Ambient')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(1, true);
            else if (e.target.value == 'string:Refrigerated')
                changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(5, true);

        }

        function changeWeightAmountAndMiscReference3(weightAmount, isHidden, isRequired) {
            $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').val(weightAmount).change();
            if (isHidden) client.$divReference3.hide();
            else client.$divReference3.show();
            client.$divReference3.find('input').css('border-color', isRequired ? '#a94442' : client.defaultMiscReference3BorderColor);
            client.vm.fieldOptions.MiscReference3.IsRequired = isRequired;
        }

    }

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
          debugger;
        //If the user profile is EU to UK, then Pickup LatestTimeReady can be calculated.
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 == "2") {
          
            var MiscRef10 = formatNumberToTime(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference10);

            // Split the times into hours and minutes
            var parts1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference9.split(":");
            var parts2 = MiscRef10.split(":");

            // Parse the hours and minutes as integers
            var hours1 = parseInt(parts1[0], 10);
            var minutes1 = parseInt(parts1[1], 10);
            var hours2 = parseInt(parts2[0], 10);
            var minutes2 = parseInt(parts2[1], 10);

            // Add the hours and minutes together
            var totalHours = hours1 + hours2;
            var totalMinutes = minutes1 + minutes2;

            // Handle carryover from minutes to hours
            if (totalMinutes >= 60) {
                totalHours += Math.floor(totalMinutes / 60);
                totalMinutes %= 60;
            }

            // Format the result as "hh:mm"
            var result = totalHours.toString().padStart(2, '0') + ':' + totalMinutes.toString().padStart(2, '0');

            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 = result;
            
                if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11 > shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference12) 
                {
                alert("Calculated Pickup Latest Time Ready is later than the Maximum Pickup Latest Time Ready for the user.");
                throw new Error("Calculated Pickup Latest Time Ready is later than the Maximum Pickup Latest Time Ready for the user.");
                }

             //Format the number to HH:MM    
             function formatNumberToTime(number) {
            
                            if (number < 0 || number > 23) {
                                return "Invalid hour";
                            }
                            // Use String interpolation to format the number as "X:00"
                            return `${number}:00`;
                        }
                        
                        
            $('[ng-click="vm.createPickupRequestClick()"]').trigger('click');
            // Assigning the Pickup request properties.
            this.vm.pickup.ContactName = $('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Contact"]').val();
            this.vm.pickup.ContactPhone = $('input[ng-model="nameaddress.Phone"]').val();
            this.vm.pickup.PaymentType = "PAY_BY_SHIPPER_ACCOUNT";
            this.vm.pickup.EarliestTimeReady = $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference9"]').val();
            this.vm.pickup.LatestTimeReady = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11;

            if (this.vm.pickup != null) {
                setTimeout(() => {
                    $('[ng-click="vm.ok()"]').trigger('click');
                }, 100);
            }
        }

    }

// PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns void
     this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
       
        this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[0].Value=shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference; //Study Reference code

        this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[1].Value=shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1;  //Protocol Number

        this.vm.profile.UserInformation.Address.CustomData[2].Value= shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2;  //Site Number

    }

// Shipping() // returns void
this.Shipping = function() {
    updateDryIceRegulationSet();
    function updateDryIceRegulationSet() {
        debugger;
        $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.hazmatdryIceBtn"]', 'click', function() {
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var $dryIceRegulationSet = $('[ng-model="vm.dryIceInfo.DryIceRegulationSet"]');
                if ($dryIceRegulationSet.length) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $dryIceRegulationSet.find('option[label="Regulations Not Specified"]').remove();
                }
            }, 50);
        });
    }
};

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        //debugger;
        this.vm.NotificationAddressEmail = this.AddEmailToNotification;

        originCustomData = getCustomData(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress);
        if (originCustomData.length) {
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = getKeyValue('Custom3', originCustomData);
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Contact;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1 = getKeyValue('Custom2', originCustomData);
        }

        $('body').delegate('div[ng-if="vm.rateResults.length > 0"] tr td a', 'click', serviceUpgrade);

        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationEmail = true;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = getUserName();
        if(getUserName() == 'SRPBulletin@mskcc.org' || this.vm.profile.Name == 'FIFTYTHIRDSTREET_Profile'){
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail = true;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = getUserName();
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationEmail = true;
            shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = getUserName();
        }

        var interval = setInterval(function() {
            var shipperReference = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ShipperReference"]')
            var miscReference3 = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference3"]')

            var loaded = shipperReference.length && miscReference3.length;
            if (loaded){
                clearInterval(interval);
                if (getKeyValue('custom5', originCustomData) == 1) {
                    // disable shipper reference on general and reference tab
                    $('div[property="ShipperReference"] input').prop('disabled', true);
                }
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// AddEmailToNotification(event) // returns void
    this.AddEmailToNotification = function(event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = getShipmentEmailAddresses(this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults);
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];

        if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) 
    {            
        //Services configured in Pending Shipments Profile Field Options
        var backup2DADomesticService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17; //UPSAPI.UPS.2DA        
        var backupNDADomesticService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference18; //UPSAPI.UPS.NDA        
        var backupExpeditedIntlService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference19; //UPSAPI.UPS.EXPEDITED        
        var backupExpressIntlService = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20; //UPSAPI.UPS.EXPRESS        

        $('body').on('click', 'table[aria-describedby="Pending Shipments"] input[type="button"]', this.vm, 
        function(e) 
        {
            $('input[ng-model="vm.deliverDate.value"]').val(e.data.currentShipment.Packages[0].MiscReference5).change();
            if (e.data.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service) 
            {
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference8"]').val(e.data.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference17"]').val(backup2DADomesticService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference18"]').val(backupNDADomesticService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19"]').val(backupExpeditedIntlService).change();
                $('input[type=text][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').val(backupExpressIntlService).change();
            }
        });
    };

// clickedPage(e) // returns undefined
        function clickedPage(e) {
            if (e.target.classList.contains('active')) return;
            this.pagination.currentPage = parseInt(e.target.innerText);
            this.buildPage();
        }        

// focusNext() // returns undefined
        function focusNext () {
            var activeNgModel = document.activeElement.attributes['ng-model'].value;
            var textArray = $('[type="text"]');
            for (var i = 0; i < textArray.length - 1; i++) {
                var ngModel = textArray[i].attributes['ng-model'].value;
                if (ngModel == activeNgModel) {                    
                    textArray[i+1].focus();
                    return;
                }
            }
            $('button[name="addReturnItem"]').focus();
        }

        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1.ShowConsignee) {

// function DimensionChange(packaging) // returns undefined
    this.DimensionChange = function (packaging) {
        for (var i = 0; i < this.packageIndex + 1; i++) {
            this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Packaging = packaging;

            if (packaging == "LETTER") {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Dimensions.Height = '';
                this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Dimensions.Length = '';
                this.currentShipment.Packages[i].Dimensions.Width = '';
            }
        }

        //make sure dims are required
        this.fieldOptions["Dimensions.Length"].IsRequired = packaging != "LETTER";
        this.fieldOptions["Dimensions.Width"].IsRequired = packaging != "LETTER";
        this.fieldOptions["Dimensions.Height"].IsRequired = packaging != "LETTER";

        generalDimensionLength.prop('disabled', packaging == "LETTER");
        generalDimensionWidth.prop('disabled', packaging == "LETTER");
        generalDimensionHeight.prop('disabled', packaging == "LETTER");
    };

// function disableConsigneeNameAddress(disabled) // returns undefined
    function disableConsigneeNameAddress(disabled) {
        if ($consigneeNameAddress !== undefined) {
            $consigneeNameAddress.find('input').each(function () {
                var type = $(this).attr('type');
                if (type == 'checkbox') {
				    $(this).prop('disabled', disabled);
                } else {
                    //alert($(this).prop('name'));
                    if ($(this).prop('name') !== 'phone') $(this).prop('readonly', disabled);
                }
            });
        }
		
    }

// function dismissAlertDialog() // returns undefined
    function dismissAlertDialog() {
        $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) {
            $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
        })
    }

// function updateDropDownMenu() // returns void
    function updateDropDownMenu() {
        angular.element('a:contains("End of Day")').hide();
        //angular.element('a:contains("History")').hide();

        var separator = null;
        var menus = ['Scan Ship', 'Batch Manager', 'Create a Batch', 'AddressBook', 'Distribution List'];
        angular.element('.dropdown-menu li').each(function () {
            var itemText = $(this).text();
            if (itemText === '') {
                separator = $(this);
            }

            if (menus.includes($(this).text())) {
                $(this).hide();
                separator.hide();
            }
        });
    }

// function documentReady() // returns void
    function documentReady() {
        generalCarrierInstructions.hide();
        //generalDescription.hide();
        generalAllServices.hide();
        generalSpanSelectAll.hide();


        internationalWorldEaseHeading.hide();
        $internationalTab.find('div button').hide();
    }

// function disableConsigneeNameAddress(disabled) // returns void
    function disableConsigneeNameAddress(disabled) {
        if ($consigneeNameAddress !== undefined) {
            $consigneeNameAddress.find('input').each(function () {
                var type = $(this).attr('type');
                if (type == 'checkbox') {
                    $(this).prop('disabled', disabled);
                } else {
                    $(this).prop('readonly', disabled);
                }
            });
        }
    }

// function setFocus(element) // returns void
    function setFocus(element) {
        var ng = angular.element(element);
        if (ng.length > 0) {
            ng.focus();
        }
    }

// function clearAlert() // returns void
    function clearAlert() {
        var alertBox = $('div[role="alert"]');
        if (alertBox.length) {
            alertBox.find('.close').click();
        }
    }

// function sleep(milliseconds) // returns void
    function sleep(milliseconds) {
        const date = Date.now();
        let currentDate = null;
        do {
            currentDate = Date.now();
        } while (currentDate - date < milliseconds);
    }

// function appendCSS() // returns void
    function appendCSS() {
        var style = document.createElement('style');
        style.innerHTML = 'input:focus, textarea:focus, select:focus{background-color: #ffffcc;}';
        document.head.appendChild(style);
    }

            $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
        })
    }

// appendDownloadMenu() // returns undefined
    function appendDownloadMenu () {
        $('body').on('click', '#sws-menu-item', function(e) {
            $('#StrattonWarrenFileDownload').click();
        })
        
        downloadMenu = true;
        var html = [
            '<li class="dropdown">',

                    '<li id="sws-menu-item"><a>Stratton Warren File</a></li>',
                    '<li role="separator" class="divider"></li>',
                    '<li id="gl-menu-item"><a href="javascript:glCodeFileDownload()">GL Code File</a></li>',
                '</ul>',
            '</li>',
            '<li id="download-loading">',
                '<img src="/Content/img/spinner-transparent.gif" class="loading-spinner" />',
                '<span class="loading-text"> Loading...</span>',
            '</li>'
        ].join("\n");

        //$('div > div.navbar.navbar-default.navbar-fixed-top > div > div.navbar-collapse.collapse > ul').append(html);
        $('div > div.navbar.navbar-default.navbar-fixed-top > div > div.navbar-collapse.collapse > div > ul').append(html);
    }

// toggleDownloadLoading(downloading, menuOption) // returns undefined
    function toggleDownloadLoading(downloading, menuOption) {
        let menuItem = "";

        $('#download-loading').toggle();
        
        switch (menuOption) {
            case "SWS" : menuItem = "#sws-menu-item"; break;
            case "GLCODE" : menuItem = "#gl-menu-item"; break;
        }
        $(menuItem).toggleClass('disabled', downloading);
    }

// stateProvinceChange() // returns undefined
    function stateProvinceChange() {

        vm.addressName = nameAddress.attr('address-property-name');
        $('#nameAddressChange').click();
    }

// showModalDialog(thisRef, title, response, option) // returns undefined
    function showModalDialog(thisRef, title, response, option) {
        //debugger;
        // hide loading spinner
        toggleDownloadLoading(false, option);
        decodeReturnString(response);

        thisRef.AlertTitle = title;
        if (response.ErrorCode == 0) {
            thisRef.AlertMessage = response.Data;
        } else {
            thisRef.AlertMessage = response.ErrorMessage;
        }
        // setting dom values since ng-model isn't available
        var responseText = response.ErrorCode == 0 || !response.ErrorMessage  ? response.Data : response.ErrorMessage
        alertModal.find('h4').text(title);
        alertModal.find('p').text(responseText);
        alertModal.modal('show');
    }

// singleCheckbox() // returns undefined
    function singleCheckbox() {
        var $checkbox = $(this);
        if ($checkbox.is(':checked') && $checkbox.is('[name]')) {
            // the name of the box is retrieved using the .attr() method
            // as it is assumed and expected to be immutable
            var group = 'input:checkbox[name="' + $checkbox.attr("name") + '"]';

            // the checked state of the group/box on the other hand will change
            // and the current value is retrieved using .prop() method
            $(group).prop('checked', false);
            $checkbox.prop('checked', true);
        }
    }

// Source: Mimaki USA (MIMAKI)_Mimaki CBR_2455.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        if (location == '/shipping') this.Shipping();

    }

// Shipping() // returns undefined
    this.Shipping = function () {

        //uncomment this to auto get weight
        this.vm.getWeight = customGetWeight;
        debugger;

        function customGetWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration) {
                var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read'
                var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: this.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition, async: false }).responseJSON;
                
                if (ret != undefined) {
                    if (ret.ErrorCode == 0) {
                        this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                            "Amount": ret.Weight.toFixed(2),
                            "Units": ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                        };
                    }
                }
            }
        }

    }//end of this.shipping

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest) {

        //enable this to get weight auto at order load time
        this.vm.getWeight();
		debugger;
        //scroll selected service into view
        scrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);
        checkForCancelled(this.vm);
        sumCommodities();

        //scroll into view stuff
        function isIE() {
            return /*@cc_on!@*/false || !!document.documentMode;
        }

        function scrollIntoView(element, value) {
            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if (element.val() == value) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        var optionTop = element.find('[value="' + value + '"]').offset().top;
                        var selectTop = element.offset().top;
                        element.scrollTop(element.scrollTop() + (optionTop - selectTop));
                    }
                }, 50);

            }

        }

        function checkForCancelled(view) {

            var $misc19 = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference19"]');

            if (!isIE()) {
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    if ($misc19.length) {
                        clearInterval(interval);

                        if ($misc19.val() == "T") {
                            debugger;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisableShip = true;
                            //view.profile.ProfileSetting.DisablePendingShipment = true;
                            $("input[value=\"Ship (F12)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Rate (F9)\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            $("input[value=\"Save\"]").prop('disabled', true);
                            alert("This order is marked as Cancelled. Please load a new order");
                        }
                    }
                }, 50);

            }
        }
		

        function sumCommodities()
        {
            var commoditiesValue = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CommodityContents.map(m => +m.Quantity * +m.UnitValue.Amount);
            var commTotal = 0.00;
            if(!commoditiesValue || Array.isArray(commoditiesValue ) || arr.commoditiesValue  !== 0)
            {
                for (let i = 0; i < commoditiesValue.length; i++) {
                    commTotal += commoditiesValue[i];
                  }
            }
            $('#SumCommTotal').text('Commodity Total: $' + commTotal);
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        $('h1').removeClass('text-danger').removeClass('text-success');

        $('#SumCommTotal').text('Commodity Total: $');
		
        client.shipping.loadValue.focus();
        client.shipping.maintabfocus('General');
        client.shipping.subtabfocus('Consignee', 'Account/Tax');

        $("input[value=\"Ship (F12)\"]").prop('disabled', false);
        $("input[value=\"Rate (F9)\"]").prop('disabled', false);
        $("input[value=\"Save\"]").prop('disabled', false);
    }

// init() // returns undefined
        init: function () {

            String.prototype.focus = function () {
                if (!focus(this)) {
                    var interval = setInterval(function (selector) {
                        if (focus(selector)) clearInterval(interval)
                    }, 10, this)
                }

                function focus(selector) {
                    $(selector).focus();
                    return $(selector).length
                }
            };
        }

// maintabfocus(tabName) // returns undefined
            maintabfocus: function (tabName) {
                $('ul li[heading="' + tabName + '"] a').click()
            }

// subtabfocus(nameAddress, tabName) // returns undefined
            subtabfocus: function (nameAddress, tabName) {
                var index = tabName == 'Email' ? 0 : tabName == "Phone or Fax" ? 1 : 2;
                var interval = setInterval(function () {
                    var $ubtab = $('name-address[address-property-name="' + nameAddress + '"] ul li[index=' + index + '] a');
                    if ($ubtab.length) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        $ubtab.click();
                    }
                }, 10)
            }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined

// Shipping() // returns undefined
    this.Shipping = function () {
        
        var interval = setInterval(function () {
                loadText = ('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');  
                
                var loaded = loadText.length;
                
                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    setFocus(loadText);
                }
            }, 50);
            
        appendCSS();

        this.vm.loadWeight = loadWeight;
        
        function loadWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration === undefined) return;
            var scale = this.profile.ScaleConfiguration;
            var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read';
            var data = {
                'PortType': scale.ScaleDefinition.PortType,
                'Port': scale.Port,
                'UsbVid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbVid,
                'UsbPid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbPid,
                'RequestCommand': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestCommand,
                'BaudRate': scale.ScaleDefinition.BaudRate,
                'StopBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.StopBits,
                'Parity': scale.ScaleDefinition.Parity,
                'DataBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.DataBits,
                'RequestTimeout': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestTimeout,
                'HostAddress': scale.HostAddress,
                'RegexPattern': scale.ScaleDefinition.RegexPattern,
                'DeviceParser': scale.ScaleDefinition.DeviceParserType,
                'DeviceName': scale.ScaleDefinition.Name,
                'Handshake': scale.ScaleDefinition.Handshake,
                'RetryCount': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryCount,
                'RetryDelay': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryDelay
            };
            var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: data, async: false }).responseJSON;
            if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                    "Amount": ret.Weight,
                    "Units": ret.WeightUnit === null ? "LB" : ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()
                };


            } else {
                client.alert.Danger(this.translations.Common.ErrorCode + " : " + ret.ErrorCode + "  " + ret.ErrorMessage);
            }            
        }
    }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
        this.PreLoad = function (loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        this.vm.loadWeight();
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) {
        client.vm = this.vm;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = intPicker;
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 = intPacker;
        clearAlert();
        setFocus(loadText);      
    }

// AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns undefined
   this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {    
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference7 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference8 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8;
}

// InitElements() // returns object
            InitElements: function ()
            {
                $('div.top-tool-bar > div.pull-left')
                .append($('<button />')
                .addClass('btn btn-xs btn-primary')
                .attr('id', 'buttonPickPack')
                .text('Set Picker & Packer')
                .fadeIn());

                /* Set up all delegates from within this block. */
                $('body').delegate('#buttonPickPack', 'click', function (e)
                {
                    $('#divModalPickPack').show();                
                });
       
                $('body').delegate('#buttonClosePickPack', 'click', function (e)
                {
					intPicker = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference7"]').val()
					intPacker = $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference8"]').val()					
                    $('#divModalPickPack').hide();
                });

            } /* End InitElements */

this.Shipping = function () {
        
        var interval = setInterval(function () {
                loadText = ('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');  
                
                var loaded = loadText.length;
                
                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    setFocus(loadText);
                }
            }, 50);

        //};
        appendCSS();

        this.vm.loadWeight = loadWeight;
        
        function loadWeight() {
            if (this.profile.ScaleConfiguration === undefined) return;
            var scale = this.profile.ScaleConfiguration;
            var url = client.config.ClientSupportServiceUrl + '/api/Scale/Read';
            var data = {
                'PortType': scale.ScaleDefinition.PortType,
                'Port': scale.Port,
                'UsbVid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbVid,
                'UsbPid': scale.ScaleDefinition.UsbPid,
                'RequestCommand': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestCommand,
                'BaudRate': scale.ScaleDefinition.BaudRate,
                'StopBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.StopBits,
                'Parity': scale.ScaleDefinition.Parity,
                'DataBits': scale.ScaleDefinition.DataBits,
                'RequestTimeout': scale.ScaleDefinition.RequestTimeout,
                'HostAddress': scale.HostAddress,
                'RegexPattern': scale.ScaleDefinition.RegexPattern,
                'DeviceParser': scale.ScaleDefinition.DeviceParserType,
                'DeviceName': scale.ScaleDefinition.Name,
                'Handshake': scale.ScaleDefinition.Handshake,
                'RetryCount': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryCount,
                'RetryDelay': scale.ScaleDefinition.RetryDelay
            };
            var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: data, async: false }).responseJSON;
            if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].Weight = {
                    "Amount": ret.Weight,
                    "Units": ret.WeightUnit === null ? "LB" : ret.WeightUnit.toUpperCase()

            } else {

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams) {
        debugger;
        var picker = "";
        var packer = "";

          picker = prompt("Picker ID", "" );
          packer = prompt("Packer ID", "");
          shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7 = "Picker :" + picker;
          shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8 = "Packer :" + packer;
          
            if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16 == "true")
            {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17 = "TRUE";
            }

    }

// Source: Nexus (NEXUS)_Nexus CBR 2.3 Fix_1760.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
        if (location === '/shipping')
        {
            var loadInterval = setInterval(function()
            {
                loadText = $('[ng-model="vm.loadValue"]');
                if (loadText.length)
                {
                    clearInterval(loadInterval);
                    setFocus(loadText);
                }
            }, 50);
            $('body').delegate('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]', 'keydown', function(e) {
                if (e.keyCode == 13 && $(this).val().indexOf(".") !== -1)
                {
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Width"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[1]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Height"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[2]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]').val($(this).val().split('.')[0]).change();
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').focus();
                }
            });
        }
    };

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        //Setting the return address on Dicks Sporting Goods orders to their address
        if (shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 == "8778469997")
        {
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Company = "Dicks Sporting Goods";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Contact = "";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Address1 = "1314 Conklin Rd.";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Address2 = "STE B";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.City = "Conklin";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.StateProvince = "NY";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.PostalCode = "13748";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Country = "US";
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress.Phone = "8778469997";
        }
        
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling)
        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = addressBookEntries[0].Company;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Contact = addressBookEntries[0].Contact;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = addressBookEntries[0].Address1;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address2 = addressBookEntries[0].Address2;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address3 = addressBookEntries[0].Address3;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.City = addressBookEntries[0].City;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.StateProvince = addressBookEntries[0].StateProvince;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.PostalCode = addressBookEntries[0].PostalCode;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Country = addressBookEntries[0].Country;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Phone = addressBookEntries[0].Phone;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Account = addressBookEntries[0].Account;
            }
        }   
        else if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms == "CONSIGNEE")
        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = addressBookEntries[0].Account;
            }
        }
        $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Length"]').focus();
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData4 == "RTGD")
        {
            alert("Please ensure to rate and select the desired service for shipping.");
        }
    };

        {
            var addressBook = this.GetAddressBook('NexusAddressBook', this.vm.UserInformation);
            var addressBookEntries = this.GetAddressBookEntries(addressBook, this.vm.UserInformation, shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3);
            if (addressBookEntries == undefined)
            {
                alert("No entry found in Address Book for Company Code '" + shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3 + "'. Please ensure Third Party Address and/or Account Number are manually entered if needed before shipping.");
            }
            else
            {
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Company = addressBookEntries[0].Company;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Contact = addressBookEntries[0].Contact;
                shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBillingAddress.Address1 = addressBookEntries[0].Address1;

// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        vm = this.vm;
        if (location == "/shipping") {
            // Select PPO vs Non-PPO
                    
            $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference18"]', 'change', function () {
                var $referenceOptions = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference18"]');
                if ($referenceOptions.val() === "PPO") {
                    //alert("PPO" + $referenceOptions.val());
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference14.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference15.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = true;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.IsRequired = true;
                    $('label:contains("Enter Name of Shipment Requestor")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference14"]').hide();
                    $('label:contains("NIKE Cost/Profit Center Bill To")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference15"]').hide();


                    $('label:contains("C/N CARTON ID NUMBER 1 Per Carton")').show();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference16"]').show();
                    $('label:contains("PO# (Begins with 35, 45)")').show();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference17"]').show();
                } else if ($referenceOptions.val() === "Non-PPO") {
                    //alert("Non-PPO" + $referenceOptions.val());
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference14.IsRequired = true;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference15.IsRequired = true;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.IsRequired = false;
                    $('label:contains("Enter Name of Shipment Requestor")').show();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference14"]').show();
                    $('label:contains("NIKE Cost/Profit Center Bill To")').show();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference15"]').show();

                    $('label:contains("C/N CARTON ID NUMBER 1 Per Carton")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference16"]').hide();
                    $('label:contains("PO# (Begins with 35, 45)")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference17"]').hide();
                } else {
                    //alert("blank" + $referenceOptions.val());
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference14.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference15.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference16.IsRequired = false;
                    vm.profile.FieldOptions.MiscReference17.IsRequired = false;
                    $('label:contains("Enter Name of Shipment Requestor")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference14"].').hide();
                    $('label:contains("NIKE Cost/Profit Center Bill To")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference15"]').hide();
                    $('label:contains("C/N CARTON ID NUMBER 1 Per Carton")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference16"]').hide();
                    $('label:contains("")').hide();
                    $('input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference17"]').hide();
                }
            });
            // Domestic Tab
            $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.TransportationCharges"]', 'change', function () {
                
                var $billOption = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.TransportationCharges"]');
                
                if ($billOption.val() == "thirdParty") {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();//.hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').show();

                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').show();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').show();//.hide();
                } else {

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').show();//.hide();

                            $thirdPartyBillingAddress.find('select[ng-model="nameaddress.AddressBookIdToProcess"]').hide();

                            $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();//.hide();
                            $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').show();//.hide();

// SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
function SendFreightCollect(shipmentRequest) {
        debugger;
        if (typeof shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 !== "undefined") 
        //shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = "";
        var selection = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20;
        if (selection.indexOf("-") > -1) {
            var position = selection.indexOf("-");
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Account = selection.substring(position + 2);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Terms = "CONSIGNEE";
        } else {
            throw new error({ "number": "001", "description": "Receiver Billing Information not found." });
        }
    }

// this.PreSearchHistory(searchCriteria) // returns undefined
	this.PreSearchHistory = function(searchCriteria) {


		if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses !== null && searchCriteria.WhereClauses !== undefined) {
			if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses.length > 0) {
				var StartShipDate = null;
				var EndShipDate = null;
				var Shipper = "";
				for (var i = 0; i <= searchCriteria.WhereClauses.length - 1; i++) {
					if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldName == "Shipper") {
						Shipper = searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldValue;
					} else if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldName == "Shipdate" && StartShipDate == null) {
						StartShipDate = searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldValue;
					} else if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldName == "Shipdate" && StartShipDate != null) {
						EndShipDate = searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldValue;
					} else if (searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i].FieldName == "MiscReference1") {
						var miscReferenceObject = searchCriteria.WhereClauses[i];
						searchCriteria.WhereClauses.splice(i, 1);
						searchCriteria.WhereClauses.push({
							"FieldName": "ConsolidationTrackingNumber",
							"FieldValue": miscReferenceObject.FieldValue,
							"Operator": miscReferenceObject.Operator
						});
					}
				}



				var data = {
					UserContext: client.userContext,
					Data: "ShipDate=" + StartShipDate + ";" + "Shipper=" + Shipper
				}
				if (StartShipDate == EndShipDate) {
					sendSearchPackages("UserMethod", data, false)
				} else {
					var divResults = document.getElementById("divResults");
					divResults.innerHTML = "Select one day only to show package count!";
				}
			}
		}

	}

		}

// ReplaceAccountNumberWithXXXXXX() // returns undefined
	function ReplaceAccountNumberWithXXXXXX() {
		const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
			// Select all child tracking numbers
			const trackingNumberElements = document.querySelectorAll('div.ng-binding');
			trackingNumberElements.forEach(element => {
				const text = element.textContent.trim();
				if (text.length === 18) {
					element.textContent = text.substring(0, 3) + 'XXXXXX' + text.substring(9);
				}
			});

			// Select all lead tracking numbers
			const tableCells = document.querySelectorAll('td.ng-binding');
			tableCells.forEach(cell => {
				const text = cell.textContent.trim();
				if (text.length === 18) {
					cell.textContent = text.substring(0, 3) + 'XXXXXX' + text.substring(9);
				}
			});
		});

		// Start observing the body for changes
		observer.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });
	}

// HighlightWrongOrderNumber() // returns undefined
	function HighlightWrongOrderNumber() {
		$('input[name="orderNumber"]').focusout(function() {
			$(this).css("background-color", ($(this).val().length > 0 && $(this).val().length < 8) ? "#f44336" : "#FFFFFF");
		})
	}

// function checkElmLoaded(selector) // returns Promise
    function checkElmLoaded(selector) {
        return new Promise(resolve => {
            if (document.querySelector(selector)) {
                return resolve(document.querySelector(selector));
            }
            const observer = new MutationObserver(mutations => {
                if (document.querySelector(selector)) {
                    resolve(document.querySelector(selector));
                    observer.disconnect();
                }
            });
            observer.observe(document.body, {
                childList: true,
                subtree: true
            });
        });
    }

// function addShipperRelease() // returns undefined
    function addShipperRelease() {
        if(checkShipperReleaseAvailable())
        {
            var htmlShipperRelease = "<div class='form-check' property='DeliveryMethod' model='vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryMethod' caption='Require Shipper Release'>" +
                "<input type='checkbox' id='shipperRelease' class='form-check-input ng-pristine ng-untouched ng-valid ng-empty' ng-model='vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryMethod'>" +
                "<label class='form-check-label ng-binding' style='padding-left: 6px;'>Shipper Release</label>" +
                "</div>"
            $('[ng-model="proofofdeliverypane"]').children().first().after(htmlShipperRelease);
    
            $('#shipperRelease').prop('checked', vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryMethod);
    
            $('#shipperRelease').change(function() {
                var shipperRelease = $('#shipperRelease').is(":checked");
                vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeliveryMethod = shipperRelease;
            });
        }
    }

// InitiateDelegates() // returns undefined
    InitiateDelegates()
    {
      let that = this

      $('body').delegate('#btnAssignCommodities', 'click', function()
      {
        if ($('#divAssignCommodities:visible').length > 0) return;
        that.ShowAssignGoodsPane();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#btnApplyCommodityAssignments', 'click', function(e)
      {
        that.ApplyCommodityAssignments();
      });

      $('body').delegate('#btnCancelAssignGoods', 'click', function(e)
      {
        that.HideAssignGoodsPane();
      });

      $('body').delegate('.assign-to-new-box', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        $('button[ng-click="vm.addPackage();"]').trigger('click').promise().done((e) =>
        {
          const cp = +$('#spanCurrentPackageIndex').text();
          that.MoveGoodToBox(li, cp);
        });
      });

      $('body').delegate('.assign-to-current-box', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        const cp = +$('#spanCurrentPackageIndex').text();
        that.MoveGoodToBox(li, cp);
      });

      $('body').delegate('.undo-box-assignment', 'click', function(e)
      {
        let li = $(e.target).closest('li');
        that.MoveGoodToBox(li, 1);
      });

    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
		var licenseTab;
		var documentsMethodsTab;
		var DDTCTab;
		
		//HIDE LICENSE TAB
		//HIDE Documents Methods TAB
		//HIDE DDTC TAB
		if (location === '/shipping') {
			var interval = setInterval(function () {
				
				var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("li"); 
				
               Array.from(tags).forEach(function(tag){
                     if(tag.innerHTML.includes("License")) licenseTab = tag;
                     if(tag.innerHTML.includes("Documents Methods")) documentsMethodsTab = tag;
                     if(tag.innerHTML.includes("DDTC")) DDTCTab = tag;
                   });
				
				if (licenseTab && documentsMethodsTab && DDTCTab) {
				    clearInterval(interval);
				    //licenseTab.style.display = "none"; 
				    documentsMethodsTab.style.display = "none";
				    //DDTCTab.style.display = "none";
			    }
			    
			}, 50); 
		 }
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
       
        /* Only apply these functions to the shipping page. */
        if (window.location.hash == "#!/shipping") {
            $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function (e) {
                $('div.alert-danger:visible').hide();
            })

            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if ((window.jQuery !== undefined) && ($('select[name=Country]').length > 0)) {
                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);

                    /* Register the event that fires when a user clicks the 'Reset' button on the main page. */
                    $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.newShipment()"]:eq(0)', 'click', function (e) {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                    });

                    /* Disable the ThirdPartyBilling edit button. */
                    $('input[type=button][ng-disabled="!vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').prop('disabled', true).attr('disabled', true);

                    /* For select boxes which are enabled, remove the default country of United States. */
                    $('select[name=Country][disabled!=disabled]').prop('selectedIndex', 0);

                    /* Trying to fix a bug where the Ship From country select element is disabled and set to the wrong country. */
                    /* Enable the element. */
                    $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').prop('disabled', false);

                    /* Hide the End Of Day dropdown menu. */
                    $('ul.nav.navbar-nav li.dropdown:eq(1) > a.dropdown-toggle').hide();

                    /* Change captions for tabs when processing return shipments. */
                    /* Register the event on change. */
                    $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDeliveryMethod"]', 'change', function (e) {
                        var isReturn = $(this).val().length > 0;
                        ReturnNameAddressCaption(isReturn);
                        vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery = isReturn;
                    });

                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                    $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="OriginAddress"] select[name="Country"]', 'change', checkOriginConsigneeCountry);
                } /* if ((window.jQuery... */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */

        } /* if (window.location.hash... */
    };

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) // returns void
    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress, addressName) {
        debugger;
        if (addressName !== '' && addressName !== 'ThirdPartyBillingAddress') {
            var checkExist = setInterval(function () {

                if (($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().length > 0) && ($('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().length > 0)) {

                    /* Stop the timer. */
                    clearInterval(checkExist);
                    /* The values are stored in the format of 'string:CC'.  We only want the CC. */
                    var shipToCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val().replace('string:', '');
                    var shipFromCountry = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(1)').val().replace('string:', '');

                    /* If we have no shipToCountry OR the shipFromCountry is either US or CA, disable the elements, return out. */
                    if (!shipToCountry | shipFromCountry == "US" | shipFromCountry == "CA") {
                        DisableThirdPartyBillingElements();
                        return false;
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != shipToCountry) {
                        /* If the shipFromCountry does NOT equal the shipToCountry then ship Third Party. */
                        SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                    }
                    else {
                        /* Now check to see if both the origin and destination countries are members of the EU. */
                        if ((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry))) {
                            SetThirdPartyBilling(shipmentRequest);
                        }

                        //ShipThirdPartyBilling((IsMemberOfEu(shipFromCountry)) && (IsMemberOfEu(shipToCountry)));
                    }

                    if (shipFromCountry != "US") {
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"]').val('string:KG').change();
                        $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Dimensions.Units"]').val('number:1').change();
                    }
                } /* if ($('div.modal-dialog.modal-md:visible') */

            }, 50); /* var checkExist = setInterval... */
        }
    };

// EmailNotificationAddress(event) // returns void
    this.EmailNotificationAddress = function (event) {
        var currentTarget = event.currentTarget;
        var ngModelName = currentTarget.attributes['ng-model'].nodeValue.split('.').pop();
        var emailAddress = this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Email;
        var pkg = this.currentShipment.Packages[0];
        debugger;
        // if (ngModelName.indexOf('DeliveryException') >= 0){
        //     SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // } else if (ngModelName.indexOf('Delivery') >= 0) {
        //     SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // } else {
        //     SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, ngModelName, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        // }

        if (ngModelName == 'ShipNotificationEmail') {
            SetShipNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName == 'DeliveryExceptionNotificationEmail') {
            SetDeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        } else if (ngModelName == 'DeliveryNotificationEmail') {
            SetDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail(pkg, emailAddress, currentTarget.checked);
        }
    };

// function ClientBusinessRules() // returns undefined
function ClientBusinessRules() {

    this.PreShip = function (shipmentRequest, userParams) {
    }

    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        var shipment = new Shipment(shipmentRequest);
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = shipment.UserRef1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = shipment.UserRef2;
    }

    this.AddPackage = function (shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
    }

    this.PostSelectAddressBook = function (shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {
    }



    class Shipment {
        constructor(shipmentRequest) {
            this.ShipmentRequest = shipmentRequest;
        }
        
        get UserEmail() { return this.GetEmail(); }
        
        get Attn() { return this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Contact; }
        
        get UserRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "User"); }
        get UserRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "User"); }
        get UserRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "User"); }
        get UserRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "User"); }
        get UserRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "User"); }
        get UserRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "User"); }
        get UserRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "User"); }
        get UserRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "User"); }
        get UserRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "User"); }
        get UserRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "User"); }

        get ToRef1() { return this.GetCustom("Custom1", "To"); }
        get ToRef2() { return this.GetCustom("Custom2", "To"); }
        get ToRef3() { return this.GetCustom("Custom3", "To"); }
        get ToRef4() { return this.GetCustom("Custom4", "To"); }
        get ToRef5() { return this.GetCustom("Custom5", "To"); }
        get ToRef6() { return this.GetCustom("Custom6", "To"); }
        get ToRef7() { return this.GetCustom("Custom7", "To"); }
        get ToRef8() { return this.GetCustom("Custom8", "To"); }
        get ToRef9() { return this.GetCustom("Custom9", "To"); }
        get ToRef10() { return this.GetCustom("Custom10", "To"); }

        get PkgRef1() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference; }
        get PkgRef2() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference; }

        get PkgMisc1() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1; }
        get PkgMisc2() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2; }
        get PkgMisc3() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3; }
        get PkgMisc4() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4; }
        get PkgMisc5() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5; }
        get PkgMisc6() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6; }
        get PkgMisc7() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference7; }
        get PkgMisc8() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference8; }
        get PkgMisc9() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference9; }
        get PkgMisc10() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference10; }

        get PkgMisc11() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11; }
        get PkgMisc12() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference12; }
        get PkgMisc13() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference13; }
        get PkgMisc14() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14; }
        get PkgMisc15() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference15; }
        get PkgMisc16() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference16; }
        get PkgMisc17() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference17; }
        get PkgMisc18() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference18; }
        get PkgMisc19() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference19; }
        get PkgMisc20() { return this.ShipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20; }

        GetEmail() {
            var emailText = "";
            var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
            Array.from(tags).forEach(function (tag) {
                if (tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!", "").trim();
            });
            return emailText;
        }



        GetCustom(fieldName, customDataType) {
            var returnValue = "";
            var customData = null;
            if (customDataType === "User") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.CustomData;
            if (customDataType === "To") customData = this.ShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.CustomData;

            if (customData) {
                customData.forEach(function (customField) {
                    if (fieldName === customField.Key) returnValue = customField.Value;
                })
            }
            return returnValue;
        }
        // End Shipment Class
    }

    class ViewModel {
        constructor(viewModel) {
            this.VM = viewModel;
        }

        IsValid(referenceField, referenceValue) {
            var isValid = false;
            if (this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField]) {
                var options = this.VM.fieldOptions[referenceField].FieldOptionValidations
                options.forEach(function (option) {
                    if (option.Value.trim() === referenceValue.trim()) isValid = true;
                });
            }

            if (referenceValue.length === 0 || !referenceValue.trim()) isValid = false;
            return isValid;
        }

        // End ViewModel Class
    }

    // End ClientBusinessRules
}

        }

        btnDN.hide();

        btnDEN.hide();

        btnRDN.hide();
        var btnCOD = $('button[ng-click="vm.showAccessorial =\'cashOnDeliveryPane\'"]');
        btnCOD.hide();
        var btnSAS = $('button[ng-click="vm.showAccessorial = \'sizeShapePane\'"]');
        btnSAS.hide();
        var btnMail = $('button[ng-click="vm.showAccessorial = \'mailingPane\'"]');
        btnMail.hide();
        var btnOther = $('button[ng-click="vm.showAccessorial = \'otherPane\'"]');

// function HideHoldAtLocation() // returns void
    function HideHoldAtLocation(){
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var hal = $('div[ng-model="vm.holdAtLocation"]');
            if (hal.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                hal.hide();
            }
        }, 50);
        
    }

// function RemoveAmountFromLastShipment() // returns void
    function RemoveAmountFromLastShipment()
    {
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var lastShip = $('div[ng-show="vm.showLastShipmentPanel"]');
            if (lastShip.length > 0)
            {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                var spanBase = lastShip.find('currency[currency_symbol="vm.lastShipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.BaseCharge.Currency"]');
                spanBase.text('');
                var spanDiscount = lastShip.find('currency[currency_value="vm.lastShipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.Discount.Amount"]');
                spanDiscount.text('');
                var spanSpecial = lastShip.find('currency[currency_value="vm.lastShipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.Special.Amount"]');
                spanSpecial.text('');
                var spanTotal = lastShip.find('currency[currency_value="vm.lastShipmentResponse.PackageDefaults.Total.Amount"]');
                spanTotal.text('');
                var gMSN = lastShip.find('div[class="ng-binding ng-scope"]');
                gMSN.text('');
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// function ReplaceShippingRatingName() // returns void
    function ReplaceShippingRatingName(){
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var a = $('a[href="/#!/shipping"]');
            if (a.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                RenameElement(a, 'Shipping', 'Expédition');
                //debugger;
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// function HideGroupManager() // returns void
    function HideGroupManager(){
        var loaded = setInterval(function() {
            var select = $('select[ng-change="vm.groupTypeChange()"]');
            if (select.length > 0) {
                clearInterval(loaded);
                //debugger;
                select.children('option[value="GUARDIAN"]').remove();
                select.children('option[value="TRADE_DIRECT"]').remove();
                $('body').delegate('select[ng-change="vm.groupTypeChange()"]', 'change', RenameShipperGroupManager); 
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// PageLoaded(loaded) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(loaded) {
        //debugger;
        if (loaded === '/shipping') {
           var interval = setInterval(function () {  
                var loaded = $('li[heading=Reference]').length && $('form[name=referenceForm]').find('div[property=MiscReference18]').length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    // after page loads, hide misc props used for settings
                    $('form[name=referenceForm]').find('div[property=MiscReference18]').hide();
                    $('form[name=referenceForm]').find('div[property=MiscReference19]').hide();
                    $('form[name=referenceForm]').find('div[property=MiscReference20]').hide();
                }
            }, 200);
        }
    };

// downloadFromCin7API() // returns void
this.downloadFromCin7API = function() {
		//debugger;
		let data = { Action: 'Download_Orders', Params: ''};
		
		downloadOrders = true;
		toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);

		// call SBR UserMethod to access Cin7 API to download orders
		$.post({
			url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
			headers: clientService.authorizationToken(),
			data: {
			    UserContext: client.userContext,
			    Data: JSON.stringify(data)
			}
		}).done(function (data) {
		    //debugger;
			downloadOrders = false;
		    toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);
		    
			if (data.Data === true) {
				alert('Download successful!');
			}
			else {
				alert('Download was not successful');
			}
		}).fail(function (err) {
		    //debugger;
			downloadOrders = false;
		    toggleDownloadLoading(downloadOrders);
			console.log(err.responseJSON);
			alert('Download was not successful');
		});
	}

// Source: Revvity Omics (PerkinElmer)_Perkin Elmer Reference Rule_1531.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        if (location == '/shipping') {
            var shippers = this.vm.profile.Shippers;
            this.vm.profile.Shippers = shippers.sort(function (a, b) {
                if (a.Name > b.Name) return 1;
                if (a.Name < b.Name) return -1;
                return 0;
            });
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
	this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest){
        this.vm.myShipperChange = this.MyShipperChange;
        this.vm.myShipperChange();
    }

// MyShipperChange() // returns undefined
    this.MyShipperChange = function () {
        var shipmentRequest = this.currentShipment;
        var originName = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Name;

        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = originName ? shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Symbol : '';
        shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference = originName ? shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince + "," + originName.split('(')[0] : '';
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) { 
        if(location === "/"){
            document.location = "#!/shipping";
             }
    $(document).ready(function () {
        if (location == '/history') {
            $('#reports').on('change', function (e)
            {
                    let v = $(this).find('option:selected').text();
                    if (v == 'Hazmat Report')
                        {
                            $('button[value="Export"]').off();
                                        $('body').delegate('button[value=Export]', 'click', function(e) {
                getHazmatReport();
            });
                        }
                })
            }   
    });
    }

    this.PostSearchHistory = function(packages) {
        var selectedValue = $('select[id="reports"]:eq(0)').val();
        var selectedReport = $("select[id='reports'] option[value='" + selectedValue + "'");
        if(selectedReport[0].innerText === "Hazmat Report"){
            $('button[value=Export]').removeAttr('ng-click');
            $('body').delegate('button[value=Export]', 'click', function(e) {
               // getHazmatReport();
            });
        }
    }
