// init() // returns undefined
init: function () {
            //this.getUserContext();

            String.prototype.focus = function () {
                if (!focus(this))
                    var interval = setInterval(function(selector) { 
                        if (focus(selector)) clearInterval(interval);
                    }, 10, this);

                function focus(selector) {
                    $(selector).focus();
                    return $(selector).length;
                }
            };
            
            String.prototype.addButtonLabel = function(text) {
                var interval = setInterval(function(selector) { 
                    var $element = $(selector);
                    if ($element.length) {
                        clearInterval(interval);                        
                        $element.wrap('<label class="ng-binding">').after(text);
                    } 
                }, 10, this);
            }
        }

// All() // returns undefined
All: function () { $('div[role="alert"]').hide() }

// Info() // returns undefined
Info: function () { $('div[role="alert"].alert-info:visible').hide() }

// Success() // returns undefined
Success: function () { $('div[role="alert"].alert-success:visible').hide() }

// Danger() // returns undefined
Danger: function () { $('div[role="alert"].alert-danger:visible').hide() }

// Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function () {
        debugger;
        this.vm.keyDown = keyDown;

        $('body').keydown(this.vm, function (event) {
            event.data.keyDownAction = undefined;
            if (event.key === "/") {
                event.preventDefault();
                event.data.keyDownAction = 'Save';
                $('#cbrKeydown').click();
            }
        });

        function keyDown() {
            this.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Contact = "hello";
            this.selectedServices = [
                { Symbol: "CONNECTSHIP_UPS.UPS.NDS" }
            ];
        }           
    }

// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns undefined
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) {  
        if (location === '/shipping') {
            // hide the select all checkbox and text
            var checkboxInterval = setInterval(function() {
                var selectAll = $('input[ng-model="vm.isAllServicesSelected"]');
                if (selectAll.length > 0) {  // if the element has rendered
                    clearInterval(checkboxInterval); // <-- important to turn the interval off
                    selectAll.hide();
                    $(".chkLabel").hide();                    
                    $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"]').hide();
                    $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12"]').hide();
                    $('div[ng-if="vm.showServiceSelection"]').attr("class", "col-md-6 no-left-right-padding");
                    $('[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Amount"]').on('input', function () {
                        this.value = this.value.match(/^\d+\.?\d{0,2}/);
                    });
                }
            }, 200);
        }
    }

// this.NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest) { 
        // set defaults
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference7 = "No";
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11 = "-- choose option --";
        $('#LoadInput').prop('disabled', false);
        $('#LoadButton').prop('disabled', false);
        $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"]').hide();
        $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12"]').hide();
        
        // Pending Shipment
        $('body').on('click', 'table[aria-describedby="Pending Shipments"] input[type="button"]', this.vm, function(e) {
            $("[property=MiscReference12] input").attr('maxlength','35'); // limit the charecter number for the service change reason field
            $('body').delegate('select[property="Service"]', 'change', function (e) { serviceChangeOptions(this.value); });
            $('body').delegate('[property="MiscReference11"] select', 'change', function (e) { serviceChangeComment(this.value); });
            $('#LoadInput').prop('disabled', true);
            $('#LoadButton').prop('disabled', true);
            serviceChangeOptionsPending();
        });
    }

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        commentRequired = false;
        showChangeOptions = true; 
        // style changes
        $("[property=MiscReference12] input").attr('maxlength','35'); // limit the charecter number for the service change reason field
        $('body').delegate('select[property="Service"]', 'change', function (e) { serviceChangeOptions(this.value); });
        $('body').delegate('[property="MiscReference11"] select', 'change', function (e) { serviceChangeComment(this.value); });
        $('#LoadInput').prop('disabled', true);
        $('#LoadButton').prop('disabled', true);
    }

// this.PostShip(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) // returns undefined
    this.PostShip = function(shipmentRequest, shipmentResponse) {
        // reset the hidden values
        showChangeOptions = false;
        $('body').delegate('select[property="Service"]', 'change', function (e) {  });
        $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"]').hide();
        $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12"]').hide();
        
        // alert any errors
        if (shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1){
            alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1);
        }
        
        // remove discount from lastShipment
        $("label:contains('Discount:')").next("span").remove();
        $("label:contains('Discount:')").next("br").remove();
        $("label:contains('Discount:')").remove();
    }

// serviceChangeOptions(newService) // returns undefined
    function serviceChangeOptions(newService){
        var originalService = $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"] :input').val();
        var ServiceChangeCode = $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"] :input').val();
        if (newService != originalService){
            showChangeOptions = true;
            $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"]').show();
            if(ServiceChangeCode == "string:Other - Comment Field"){
                commentRequired = true;
                $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12"]').show();
            }
        } else {
            showChangeOptions = false;
            commentRequired = false;
            $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"]').hide();
            $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12"]').hide();
        }
    }

// serviceChangeComment(value) // returns undefined
    function serviceChangeComment(value){
        if (value == "string:Other - Comment Field"){
            commentRequired = true;
            $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12"]').show();
        } else {
            commentRequired = false;
            $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12"]').hide();
        }
    }

// serviceChangeOptionsPending() // returns undefined
    function serviceChangeOptionsPending(){
        var currentService = $('[property="Service"] :selected').val();
        var originalService = $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference10"] :input').val();
        var ServiceChangeCode = $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"] :input').val();
        if (currentService != originalService){
            showChangeOptions = true;
            $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"]').show();
            if(ServiceChangeCode == "string:Other - Comment Field"){
                commentRequired = true;
                $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12"]').show();
            }
        } else {
            showChangeOptions = false;
            commentRequired = false;
            $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference11"]').hide();
            $('div[model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.MiscReference12"]').hide();
        }
    }

// alertMessage(type, msg) // returns undefined
    function alertMessage(type, msg){
        var $alert = $('#alert' + type); //info, success and danger
        $alert.find('span:eq(2)').html(msg);
        $alert.show();
    }

// Shipping() // returns undefined
this.Shipping = function()

    {
		
		
        //Set Consignee Countries
        var consigneeCountries = ['', 'US', 'CA', 'AU']
        setConsigneeCountries(consigneeCountries);

        //Set Currency Options
        declaredValueCurrencyOptions();
        customsDeclaredValueCurrencyOptions();
        commodityUnitValueCurrencyOptions();
        invoiceDiscountCurrencyOptions();
        invoiceFreightCurrencyOptions();
        invoiceInsuranceFeeCurrencyOptions();


        $(document).ready(function () {
            filterPickupPaymentType();
        });

        function filterPickupPaymentType() {
            $('body').delegate('button[ng-click="vm.createPickupRequestClick()"]', 'click', function (event) {
                var list = ['PAY_BY_SHIPPER_ACCOUNT'];
                var element = '[ng-model="vm.pickup.PaymentType"] option';
                replaceOptionValues(list, element);
            });
        }
        //var currencies = ['USD', 'CAD'];
        //setCurrency(currencies);
    }

// setConsigneeCountries(selectedCountries) // returns undefined
function setConsigneeCountries(selectedCountries)
    {
        var countryStringValue = ('string:' + selectedCountries.join('|string:')).split('|');
        var interval = setInterval(function()

        {
            var consigneeCountries = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] select[name="Country"] option');
            if (consigneeCountries.length)
            {
                clearInterval(interval);
                Array.from(consigneeCountries).forEach(function(opt)

                {
                    if (opt.value != '')
                    {
                        if (!countryStringValue.includes(opt.value))
                        {
                            opt.remove();
                        }
                    }
                });
            }
        }, 50);            
    }

// declaredValueCurrencyOptions() // returns undefined
function declaredValueCurrencyOptions()
    {
        var list = ['USD', 'CAD'];
        var element = '[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].DeclaredValueAmount.Currency"] option';
        setCurrencyOptions(list, element);
    }

    }

    {

// setCurrencyOptions(list, element) // returns undefined
function setCurrencyOptions(list, element)
    {
        var interval = setInterval(function() 
            {
                var currencies = $(element);
                if (currencies.length)
                {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function(){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
    }

// replaceOptionValues(list, element) // returns undefined
function replaceOptionValues(list, element) {
        var valuelist = list.map(function (e) { return 'string:' + e });
        var interval = setInterval(function () {
            var $element = $(element);
            if ($element.length) {
                clearInterval(interval);
                $element.each(function () {
                    if (!valuelist.includes(this.value) && this.value != '') this.remove();
                });
            }
        }, 50);
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest)
    {
    this.vm.shipMode = 0;
    this.vm.disableShipMode = true;
    filterPickupPaymentType();

        function filterPickupPaymentType() {
            var list = ['Pay by shipper account'];            
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                var currencies = $('[ng-model="vm.pickup.PaymentType"] option');
                if (currencies.length) {
                    debugger;
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    currencies.each(function (){ if (!list.includes(this.text)) this.remove(); });
                }
            }, 50);
        }
}

// PostSelectAddressBook(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) // returns undefined
this.PostSelectAddressBook = function(shipmentRequest, nameaddress) {

    //debugger;

    //Map Store Number to ShipperReference
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference = nameaddress.Code;

    //Set Default Services Based on From and To Countries		
    var fromCountry = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.Country;
    var toCountry = nameaddress.Country;

    //Email Address Mappings
	if(nameaddress.Email != null)
	{
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].DeliveryExceptionNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryNotificationAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
		shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryAddressEmail = nameaddress.Email.trim();
	}

    //Store Address Book ID value in MiscReference20 to signify that consignee address came from Address Book and was not manually entered.
    shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference20 = nameaddress.AddressBookId.toString();


    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.GND")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'US' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'CA')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}

    if (fromCountry == 'CA' && toCountry == 'US')
    {
        this.SetSelectedService("UPSAPI.UPS.STANDARD")
		this.SetCurrencyCAD(toCountry)
		this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
	}
}

// SetSelectedService(serviceSymbol) // returns undefined
this.SetSelectedService = function(serviceSymbol)
    {
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        for (var i = 0; i < this.vm.profile.Services.length; i++)
        {
            if (this.vm.profile.Services[i].Symbol === serviceSymbol)
            {
                this.vm.selectedServices = [this.vm.profile.Services[i]];
                this.vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Service = this.vm.profile.Services[i];
                break;
            }
        }
    }
}

// SetCurrencyCAD(shipToCountry) // returns undefined
this.SetCurrencyCAD = function(shipToCountry)
{
    if (this.vm.profile != null)
    {
        if (shipToCountry === "CA")
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "CAD" };
        }
        else
        {
            //this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].DeclaredValueCustoms = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].CodAmount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceDiscount = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceFreight = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceInsuranceFee = { Currency: "USD" };
            this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].InvoiceOtherFee = { Currency: "USD" };
        }
    }
}

// function CreateCustomShippingElements(vm) // returns void
    function CreateCustomShippingElements(vm) {
        //debugger;
        //#region Create Ship Goods Type DropDown

        //#region Click Search Button
        $("#searchButton").click(function() {
            //Remove drop-down control if it exists before creating a new one
            //$("#costcodes").remove();

            // added prefix to beginning of search value for UserMethod call, since method is used for other functions
            var searchName = "search|" + $('#search_input').val();

            if (searchName.length !== 0 && searchName != 'search|')
            {
                // reset dropdown
                $('#costcodes').off('change');
                $('#costcodes option:not(:first)').remove();
                $('#costcodes').hide();

                // call user method
                var params = searchName;

                //$.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
                //{
                //    UserContext: userContext,
                //    Data: JSON.stringify(params)
                
                // updated for 2.3
                $.post({
                    url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
                    data: {
                        UserContext: client.userContext,
                        Data: JSON.stringify(params)
                    },
                    headers: clientService.authorizationToken()
                }).done(function(result) {
                    //debugger;
                    result = decodeReturnString(result);
                    if (result !== null && result !== undefined && result !== '') {
                        if (result.ErrorCode === 0 && result.Data !== undefined && !(typeof(result.Data) == 'string' && result.Data.indexOf('[Error]') == -1)) {
                            ParseJson(result.Data);
                        }
                        else {
                            //Display Error
                            alert(result.Data);
                        }
                    }
                    else {
                        alert("No data was returned from search");
                    }
                }).fail(function (e) {
                    alert(e.message);
                });
            }
            else
            {
                alert("Please enter name of whom you are shipping for before clicking the search button.");
                $('#search_input').css('background-color', '#fffef0');
                $('#search_input').focus();
            }
        });
        //#endregion

        //#region Create Cost Code File Button
        var costCodeFileButton = "<span>" +
            "<input type='file' id='fileLoader' name='files' title='Load Cost Code File' style='display:none;'> " +
            "<button id='btnOpenFileDialog' value='Import New GL Code File' class='btn btn-xs btn-primary'>Import New GL Code File</button>" +
            "</span>";

        // add button beside Pending Shipments
        $("div.row.top-tool-bar").find("div.pull-left").append(costCodeFileButton);
        $("#fileLoader").change(function() {
            openFileDialog();
        });
        $("#btnOpenFileDialog").click(function() {
            $("#fileLoader").click();
        });
        //#endregion
    }

// function openFileDialog() // returns void
    function openFileDialog() {
        //debugger;
        var filesSelected = document.getElementById("fileLoader");

        if (filesSelected !== undefined) {
            const fileReader = new FileReader();

            if (filesSelected.files[0]) {
                fileReader.readAsDataURL(filesSelected.files[0]);
            }

            fileReader.onload = function (event) {
                var files = event.target.result;

                // Get base64 file data
                var contents = event.target.result.split(',')[1];

                // adding prefix to beginning of file data to send to user method
                var fileData = "file|" + contents;

                // $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
                // {
                //     UserContext: userContext,
                //     Data: JSON.stringify(fileData)

                // updated for 2.3
                $.post({
                    url: clientService.config.ShipExecServiceUrl + '/UserMethod',
                    data: {
                        UserContext: client.userContext,
                        Data: JSON.stringify(fileData)
                    },
                    headers: clientService.authorizationToken()
                }).done(function(result) {
                    //debugger;
                    // result.Data should be unencoded [Success] or [Error] string
                    if (result.ErrorCode === 0 && result.Data !== undefined && result.Data.indexOf('[Error]') == -1) {
                        alert(result.Data);
                    }
                    else {
                        // display error
                        alert(result.Data);
                    }
                }).fail(function (e) {
                    alert(e.message);
                });
            };
        }
    }

// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
this.PageLoaded = function(location) {
		
		var vm, userContext ;
		var pickupDeliveryPane;
		
		vm = this.vm;
		
		if (location === '/shipping') {
			var interval = setInterval(function () {
				//pickupDeliveryPane = $('[ng-model="pickupDeliveryPane"]');
				pickupDeliveryPane = $('[name="pickupDeliveryForm"]')
				var loaded = pickupDeliveryPane.length;
				
				if (loaded) {
				    clearInterval(interval);
				    pickupDeliveryPaneReady(pickupDeliveryPane);
				}
			}, 50); 
		 }
    }

// Shipping() // returns void

// GetDataManagementContents(apiMethod) // returns void
this.GetDataManagementContents = function (apiMethod) {
        var userContext = this.GetUserContext();
        var thinClientAPIRequest = this.thinClientAPIRequest;

        var data = { CompanyId: userContext.CompanyId };
        thinClientAPIRequest(apiMethod, data, true).done(function (result) {
            if (result.ErrorCode == 0) {
                var userObject = { Action: apiMethod, Data: JSON.stringify(result) };
                data = { Data: btoa(JSON.stringify(userObject)), UserContext: userContext };
                thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, true);//.done(function (result) { debugger; });
            };
        });
    }

// thinClientAPIRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns jqXHR
this.thinClientAPIRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = client.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = client.getAuthorizationToken();
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken })
    }

    this.GetDataManagementContents = function (apiMethod) {
        var userContext = this.GetUserContext();
        var thinClientAPIRequest = this.thinClientAPIRequest;

        var data = { CompanyId: userContext.CompanyId };
        thinClientAPIRequest(apiMethod, data, true).done(function (result) {
            if (result.ErrorCode == 0) {
                var userObject = { Action: apiMethod, Data: JSON.stringify(result) };

    this.thinClientAPIRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = client.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = client.getAuthorizationToken();
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken })
    }

// GetUserContext() // returns userContext or UserInformation
    this.GetUserContext = function () {
        if (this.vm.userContext) return this.vm.userContext;
        if (this.vm.UserInformation) return this.vm.UserInformation;
    }

// InitializeDelegateFunctions() // returns void
  InitializeDelegateFunctions = () =>
  {
    let that = this;
    this.DataStore = new DataStore(this.H);
    this.Dialogs = new UserDialogs(this);

    this.LoadSampleData();

    //create the first container object
    this.Containers.Create(1);

    //if the elements exist at the time of rendering, use .on
    $('#btnAddMultipleItems').on('click', function(e) { that.Dialogs.Show('MultipleOperationsDialog'); });
    $('#btnRemoveMultipleItems').on('click', function(e) { that.Dialogs.Show('MultipleOperationsDialog', true); });
    $('#btnDev').on('click', function(e)
    {
      let post = new PostBack();
      const p = post.SessionData(that.Containers.List).then((ret) => console.log(ret));
      //that.Dialogs.Dialog.Show('PackingCompleteDialog');
    });

    //change the ShipExec logo to remove the overlay and show the standard shipping screen
    $('div.navbar-header').find('a[href="/ShipExecThinClient/"]').attr('href', '').on('click', function(e)
    {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      e.stopImmediatePropagation();
      that.ShowStandardShippingScreen();
    });

    //*** DEVELOPMENT CODE ONLY.  REMOVE BEFORE PROD */
    $('body').delegate('td.item-number', 'click', function(e)
    {
      let tr = $(this).closest('tr').data();
      that.Items.Add(tr);
    });

    $('body').on('click', function(e)
    {
      let target = e.target;

      let bDropdown = $(target).closest('div').hasClass('dropdown');

      bDropdown = bDropdown || $(target).closest('span').hasClass('dropdown');

      if (bDropdown) { return false; }

      $('.dropdown-menu').slideUp();

      if ($('#inputFilterTerm').is(':focus'))
      {
        return false;
      }
      else
      {
        $('.escape-target').hide();
      }
    });

      if ($(e.target).hasClass('glyphicon') || $(e.target).closest('div.container-parent').hasClass('active'))

    //event handler for moving the toast notification around
    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('.draggable', 'mousedown', function(e)
    {
      var dr = $(this).addClass("drag");

      let height = dr.outerHeight();
      let width = dr.outerWidth();

      let ypos = dr.offset().top + height - e.pageY;
      let xpos = dr.offset().left + width - e.pageX;

      $(document.body).on('mousemove', function(e)
      {
        var itop = e.pageY + ypos - height;
        var ileft = e.pageX + xpos - width;

        if (dr.hasClass("drag"))
        {
          dr.offset({ top: itop, left: ileft });
        }
      }).on('mouseup', function(e)
      {
        dr.removeClass("drag");
      });
    });

    //when the user hovers over a row, highlight the matching row in the panel list items
    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate(this.H.TableRowsAll, 'mouseover mouseout', function(e)
    {
      const row = $(this).data();
      const containers = that.DataStore.GetContainersForFocusedItem(row.RowId);
      if (containers)
      {
        containers.map(m => $(`.container-parent[container-index="${m}"]`).addClass('highlight'));
      }

      switch (e.type)
      {
        case 'mouseover':
          $(that.H.PanelOpenContainersActiveList).find(`.list-group-item[row-id="${row.RowId}"]`).addClass('item-hover');
          if (containers) containers.map(m => $(`.container-parent[container-index="${m}"] .panel-body`).addClass('highlight'));
          break;

        case 'mouseout':
          $(that.H.PanelOpenContainersActiveList).find(`.list-group-item[row-id="${row.RowId}"]`).removeClass('item-hover');
          if (containers) containers.map(m => $(`.container-parent[container-index="${m}"] .panel-body`).removeClass('highlight'));
          break;
      }
    });

    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('[event="SetActiveContainer"]', 'mouseover mouseout', function(e)
    {
      switch (e.type)
      {
        case 'mouseover':
          let i = $(this).closest('div.container-parent').attr('container-index');
          that.HighlightRowsInContainer(i);
          break;

        case 'mouseout':
          that.HighlightRowsInContainer();
          break;
      }
    });

    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate(that.H.PanelOpenContainersActiveListItems, 'mouseover mouseout', function(e)
    {
      switch (e.type)
      {
        case 'mouseover':
          that.HighlightSelectedRow($(this).attr('row-id'));
          break;

        case 'mouseout':
          that.HighlightSelectedRow();
          break;
      }
    });

     * TODO:  Move this to the HTML class.

    $(this.H.UIContainer).delegate('[event=ShowContainerDetails]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      const data = $(this).closest('.container-parent').data();
      const containerIndex = data[0].PackedItems[0].ContainerIndex;
      const productCount = Object.keys(data).length;

      let div = $('div.container-item-details').first();
      let itemCount = 0;

      //get rid of any existing entries
      $(div).find('.divTableRow').not('.template').remove();
      $(div).find('span.container-index').text(containerIndex);

      Object.keys(data).forEach((key) =>
      {
        let item = data[key];
        let count = item.PackedItems[0].Count;
        itemCount += count;
        let p = $(div).find('.divTableRow.template').first().clone();
        $(p).removeClass('template');

        $(p).find('span.item-count').text(count);
        $(p).find('span.item-number').text(item.ItemNumber);
        $(p).find('span.item-description').text(item.ItemDescription);

        $(p).appendTo(div)
      });

      $(div).find('.container-title').text(`${productCount} Product${productCount > 1 ? `s` : ``} | ${itemCount} Item${itemCount > 1 ? `s` : ``} | 36X48X72 | 1825 LBS`);

      that.Overlay.Show();

      $(div).fadeIn();
    });

    //*** END DEVELOPMENT CODE ONLY */

    $('#ulContainerList').find('ul:gt(0)').remove();

    $('body').delegate('#inputBarcodeValue', 'keyup', function(e)
    {
      if ($(this).val().trim().length === 0) return false;

      let u = $(this).val().trim().toUpperCase();

      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      if (keycode == 13) //enter
      {
        that.AddItemToCurrentContainer(u);
      }
    });

    return;

    $(this.UIContainer).delegate('#inputFilterTerm', 'keyup', function(e)
    {
      //show or hide the 'clear' anchor visibility
      $('[event="ClearTableFilters"]').toggle($(this).val().length > 0);

      var keycode = (e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which);
      if (keycode == 13) //enter
      {
        //the table rows filter as the user types so just need to hide the div when they press enter
        //the escape key is handled in another delegate as it applies to multiple elements
        $('#divFilterInput').hide();
      }

      const rows = that.GetTableRowsWithMatchingText($(this).val().toUpperCase());
      that.AppEvents.On_FilterTableRowsByText(rows);
    });

    $(this.UIContainer).delegate('[event=ClearTableFilters]', 'click', function(e)
    {

    $(this.UIContainer).delegate('[event=CollapsePanel]', 'click', function(e)
    {
      //rotate the icon 180 degrees
      $(this).toggleClass('up');

      let pb = $(this).closest('div.panel').find('div.panel-body');
      let ul = $(this).closest('div.panel').find('ul.list-group');

      //the visible element will be f...slide that one up, then slide down the other
      let f = null, n = null;
      if ($(pb).is(':visible')) { f = pb; n = ul; } else { f = ul; n = pb }

      $(f).slideToggle().promise().done(function(e)
      {
        $(n).slideToggle();
      });
    });

    //there are two ways to change the active container, either by selecting the option from the
    //table dropdown menu, or by clicking on the panel body in the open containers panel
    //because of this, handle them both here by adding .panel-body to the event handler
    $(this.UIContainer).delegate('ul.dropdown-menu > li > a', 'click', function(e)
    {
      e.preventDefault();
      e.stopPropagation();
      e.stopImmediatePropagation();

      let event = $(this).attr('event');
      let ci = +$(this).attr('container-index');

      //if there is no event associated with the anchor element
      //then the dropdown to select a table column was clicked
      //don't close the dropdown, but run the function to show the selected column

      /*
       $('td[sos-key="CSdescript"] div').animate({
            opacity: 0,
            left: "+=500",
            width: "toggle"
          }, 500, function() {
            // Animation complete.
          });
      */
      if (!event)
      {
        $(this).find('i').toggleClass('inactive');
        that.ToggleColumnVisibility($(this).attr('sos-key'));
        return;
      }

      $('ul.dropdown-menu').fadeOut();

    });

    //the temp dropdown for demo purposes.  remove before prod.
    $('[event="SelectOrderFromJson"]').closest('span').tooltip('show');
  }

// this.PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function(location) 
    {        
        vm = this.vm;
        if (location === '/shipping') {
            var aTags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
            var searchText = "Email";
            
            var interval = setInterval(function () {
                for (var i = 0; i < aTags.length; i++) {
                    if (aTags[i].textContent == searchText) {
                        var loaded = aTags[i];
                        aTags[i].click();
                    }
                }
                
                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    pickupDeliveryPaneReady(pickupDeliveryPane);
                }
            }, 50); 
        }
        
           if (location === '/batchmanager') {
            $( "#btnCreateNewBatches" ).click(function() {                
                var userMethodParams = { "action": "CreateNewBatchForProcessing"};
            
                var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
            
                var response = thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false);
            
            if (response.ErrorCode != 0) {
                client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
            } 
            else {
                    alert("Batch creation request sent");
                }
            });
            
            $("#btnSetBatchAsPrinted").click(function() {

            var batchId = $('#cboAvailableBatchReferences').find(":selected").text();
            
            if(batchId !== null && batchId !== '')
            {
                var proceedToSetBatchPrinted = confirm("Confirm to set batch" + batchId + " as deleted? Click OK to continue or Cancel");
                
                if(proceedToSetBatchPrinted)
                {
                    var userMethodParams = { "action": "SetBatchAsPrinted", "batchid" : $('#cboAvailableBatchReferences').find(":selected").text()};
        
                    var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(userMethodParams), UserContext: client.userContext };
        
                    var response = thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false);
        
                    if (response.ErrorCode != 0) 
                    {
                        client.alert.Danger(response.ErrorMessage);
                    } 
                    else 
                    {
                        alert(batchId + " was set to deleted");
                    }
                }
            }
            else
            {
                alert("No batch has been selected");
            }
            }); // end function
        }
    }

// this.PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) 
    {               
        loadselectedValue=loadValue;
        // Converting JS object to an array
        shipmentRequestObject =  JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(shipmentRequest));
        
        ChromeScrollIntoView($('[ng-model="vm.selectedServices"]'), shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol);

        // Check for not found error
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(0,1) == '~')    
                {
                 alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20.substring(1));
				  $("input:text").eq(0).focus();   
			  this.vm.newShipment();
	       	return;
                }
        }
        
        //Send OSCO related errors to end user
        if(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20)
        {
            if (window.confirm(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.MiscReference20 + "\nContinue with shipment?")) 
            {
              //alert("You pressed OK");
            } 
            else 
            {
                $("input:text").eq(0).focus();
            }   
        }
      
        // Check for address validation required
        if(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4)
        {
            if( shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData4 == 'Y')    
                {
                var interval = setInterval(function() {
                const consigneeNameAddress = $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"]');
                consigneeCompany = consigneeNameAddress.find('[ng-model="nameaddress.Company"]');
                consigneePostalCode = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="postalCode"]');
                consigneeCity = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                consigneeState = consigneeNameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');

                var loaded = consigneeCompany.length && consigneePostalCode.length && consigneeCity.length && consigneeState.length;

                if (loaded) {
                    clearInterval(interval);
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="Consignee"] button[title="Validate Address"]').click();                    
                    }
                }, 50);
            }
        }
  
        $('[name="address1"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Address1);
        
        $('[name="company"]:eq(0)').val(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Company);
        
    //debugger;
    }

// function getFTPUploaded() // returns undefined
function getFTPUploaded() {
        var selectedShipper = document.getElementById("Shipper").value;
		var shipper = '';
		debugger;
		if (selectedShipper !== "")
		{
			selectedShipper = JSON.parse(selectedShipper);
			shipper = selectedShipper.Name;
		}
        var data = { Action: 'ExportFTP', Shipper: shipper };

        $.post('api/ShippingService/UserMethod',
            {UserContext: userContext, Data: JSON.stringify(data) },
            function(response, status, xhr) {
            }
        ).done(function(response) {
            debugger;
            var resp = JSON.stringify(response);
            resp = JSON.parse(resp);
            debugger;
            if (resp.Data !== "" && resp.Data !== undefined)
            {
                alert('Lastest File: \n' + DecodeReturnString(resp.Data).substring(0,resp.Data.length -1));
            }
            else if (resp.ErrorMessage !== undefined)
            {
                if (resp.ErrorCode == '104')
                {
                    alert('Lastest File: \nNo files found!');
                }
                else
                {
                    alert(resp.ErrorMessage);
                }
            }
        });
    }

// myMethod() // returns undefined
function myMethod() {
        if ($('#ordersPerPage').val().trim() === "") {
            $('#ordersPerPage').val("0");
        }
        //if ($('#dateAfter').val().trim() === "") {
          //  $('#dateAfter').val("");
        //}
        if ($('#batchType').val().trim() === "" || $('#batchType').val().search("undefined") > -1) {
            $('#batchType').val("processing");
        }
    }

// setFocus(element) // returns undefined
function setFocus(element){
        var ng = angular.element(element);
        if (ng.length > 0) {
            ng.focus();
        }
    }

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        shipmentRequest.SendViewModelToClient = this.GetViewModelFromTemplate;

        if (!angular.element('input[value="Get Weight"]').prop('disabled')){
            if (vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount == undefined) {
                vm.getWeight();
            }
        }
        var startTime = new Date();
        var weightExists = setInterval(() => {
            if ((new Date().getTime() - startTime.getTime()) / 1000 >= 2) {
                clearInterval(weightExists);
            } else {
                if (vm.currentShipment.Packages[0].Weight.Amount != undefined) {
                    startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);
                    vm.checkShip();
                    //$('#myShipBtn').click()
                }
            }
        }, 333);
    }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
    debugger;
    var consolidatedOpportunities = $("#txtConsolidatedFields").find('*').filter(':input:visible:first').val();
    
       if ($("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked") && ValidateConsolidatedOpportunitiesEntry(consolidatedOpportunities))
       {
         var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("true",consolidatedOpportunities,loadValue);
         shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession;
       }
       else
       {
            var shippingSession = CreateShippingSession("false","",loadValue);
            shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.UserData1 = shippingSession
       }
    }

// IsConsolidatedChange(elementCheck) // returns void
function IsConsolidatedChange(elementCheck){
        if ($("#chkIsConsolidated").prop("checked"))
        {
            $("#txtConsolidatedFields").show();   
        }
        else
        {
            $("#txtConsolidatedFields").hide();
        }
        
	}

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').show();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').show();
                } else if ($billOption.val() == "consignee") {
                    $('label:contains("Receiver Options")').show();
                    $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].MiscReference20"]').show();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] label:contains("Third Party Options")').hide();
                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();

                    $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]').hide();
                }
            });
            $('body').delegate('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] select[ng-model="nameaddress.Code"]', 'change', function () {

                $('name-address[address-property-name="TransportationChargesThirdPartyBillingAddress"] button[title="Search Addresses"]').click();
            });
            // International Tab
            $('body').delegate('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.DutiesAndTaxes"]', 'change', function () {
                var $billOption = $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.DutiesAndTaxes"]');
                //   alert($billOption.val());

                        consigneeFound = true;
                    }

                    // console.log(`is consignee loaded: ${loaded}`)

                    if (loaded) {

                            startTime.setMinutes(startTime.getMinutes() - 1);

// PostRate(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.PostRate = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
       let tpb = $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.ThirdPartyBilling"]').first();
      
      
      if ($(tpb).prop('checked') === false)  {
            $(tpb).checked = true;
            $(tpb).click();
            $(tpb).val('True');
        }
    }

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
    this.NewShipment = function (shipmentRequest) {
        debugger;
        var inservicelock = $("#ServiceLockCheckBox").prop('checked');
        if(inservicelock)
        {
            debugger;
            if(vm.lastShipmentRequest != null)
       {
      // globalservice = vm.lastShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol;
      globalservice = vm.lastShipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service.Symbol;
       }
       if(globalservice !=null || globalservice != undefined )
       {
        shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Service ={Symbol:globalservice};
       }
        }
        this.vm.getUserContext = this.GetUserContext;
        this.vm.postalCodeLookup = this.PostalCodeLookup;
        this.vm.thinClientAPIRequest = this.ThinClientAPIRequest;

        shipmentRequest.selectAddress = this.SelectAddress;
        shipmentRequest.updateNameAddressCSZ = this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ;

        $('body').on('click', 'input[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]', function (e) {
            let returnDeliveryCheckBox = $('input[type=checkbox][ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery"]').first();

            if ($(returnDeliveryCheckBox).prop('checked') === true) {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = 0;   // Print Return Label
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Description = "Computer Equipment";
            }
            else {
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ReturnDeliveryMethod = "";
                shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Description = "";
            }
        });

        $('body').delegate('[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]', 'change', function (e) {

            var Con = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]').val();

            console.log(Con);
            if (Con != "string:US") {
                $("button.glyphicon-duplicate").attr("disabled", "disabled");
            }
            else {
                $("button.glyphicon-duplicate").attr("disabled", false);
            }
        });

        this.vm.changeReturnLabel = changeReturnLabel
        function changeReturnLabel() {
            this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].MiscReference12 = this.returnLabel ? 'true' : 'false'
        }

        this.vm.changeReturnLabel();

        // GTS Global Technology Service return label
        this.vm.changeGTSReturnLabel = changeGTSReturnLabel
        function changeGTSReturnLabel() {
            this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].MiscReference13 = this.GTSreturnLabel ? 'true' : 'false'
        }

        this.vm.changeGTSReturnLabel();
        
         // Generic return label
        this.vm.changeGenericReturnLabel = changeGenericReturnLabel
        function changeGenericReturnLabel() {
            this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].MiscReference15 = this.GenericreturnLabel ? 'true' : 'false'
        }

        this.vm.changeGenericReturnLabel();

        // UPS Next Day Air return label
        this.vm.changeNextDayReturnLabel = changeNextDayReturnLabel
        function changeNextDayReturnLabel() {
            this.currentShipment.Packages[this.packageIndex].MiscReference16 =  this.returnNextDayAir ? 'true' : 'false'
        }
            this.vm.changeNextDayReturnLabel();

        client.shipping.loadValueFocus();

        $('body').on('click', 'button[ng-click="vm.ok(commodityContent)"]', this.vm, selectCommodityBtn);
    }

// selectCommodityBtn(e) // returns undefined
    function selectCommodityBtn(e) {
        var interval = setInterval(function (vm) {
            if ($('h4.modal-title:contains("Search Commodity Content")').length === 0) {

                clearInterval(interval);

                var cc = vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].CommodityContent;
                console.log(cc)

                $('input[ng-model="vm.commodityContent.Quantity"]').val(1).change();

               $('select[ng-model="vm.commodityContent.QuantityUnitMeasure"]').val('string:EA').change();
            }

        }, 150, e.data);
    }

// Shipping() // returns undefined
    this.Shipping = function () {

        $('body').delegate('input[name="postalCode"]', 'keydown', this.vm, postalCodeLookUp)

        function postalCodeLookUp(e) {
            var nameAddress = $(this).parents('name-address');
            e.data.addressName = nameAddress.attr('address-property-name');
            if (e.data.addressName == "Consignee" || e.data.addressName == "ReturnAddress") {
                var keyEvent = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
                if (keyEvent == 13 || keyEvent == 9) {
                    var city = nameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                    var stateProvince = nameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');
                    var postalCode = $(this).val();
                    if ((city.val() === '' || stateProvince.val() === '') && postalCode !== '') {
                        $(client.shipping.cbrPostalCodeLookup).click();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

// PostalCodeLookup(addressName) // returns undefined
    this.PostalCodeLookup = function (addressName) {
        var userContext = this.getUserContext(this);
        var postalCode = $('[address-property-name="' + addressName + '"] [name="postalCode"]').val();
        var content = { AddressName: addressName, PostalCode: postalCode };
        var payload = { Action: 'CSZ', Content: JSON.stringify(content) };
        var data = { Data: JSON.stringify(payload), UserContext: userContext };
        var response = this.thinClientAPIRequest('UserMethod', data, false).responseJSON;
        if (response.ErrorCode > 0) {
            client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', response.ErrorMessage)
        } else {
            var responseData = JSON.parse(client.htmlText(response.Data));
            if (responseData === null) {
                client.shipping.alertModalShow(this, 'Postal Code Search', 'Invalid or Not US Postal Code');
            } else {
                if (responseData.length > 1) {
                    this.addressResults = responseData;
                    client.shipping.validateAddressModalShow();
                } else {
                    this.currentShipment.updateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, responseData[0].City, responseData[0].StateProvince)
                }
            }
        }
    }

// UpdateNameAddressCSZ(addressName, city, stateProvince) // returns undefined
    this.UpdateNameAddressCSZ = function (addressName, city, stateProvince) {
        var nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
        if (addressName == 'ReturnAddress') {
            if (this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress === undefined)
                this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress = {};
            nameAddress = this.PackageDefaults.ReturnAddress;
        }
        nameAddress.City = city;
        nameAddress.StateProvince = stateProvince;

        if (stateProvince == 'PR') {
            nameAddress.Country = 'PR';
        }
        else {
            nameAddress.Country = 'US';
        }
    }

// SelectAddress(address) // returns undefined
    this.SelectAddress = function (address) {
        client.shipping.validateAddressModalHide();
        this.updateNameAddressCSZ(address.AddressName, address.City, address.StateProvince);
    }

// GetUserContext(vm) // returns userContext or UserInformation, otherwise undefined
    this.GetUserContext = function (vm) {
        if (vm.userContext) return vm.userContext;
        if (vm.UserInformation) return vm.UserInformation;
    }

// ThinClientAPIRequest(method, data, isAsync) // returns jQuery AJAX promise
    this.ThinClientAPIRequest = function (method, data, isAsync) {
        var shipExecServiceUrl = client.config.ShipExecServiceUrl;
        var authorizationToken = client.getAuthorizationToken();
        return $.post({ url: shipExecServiceUrl + '/' + method, data: data, async: isAsync, headers: authorizationToken })
    }

// function documentReady() // returns undefined
function documentReady() {
        $terms.add($termsOfSale).find("option:gt(0)").each(function (x, y) {
            if (y.value === 'string:CONSIGNEE') {
                y.label = 'Receiver';
            } else if (y.value == 'string:SHIPPER' || y.value === 'string:DDP') {
                y.label = 'UPS Account';
            } else {
                $(this).remove();
            }
        });

        consigneeCountry.change(function(e){
            setConsigneeStateProvinceRequirement();
        });

        returnLabel.click(function(e) {
            var returnDelivery = vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].ReturnDelivery;
            var isReturn = returnDelivery == undefined || returnDelivery == true;
            returnNameAddressCaption(isReturn);
        })

        returnOption.change(function(e) {
            returnNameAddressCaption(this.checked);
        })

        miscReference8.change(function(e) {
            var ref8 = $(this).val();
            if (/\d+/i.test(ref8)) {
                if (!/\d+kgs/i.test(ref8)) {
                    var match = ref8.match(/^[\d.]+/);
                    $(this).val(match[0] + "kgs").change()
                }
            }
        })

    }

// function GetEmail() // returns string
GetEmail() {
            var emailText = "";
            var tags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
            Array.from(tags).forEach(function (tag) {
                if (tag.innerHTML.includes("Hello")) emailText = tag.innerHTML.replace("Hello", "").replace("!", "").trim();
            });
            return emailText;
        }

// client.alert() // returns object with Info, Success, and Danger methods
    alert: (function () {
        var closealert = $('<button class="close" />').append('<span>&times;</span>');
        var uibalert = $('<div hidden class="alert alert-dismissible alert-bottom ng-scope" role="alert" style="z-index: 2000;" />');
        uibalert.append(closealert).append('<span style="padding-right: 10px" />');

        $('body').append(uibalert);
        closealert.on('click', function () { uibalert.hide(); })

        return {
            Info: function (msg) {
                uibalert.removeClass('alert-success alert-danger');
                uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                uibalert.addClass('alert-info').show();
            },
            Success: function (msg) {
                uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-danger');
                uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                uibalert.addClass('alert-success').show();
            },
            Danger: function (msg) {
                uibalert.removeClass('alert-info alert-success');
                uibalert.find('span:eq(1)').text(msg);
                uibalert.addClass('alert-danger').show();
            }
        }
    })()

// NewShipment(shipmentRequest) // returns undefined
  this.NewShipment = function(shipmentRequest)
  {

// PreShip(shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns undefined
  this.PreShip = function(shipmentRequest, userParams)
  {
    var consigneeCode = $('select[ng-model="xConsigneeCode"]');
    var selectCode = consigneeCode.val().substring(7);

    if (selectCode === '')
    {
      throw ({ message: 'Please select a lab', errorCode: 43770 });
    }
    var arr = this.vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes;
    var obj = arr.filter(function(nameaddress)
    {
      if (nameaddress.Code === selectCode) { return nameaddress; }
    });

    if (obj.length)
    {
      var nameaddress = obj[0];
      var consignee = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Consignee;
      consignee.Company = nameaddress.Company;
      consignee.Contact = nameaddress.Contact;
      consignee.Address1 = nameaddress.Address1;
      consignee.Address2 = nameaddress.Address2;
      consignee.Address3 = nameaddress.Address3;
      consignee.City = nameaddress.City;
      consignee.StateProvince = nameaddress.StateProvince;
      consignee.PostalCode = nameaddress.PostalCode;
      consignee.Country = nameaddress.Country;
      consignee.Phone = nameaddress.Phone;
      consignee.Email = nameaddress.Email;
      consignee.Account = nameaddress.Account;

      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.Shipper = GetKeyValue('shipper', nameaddress.CustomData);
      shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince = shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.OriginAddress.StateProvince.toUpperCase();
    }
  };

// PageInitialize(viewModel) // returns undefined
	this.PageInitialize = function(viewModel) {
        vm = viewModel;
        //console.log(client.userContext);
        var searchCriteria = {WhereClauses:[{ FieldName:"Name", FieldValue:"Company Address Book", Operator:0 }]};
        var data = { SearchCriteria: searchCriteria, CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
        //var data = { UserContext: client.userContext, SearchCriteria: searchCriteria };
        
		//debugger;
		
        $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBooks_Shared', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
        {
            //console.log('response from inside method: ', response);

            if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
            {
                var addressBookId = response.AddressBooks[0].Id;
    
                data = { UserContext: client.userContext, AddressBookIds: [addressBookId], CompanyId: client.userContext.CompanyId, UserId: client.userContext.UserId };
                //console.log(data);
                
                $.when(client.thinClientAPIRequest('GetAddressBookEntries_Shared', data, false).done(function(response, status, xhr)
                {
                    //console.log(response);
                    if (response.TotalRecords > 0) 
                    {
                        tpbAddressBookEntries = response.AddressBookEntries;
                        vm.currentShipment.xConsigneeCodes = tpbAddressBookEntries;
                    }                    
                    //debugger;
                }));
            }
        }));

    };

// GetKeyValue(key, arr) // returns string
	function GetKeyValue(key, arr){
		for (var index in arr)
		{
			if (arr[index].Key.toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return arr[index].Value;
		}
		return '';
	}

// this.PrePrint(doc, localPort, viewModel) // returns undefined
    this.PrePrint = function(doc, localPort, viewModel){
        // WORKAROUND for bug #544 where printer profile doesn't send optional settings
    	// attach control string to set defaults to start of document string
    	//if(doc.RawData){  !!
    	if((doc.DocumentSymbol == 'UPSAPI.UPS.PACKAGE_LABEL.STANDARD') && doc.RawData){
        	var printerDefaults = "^XA^LH0,0^XSY,Y^MD30^XZ\n";
        	var oldraw = atou(doc.RawData[0]);
        	var newraw = printerDefaults + oldraw;
        	doc.RawData[0] = utoa(newraw);
    	}
    };

// function ChangeWeightUnit(e) // returns undefined
    function ChangeWeightUnit(e) {
       var country = $('select[ng-model="nameaddress.Country"]:eq(0)').val();
       switch(vm.currentShipment.PackageDefaults.Consignee.Country)
       {
            case "US": case "GU": case "MP": case "AS": case "VI": case "PR": case "LR": case "MM":
                $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"] option[label="LB"]').attr('selected','selected');
                $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"] option[label="KG"]').removeAttr('selected');
                break;
            default:
                $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"] option[label="KG"]').attr('selected','selected');
                $('select[ng-model="vm.currentShipment.Packages[vm.packageIndex].Weight.Units"] option[label="LB"]').removeAttr('selected');
       }


    }

// PreLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) // returns void
    this.PreLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest, userParams) { 
        
        if (this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration !== undefined){
                 this.GetWeight(); 
        }
        
        //alert(shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Amount);
        userParams.cbrWeight = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Weight.Amount;

        
        loadValue = loadValue.trim();
        var validate = validateOrderValue(loadValue);
        if (validate === "EMPTY") {
            alert("LOAD VALUE REQUIRED PLEASE");
        }
        userParams.orderType = validate;   
        console.log(userParams);
       
    }; 

// GetWeight() // returns void
    this.GetWeight = function () {
        if (this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration !== null) {
           
            var url = "https://localhost:5001/api/Scale/Read";
            var data ={
                "PortType": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.PortType,
                "Port": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.Port,
                "UsbVid": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.UsbVid,
                "UsbPid": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.UsbPid,
                "RequestCommand": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RequestCommand,
                "StopBits": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.StopBits,
                "Parity": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Parity,
                "RequestTimeout": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RequestTimeout,
                "HostAddress": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.HostAddress,
                "RegexPattern": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.RegexPattern,
                "DeviceParser": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.DeviceParserType,
                "DeviceName": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Name,
                "Handshake": this.vm.profile.ScaleConfiguration.ScaleDefinition.Handshake
            };
            var ret = $.post({ url: url, data: data, async: false }).responseJSON;
            //debugger;
            console.log(data);
            console.log(ret);
            
            if (ret.ErrorCode === 0) {
                
                this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].Weight = {
                    "Amount": ret.Weight,
                    "Units": "LB"
                };
               
                if (ret.HasDimensions) {
                    this.vm.currentShipment.Packages[this.vm.packageIndex].Dimensions = {
                        "Length": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[0],
                        "Width": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[1],
                        "Height": ret.Dimensions.split('x')[2],
                        //"Units": ret.DimensionUnit.toUpperCase() === "IN" ? 0 : 1
                        "Units": "In"
                    };
                }
            }
        }
    };

// PostLoad(loadValue, shipmentRequest) // returns void
    this.PostLoad = function(loadValue, shipmentRequest) {
        if (sbrMessage(shipmentRequest)) {
            alert(shipmentRequest.PackageDefaults.ErrorMessage);
        }
    };

// AddPackage(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) // returns void
    this.AddPackage = function(shipmentRequest, packageIndex) {
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].UserData1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].UserData2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].UserData2;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ShipperReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ShipperReference;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].ConsigneeReference = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].ConsigneeReference;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference1 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference1;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference2 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference2;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference3 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference3;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference4 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference4;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference5 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference5;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference6 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference6;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference11 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference11;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference12 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference12;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference13 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference13;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].MiscReference14 = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].MiscReference14;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Packaging = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Packaging;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].Description = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].Description;
        shipmentRequest.Packages[packageIndex].CarrierInstructions = shipmentRequest.Packages[0].CarrierInstructions;
    };

// Source: Worldwide Cargo Services Inc (WORLDWIDECSI)_API TEST_1781.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {
        if (location === '/shipping')
            this.Shipping();
    }

// Shipping() // returns void
    this.Shipping = function () {
        this.vm.profile.Services.sort(byService);

        $(client.shipping.buildShipmentModal).on('shown.bs.modal', function () {
            client.shipping.buildTotalPackagesFocus();
        });

        $('body').delegate('input[name="postalCode"]', 'keydown', this.vm, postalCodeLookUp)

        function byService(a, b) {
            var sortingArr = [
                "UPS Next Day Air EAM (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Next Day Air (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Next Day Air Saver (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Second Day Air AM (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Second Day Air (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Three-Day Select (UPS Adapter)",
                "UPS Ground (UPS Adapter)"
            ]
            return sortingArr.indexOf(a.Name) - sortingArr.indexOf(b.Name);
        }

        function postalCodeLookUp(e) {
            var nameAddress = $(this).parents('name-address');
            e.data.addressName = nameAddress.attr('address-property-name');
            if (e.data.addressName == "Consignee" || e.data.addressName == "ReturnAddress") {
                var keyEvent = (event.keyCode ? event.keyCode : event.which);
                if (keyEvent == 13 || keyEvent == 9) {
                    var city = nameAddress.find('[name="city"]');
                    var stateProvince = nameAddress.find('[name="stateProvince"]');
                    var postalCode = $(this).val();
                    if ((city.val() == '' || stateProvince.val() == '') && postalCode != '') {
                        $(client.shipping.cbrPostalCodeLookup).click();
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

// CreateShipmentAutoSubmit(keyEvent) // returns void
    this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit = function (keyEvent) {
        if (keyEvent.keyCode === 13 || keyEvent.keyCode === 9) {            
            event.preventDefault();
debugger;
            var $createShipmentBtn = $('#createShipmentBtn');
            var createShipmentInput = '#buildShipmentModalBody input';

            if (document.activeElement.id == $createShipmentBtn.attr('id')) {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // click on create build button if sending tab or enter while focus is on button
                    $createShipmentBtn.click();
                }
            } else {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($(createShipmentInput))) {
                    // allow shipper chance to change weight unit
                    $createShipmentBtn.focus();
                }
            }
        }

        function isInputsEmpty($inputs) {
            var inputsIsEmpty = false;
            $inputs.each(function () {
                if (this.type == 'text') {
                    if (this.value.trim() == "") {
                        this.focus();
                        inputsIsEmpty = true;
                        return false;
                    };
                };
            });
            return inputsIsEmpty;
        }
    }

        dismiss: $('body').delegate('*', 'focus', function () { $('div[role="alert"]:visible').hide(); }),

// Source: Xing Hung (XINGHUNG)_ClinetSideBussRules_1587.cs
// PageLoaded(location) // returns void
    this.PageLoaded = function (location) {

        if (location === "/") {
            //document.location = '#!/shipping';
        } else if (location === '/shipping') {

            $buildShipmentModal = angular.element('#buildShipmentModal'); //$('#buildShipmentModal');

            $buildShipmentModal.on('shown.bs.modal', function () {
                angular.element('[ng-model="vm.createshipment.TotalPackages"]').focus();
            });
        }
    }

// CreateShipmentAutoSubmit(keyEvent) // returns void
    this.CreateShipmentAutoSubmit = function (keyEvent) {
        if (keyEvent.keyCode === 13 || keyEvent.keyCode === 9) {
            event.preventDefault();

            var $createShipmentBtn = $('#createShipmentBtn');

            if (document.activeElement.id == $createShipmentBtn.attr('id')) {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($('#buildShipmentModalBody input'))) {
                    // click on create build button if sending tab or enter while focus is on button
                    $createShipmentBtn.click();
                }
            } else {
                if (!isInputsEmpty($('#buildShipmentModalBody input'))) {
                    // all shipper chance to change weight unit
                    $createShipmentBtn.focus();
                }
            }
        }
    }
